I THEREFORE LET GO THE CORD AND LEAVING THE HOOKS FIXED TO THE SHIPS I RESOLUTELY CUT WITH MY KNIFE THE CABLES THAT FASTENED THE ANCHORS RECEIVING ABOVE TWO HUNDRED SHOTS IN MY FACE AND HANDS
I REMAINED UPON THE TREE TILL IT WAS DAY AND THEN CAME DOWN MORE LIKE A DEAD MAN THAN ONE ALIVE EXPECTING THE SAME FATE WITH MY TWO COMPANIONS
AND CONSIDERED LORD
AND IF YOU WOULD TAKE MY ADVICE YOU WOULD PART ALSO WITH THE RING AND NOT HAVE ANYTHING TO DO WITH GENIES WHO AS OUR PROPHET HAS TOLD US ARE ONLY DEVILS WITH YOUR LEAVE MOTHER REPLIED ALADDIN I SHALL NOW TAKE CARE HOW I SELL A LAMP WHICH MAY BE SO SERVICEABLE BOTH TO YOU AND ME
NOW WHISPERED THE MAN AT BERTRAM'S LEFT SHAKE OFF THAT FELLOW AND FOLLOW ME BERTRAM WITH A VIOLENT AND SUDDEN EFFORT BURST AWAY FROM THE MAN ON HIS RIGHT AND CLOSELY FOLLOWING HIS MYSTERIOUS FRIEND ATTENDED BY THE FAITHFUL DINMONT WHO NEVER LEFT HIM RAN QUICKLY DOWN A NARROW LANE WHICH LED FROM THE MAIN STREET
THAT THE SAID MAN-MOUNTAIN SHALL IN TWO MOONS TIME DELIVER IN AN EXACT SURVEY OF THE CIRCUMFERENCE OF OUR DOMINIONS BY A COMPUTATION OF HIS OWN PACES ROUND THE COAST
I REMEMBERED THE SAYING OF THE GREAT SOLOMON WHICH I HAD FREQUENTLY HEARD FROM MY FATHER A GOOD NAME IS BETTER THAN PRECIOUS OINTMENT
WE HOPE WHEN YOU LOOK UPON IT YOU WILL PERCEIVE OUR GOOD INTENTION AND BE PLEASED WITH IT
WE HAD A BOAT AT OUR STERN JUST BEFORE THE STORM BUT SHE WAS FAST STAVED BY DASHING AGAINST THE SHIP'S RUDDER AND IN THE NEXT PLACE SHE BROKE AWAY AND EITHER SUNK OR WAS DRIVEN OFF TO SEA
I THEN TOOK MY TURN AND EMBRACED HIM AS MY DELIVERER AND WE REJOICED TOGETHER
THIS CHEERED ME UP A LITTLE TOO AND I BEGAN TO PERSUADE MYSELF IT WAS ALL A DELUSION
FOR THOU ART NOW OUT OF THE WAY
I BELIEVE HE HAD BURIED THEM BOTH IN A QUARTER OF AN HOUR
AND AFTER THIS MADE ALL THE SIGNS TO ME OF SUBJECTION SERVITUDE AND SUBMISSION IMAGINABLE TO LET ME KNOW HOW HE WOULD SERVE ME SO LONG AS HE LIVED
I WAS AT FIRST READY TO SINK DOWN WITH THE SURPRISE
SIX OF THE CREW OF WHOM I WAS ONE HAVING LET DOWN THE BOAT INTO THE SEA MADE A SHIFT TO GET CLEAR OF THE SHIP AND THE ROCK
IN THIS APARTMENT WHICH WAS NEAR THE TOP OF THE PRISON HIS FEET WERE CHAINED TO AN IRON BAR FIRMLY FIXED AT THE HEIGHT OF ABOUT SIX INCHES FROM THE FLOOR
AND HE CAME NEARER AND NEARER KNEELING DOWN EVERY TEN OR TWELVE STEPS IN TOKEN OF ACKNOWLEDGMENT FOR SAVING HIS LIFE
HOWEVER MY SPEECH PRODUCED NOTHING ELSE BESIDE A LOUD LAUGHTER WHICH ALL THE RESPECT DUE TO HIS MAJESTY FROM THOSE ABOUT HIM COULD NOT MAKE THEM CONTAIN
I MADE MY OBEISANCE AND PRESENTED THE LETTER AND GIFT
FOR THERE WAS LITTLE OR NOTHING MORE FOR US TO DO IN THIS
AND THAT IT WAS MY PART TO SUBMIT TO BEAR HIS INDIGNATION BECAUSE I HAD SINNED AGAINST HIM
HOWEVER THE CAPTAIN SEEMED TO MAKE SOME DIFFICULTY OF IT AS IF HE DURST NOT LEAVE THEM THERE
THE GUNS WILL FLASH AND THE SWORDS WILL GLITTER IN THE MOONLIGHT SHE THEN ASKED HIM IF HE BORE ANY MALICE TO THE MAN THAT WOUNDED HIM AND ON HAZLEWOOD ASSURING HER THAT HE HAD ALWAYS THOUGHT IT WAS AN ACCIDENT SHE SAID
WHETHER AN ISLAND OR THE MAIN WHETHER INHABITED OR NOT INHABITED
TO WHOM IT WAS ANSWERED THEY ARE STANDING WITHOUT THE GATE
AND DIRECTLY HE SAW HER HE LOVED HER AND LEFT HIS OWN LADY UNDER THE SPELL OF THE PURPLE FLOWER
FOR THEY TOOK PROSPERO TO SEA AND WHEN THEY WERE FAR AWAY FROM LAND FORCED HIM INTO A LITTLE BOAT WITH NO TACKLE MAST OR SAIL
LOOK WELL AT HIM AND YOU WILL FIND HIM TO BE BOTH THE FICTITIOUS OIL MERCHANT AND THE CAPTAIN OF THE GANG OF FORTY ROBBERS
GO AND BRING HIM IF YOU MEET WITH HIM ALADDIN WAS JUST READY TO GO WHEN THE MAGICIAN KNOCKED AT THE DOOR AND CAME IN LOADED WITH WINE AND ALL SORTS OF FRUITS WHICH HE BROUGHT FOR A DESSERT
FOR WHAT DID YOU BRING YOURSELF INTO THIS CONDITION
TREES ALSO GROW HERE MOST OF WHICH ARE OF WOOD OF ALOES EQUAL IN GOODNESS TO THOSE OF COMARI
VERY OFTEN THE CHIEF MINISTERS THEMSELVES ARE COMMANDED TO SHOW THEIR SKILL AND TO CONVINCE THE EMPEROR THAT THEY HAVE NOT LOST THEIR FACULTY
HERE SHE SAID HERE BE STILL AND YOU ARE SAFE
NESBIT THERE WAS ONCE A WICKED DUKE NAMED FREDERICK WHO TOOK THE DUKEDOM THAT SHOULD HAVE BELONGED TO HIS BROTHER SENDING HIM INTO EXILE
IF IT WAS A LITTLE CLEANER I BELIEVE IT WOULD BRING SOMETHING MORE SHE TOOK SOME FINE SAND AND WATER TO CLEAN IT
AND AGAINST HIM THE STRANGER WAS EQUALLY SUCCESSFUL
THE NEXT MORNING AT DAYBREAK THE GENIE PRESENTED HIMSELF AND HAVING OBTAINED ALADDIN'S CONSENT TRANSPORTED HIM IN A MOMENT TO THE PALACE HE HAD MADE
AND WHEN I WAS ASHORE IN OBSERVING THE MANNERS AND DISPOSITIONS OF THE PEOPLE AS WELL AS LEARNING THEIR LANGUAGE WHEREIN I HAD A GREAT FACILITY BY THE STRENGTH OF MY MEMORY
I WENT TO SEE AND COMFORT HIM IN HIS AFFLICTION AND FINDING HIM ABSORBED IN SORROW I SAID TO HIM AS SOON AS I SAW HIM GOD PRESERVE YOU AND GRANT YOU A LONG LIFE ALAS REPLIED HE HOW DO YOU THINK I SHOULD OBTAIN THE FAVOR YOU WISH ME
IN THIS GREAT EMERGENCY HE SAID THERE IS NO STRENGTH OR POWER BUT IN THE GREAT AND HIGH GOD
WHEN HERMIA WOKE SHE FOUND LYSANDER GONE AND WANDERED ABOUT THE WOOD TRYING TO FIND HIM
WHEN HE HAD PASSED IN AND OUT AS OFTEN AS HE WISHED HE STOOD BEFORE THE DOOR AND PRONOUNCING THE WORDS SHUT SESAME THE DOOR CLOSED OF ITSELF
AND IN THE SPACE OF AN HOUR OR BETTER THAT SIDE OF THE BOX WHERE THE STAPLES WERE AND HAD NO WINDOWS STRUCK AGAINST SOMETHING THAT WAS HARD
AMONGST THE PERSONS WHOM BERTRAM RECALLED THERE WAS HE SAID A TALL THIN KIND-TEMPERED MAN WHO USED TO TEACH ME MY LETTERS AND WALK WITH ME ON HEARING THIS THE POOR DOMINIE COULD CONTAIN HIS FEELINGS NO LONGER AND RISING HASTILY FROM HIS CHAIR WITH CLASPED HANDS TREMBLING LIMBS AND STREAMING EYES HE CALLED OUT ALOUD
I FELL ON MY KNEES AND LIFTED UP MY HANDS AND EYES AND SPOKE SEVERAL WORDS AS LOUD AS I COULD
AND ON THE OTHER SIDE WHAT SIGHS AND GROANS BURST FROM CHRISTIAN'S HEART
HIS SHIPS WERE ON NEARLY EVERY SEA AND HE TRADED WITH PORTUGAL WITH MEXICO WITH ENGLAND AND WITH INDIA
HE NEVER LEFT HIS SEAT ALL DAY
AND AFTER ENJOINING ME SECRECY THEY TOLD ME THAT THEY HAD A MIND TO FIT OUT A SHIP TO GO TO GUINEA
HE THOUGHT IT HIS DUTY NOW TO PUNISH AND EXTERMINATE ALL AMONGST THEM WHO WERE POACHERS AND TRESPASSERS AND CAUSED EVEN THE POOR BEGGARS AT HIS DOOR TO BE SENT TO THE WORKHOUSE
AS WE WENT BY THE PLACE WHERE HE HAD BURIED THE TWO MEN HE POINTED EXACTLY TO THE PLACE AND SHOWED ME THE MARKS THAT HE HAD MADE TO FIND THEM AGAIN MAKING SIGNS TO ME THAT WE SHOULD DIG THEM UP AGAIN AND EAT THEM
HAVING THEREFORE CONSULTED WITH MY WIFE AND SOME OF MY ACQUAINTANCE I DETERMINED TO GO AGAIN TO SEA
SO THAT I HAD NOW A DOUBLE WALL
HE THEN TURNED HIS STEED UPON ATHELSTANE AND WRENCHING FROM THE HAND OF THE BULKY SAXON THE BATTLE-AXE WHICH HE WIELDED BESTOWED HIM SUCH A BLOW UPON THE CREST THAT THE LORD OF CONINGSBURGH ALSO LAY SENSELESS ON THE FIELD
INTO THAT ON THE LEFT SIDE THE KING'S SMITH CONVEYED FOURSCORE AND ELEVEN CHAINS LIKE THOSE THAT HANG TO A LADY'S WATCH IN EUROPE AND ALMOST AS LARGE WHICH WERE LOCKED TO MY LEFT LEG WITH SIX AND THIRTY PADLOCKS
HE LEFT THE APARTMENT SAYING THAT HE WOULD RESCUE HIS FRIENDS OR RETURN AND DIE ALONG WITH THEM
I THEN WITH THE BUTT-END OF MY FOWLING-PIECE RAMMED THE HEAD FARTHER INTO THE THROAT OF THE CROCODILE AND DESTROYED HIM BY SUFFOCATION FOR HE COULD NEITHER GORGE NOR EJECT IT
I HAD THE GOOD FORTUNE TO DIVERT THE EMPEROR ONE DAY AFTER A VERY EXTRAORDINARY MANNER
IN SHORT AFTER A LONG VOYAGE I ARRIVED AT BUSSORAH AND THENCE RETURNED TO BAGDAD WITH SO MUCH WEALTH THAT I KNEW NOT ITS EXTENT
BEING DELIVERED FROM THIS SECOND CAPTIVITY THE SAME DAY OF THE MONTH THAT I FIRST MADE MY ESCAPE IN THE LONG-BOAT FROM AMONG THE MOORS OF SALLEE
THAT MY STORY COULD CONTAIN LITTLE BESIDES COMMON EVENTS WITHOUT THOSE ORNAMENTED DESCRIPTIONS OF STRANGE PLANTS TREES BIRDS AND OTHER ANIMALS
FOR IT WAS WORTH CONSIDERING WHETHER WE MIGHT VENTURE TO TAKE THEM WITH US OR NO ESPECIALLY TWO OF THEM WHOM HE KNEW TO BE INCORRIGIBLE AND REFRACTORY TO THE LAST DEGREE
SO AFTER HE HAD RECEIVED AND GIVEN MANY WOUNDS TO THOSE THAT ATTEMPTED TO KEEP HIM OUT HE CUT HIS WAY THROUGH THEM ALL AND PRESSED FORWARD INTO THE PALACE AT WHICH THERE WAS A PLEASANT VOICE HEARD FROM THOSE THAT WERE WITHIN EVEN OF THOSE THAT WALKED UPON THE TOP OF THE PALACE SAYING COME IN COME IN
BUT SINCE THOU COMPLAINEST OF THY SERVICE AND WAGES BE CONTENT TO GO BACK

IF AN EXPRESS REQUIRES EXTRAORDINARY DISPATCH THE MAN MOUNTAIN SHALL BE OBLIGED TO CARRY IN HIS POCKET THE MESSENGER AND HORSE A SIX DAYS JOURNEY ONCE IN EVERY MOON AND RETURN THE SAID MESSENGER BACK IF SO REQUIRED SAFE TO OUR IMPERIAL PRESENCE

ITS TRUE AUTHOR IS THE BROTHER OF THE AFRICAN MAGICIAN YOUR ENEMY WHOM YOU HAVE DESTROYED
AND AS FOR THAT MONSTROUS ANIMAL WITH WHOM I WAS SO LATELY ENGAGED IT WAS INDEED AS LARGE AS AN ELEPHANT IF MY FEARS HAD SUFFERED ME TO THINK SO FAR AS TO MAKE USE OF MY HANGER LOOKING FIERCELY AND CLAPPING MY HAND UPON THE HILT AS I SPOKE WHEN HE POKED HIS PAW INTO MY CHAMBER PERHAPS I SHOULD HAVE GIVEN HIM SUCH A WOUND AS WOULD HAVE MADE HIM GLAD TO WITHDRAW IT WITH MORE HASTE THAN HE PUT IT IN

I STOOD STILL A FEW MOMENTS TO RECOVER BREATH AND TILL THE WATERS WENT FROM ME AND THEN TOOK TO MY HEELS AND RAN WITH WHAT STRENGTH I HAD FARTHER TOWARD THE SHORE
ANTONIO DESPISED AND DISLIKED THIS MAN VERY MUCH AND TREATED HIM WITH THE GREATEST HARSHNESS AND SCORN
IT WAS ONLY ONE SUBSTANTIAL DISH OF MEAT FIT FOR THE PLAIN CONDITION OF A HUSBANDMAN IN A DISH OF ABOUT FOUR-AND-TWENTY FEET IN DIAMETER
AFTER WHICH AS THEY WERE NOT ABLE TO MAKE RESISTANCE SO THEY COULD EXPECT NO MERCY
HAD THEY BEEN ALL OF THE WICKED PART OF THE CREW I SHOULD HAVE THOUGHT GOD'S PROVIDENCE HAD SINGLED THEM OUT TO DELIVER THEM INTO YOUR HANDS
FOR NEARLY THREE HOURS THE WRETCHED JEW REMAINED SITTING IN A CORNER OF HIS DUNGEON WHEN STEPS WERE HEARD ON THE STAIR BY WHICH IT WAS APPROACHED
IN THE ENJOYMENT OF WHICH I DID THEN PROMISE MYSELF MUCH DELIGHT
WHEN SHE CAME TO THE GATES THE GRAND VIZIER THE OTHER VIZIERS AND MOST DISTINGUISHED LORDS OF THE COURT WERE JUST GONE IN
ASK HIM SAID THE INTERPRETER
AND IT HAVING BEEN A DAY OF GREAT FATIGUE TO ME I SLEPT SOUND TILL I WAS SURPRISED WITH THE NOISE OF A GUN
AND HE SIGHED AS IF HE WOULD BREAK HIS HEART
ALI BABA KNOCKED AT THE DOOR WHICH WAS OPENED BY MORGIANA A CLEVER INTELLIGENT SLAVE WHO WAS FRUITFUL IN INVENTIONS TO MEET THE MOST DIFFICULT CIRCUMSTANCES
BUT IT WAS SO DARK AND THE FLOOD WAS SO HIGH THAT IN THEIR GOING BACK THEY HAD LIKE TO HAVE BEEN DROWNED NINE OR TEN TIMES
AND PIQUED TO THE QUICK AT ALADDIN'S HIGH ESTATE HE RETURNED TO THE KHAN
BUT UPON THE NEXT ABOUT THREE IN THE AFTERNOON WHEN I HAD BY MY COMPUTATION MADE TWENTY-FOUR LEAGUES FROM BLEFUSCU I DESCRIED A SAIL STEERING TO THE SOUTHEAST
THIS MADE HIM REPENT OF HIS WICKEDNESS AND HE BEGGED ORLANDO'S PARDON AND FROM THENCEFORTH THEY WERE DEAR BROTHERS
AND BEFORE I BEGAN MY SECOND VOYAGE I SOLD THEM FOR SIX HUNDRED POUNDS
ONE DAY THERE WAS A WRESTLING MATCH AT COURT AND ROSALIND AND CELIA WENT TO SEE IT
NOR CAN ALL THE MEN IN THE WORLD LET ME OUT
NEVERTHELESS SAID THE PILGRIM YOU WILL NOT I THINK REFUSE ME THAT FAVOUR SO SAYING HE WHISPERED SOMETHING IN HIS EAR IN SAXON
THE CAPTAIN WELL SATISFIED WITH HIS ATTEMPT AND INFORMED OF WHAT HE WANTED TO KNOW RETURNED TO THE FOREST
AND APOLLYON AS FAST MADE AT HIM THROWING DARTS AS THICK AS HAIL
BUT HE LEARNED ON ASKING ABOUT HIM THAT HE WAS A STRANGER IN THOSE PARTS WHO HAD COME FROM THE SOUTH-WEST OF SCOTLAND AND THAT HIS NAME WAS GABRIEL
AH
TO WHICH THE CAPTAIN AT MY INTERCESSION CAUSED THEIR CHESTS AND CLOTHES TO BE ADDED WHICH THEY TOOK AND WERE VERY THANKFUL FOR
I CANNOT TELL HOW LONG I SLEPT BUT WHEN I AWOKE THE SHIP WAS GONE
IT SEEMED AN ENDLESS CAVERN AND MIGHT BE ABOUT FIFTY FATHOMS DEEP
AND WITHAL LAUGHED PATIENCE TO SCORN
CHRISTIAN AND HOPEFUL ARRIVE AT THE CAELESTIAL CITY BY JOHN BUNYAN I SAW THAT AS THEY WENT ON THERE MET THEM TWO MEN IN RAIMENT THAT SHONE LIKE GOLD ALSO THEIR FACES SHONE AS THE LIGHT
THERE BEING A CONSIDERABLE QUANTITY OF IT HE SOON BEGAN TO SING AND TO MOVE ABOUT FROM SIDE TO SIDE IN HIS SEAT UPON MY SHOULDERS AND BY DEGREES TO LOOSEN HIS LEGS FROM ABOUT ME
WHAT IS MOST REMARKABLE IN THIS PLACE IS THAT THE STONES OF THE MOUNTAIN ARE OF CRYSTAL RUBIES OR OTHER PRECIOUS STONES
UPON THE CAPTAIN COMING TO ME I TOLD HIM MY PROJECT FOR SEIZING THE SHIP WHICH HE LIKED WONDERFULLY WELL AND RESOLVED TO PUT IT IN EXECUTION THE NEXT MORNING
HE PRACTICED THE ARTS OF MAGIC NO MORE BUT HIS LIFE WAS HAPPY AND NOT ONLY BECAUSE HE HAD FOUND HIS OWN AGAIN BUT CHIEFLY BECAUSE WHEN HIS BITTEREST FOES WHO HAD DONE HIM DEADLY WRONG LAY AT HIS MERCY HE TOOK NO VENGEANCE ON THEM BUT NOBLY FORGAVE THEM
O ETERNITY
SO I CAME BACK FOR THE PRESENT BEING MORE INTENT UPON GETTING AT THE SHIP WHERE I HOPED TO FIND SOMETHING FOR MY PRESENT SUBSISTENCE
BUT ABOVE ALL THE RUBIES AND EMERALDS FOR HE HAD NONE IN HIS TREASURY THAT EQUALLED THEM
AND IF EVER THAT SHOULD COME TO PASS AGAIN FOR MY PART I AM RESOLVED TO PLUCK UP THE HEART OF A MAN AND TO TRY MY UTMOST TO GET FROM UNDER HIS HAND
BUT AGAIN WHEN I FELT THE SMART OF THEIR ARROWS UPON MY FACE AND HANDS WHICH WERE ALL IN BLISTERS AND MANY OF THE DARTS STILL STICKING IN THEM
THAT AS I COULD NOT FORESEE WHAT THE ENDS OF DIVINE WISDOM MIGHT BE IN ALL THIS SO I WAS NOT TO DISPUTE HIS SOVEREIGNTY
TUSH SAID OBSTINATE AWAY WITH YOUR BOOK
I WOULD GLADLY HAVE TAKEN A DOZEN OF THE NATIVES BUT THIS WAS A THING THE EMPEROR WOULD BY NO MEANS PERMIT
THE WHITE WERE PEARLS
AND THERE WHENEVER I HAD OCCASION TO BE ABSENT FROM MY CHIEF SEAT I TOOK UP MY COUNTRY HABITATION
THAT TO HAVE SEEN ONE OF MY OWN SPECIES WOULD HAVE SEEMED TO ME A RAISING ME FROM DEATH TO LIFE AND THE GREATEST BLESSING THAT HEAVEN ITSELF NEXT TO THE SUPREME BLESSING OF SALVATION COULD BESTOW--I SAY THAT I SHOULD NOW TREMBLE AT THE VERY APPREHENSIONS OF SEEING A MAN AND WAS READY TO SINK INTO THE GROUND AT BUT THE SHADOW OR SILENT APPEARANCE OF A MAN HAVING SET HIS FOOT IN THE ISLAND
THE ROBBERS STAYED SOME TIME WITHIN THE ROCK DURING WHICH ALI BABA FEARFUL OF BEING CAUGHT REMAINED IN THE TREE
AND PRODUCING HIS CREDENTIALS UNDER THE SIGNET ROYAL WHICH HE APPLIED CLOSE TO MY EYES SPOKE ABOUT TEN MINUTES WITHOUT ANY SIGNS OF ANGER BUT WITH A KIND OF DETERMINATE RESOLUTION
ARISE MY LIEGEMEN AND BE GOOD SUBJECTS IN FUTURE
AND NOW I BEGAN TO THINK SEDATELY
DEPART AND HAUNT MY COUCH NO MORE
WHEN I HAD DONE PRAYING I TOOK UP MY BIBLE AND OPENING IT TO READ THE FIRST WORDS THAT PRESENTED TO ME WERE WAIT ON THE LORD AND BE OF GOOD CHEER AND HE SHALL STRENGTHEN THY HEART
TWO OR THREE DAYS AFTER HE WAS SETTLED ALI BABA CAME TO SEE HIS SON AND THE CAPTAIN OF THE ROBBERS RECOGNIZED HIM AT ONCE AND SOON LEARNED FROM HIS SON WHO HE WAS
HIS WHOLE NAME WAS HIERONYMUS KARL FRIEDRICH VON MUNCHAUSEN A GERMAN OF COURSE BUT SERVING IN THE RUSSIAN ARMY
WE ROWED BY MY COMPUTATION ABOUT THREE LEAGUES TILL WE WERE ABLE TO WORK NO LONGER BEING ALREADY SPENT WITH LABOR WHILE WE WERE IN THE SHIP
WHEN THEY CAME DIRECTLY OVER MY SHIP THEY HOVERED AND ONE OF THEM LET GO HIS ROCK
AT LAST ONE CAME TO THE DOOR AND ASKED WHO WAS THERE
THE NEXT MAN WAS SHOT IN THE BODY AND FELL JUST BY HIM THOUGH HE DID NOT DIE TILL AN HOUR OR TWO AFTER
BUT BEWARE OF THE FUTURE LEST A WORSE THING BEFALL THEE
WHERE I WAS ABLE TO DRAW AN IMPERIAL FLEET IN MY HAND AND PERFORM THOSE OTHER ACTIONS WHICH WILL BE RECORDED FOREVER IN THE CHRONICLES OF THAT EMPIRE WHILE POSTERITY SHALL HARDLY BELIEVE THEM ALTHOUGH ATTESTED BY MILLIONS
YES SAID CHRISTIAN FOR THAT WAS HIS NAME BECAUSE THAT ALL WHICH YOU SHALL FORSAKE IS NOT WORTHY TO BE COMPARED WITH A LITTLE OF THAT THAT I AM SEEKING TO ENJOY
TAKE CARE MY BATHING LINEN BE READY GIVE THEM TO ABDALLA WHICH WAS THE SLAVE'S NAME AND MAKE ME SOME GOOD BROTH AGAINST I RETURN AFTER THIS HE WENT TO BED
SUCH AS IT IS I HEARTILY OFFER IT SIR REPLIED COGIA HOUSSAIN I AM THOROUGHLY PERSUADED OF YOUR GOOD WILL
IT WAS AFTER THREE HOURS GOOD WALKING THAT THE SERVANTS OF CEDRIC WITH THEIR MYSTERIOUS GUIDE ARRIVED AT A SMALL OPENING IN THE FOREST
THE FIRST CARE OF THE ROBBERS AFTER THIS WAS TO EXAMINE THE CAVE
AND HE AND SHE CONTINUED TO LEAD A QUIET AND NOT UNHAPPY LIFE IN THEIR NEW HOME
WHEN THE HORSES WERE UNABLE TO PROCEED ANY FURTHER BROWN DISMOUNTED FROM THE CARRIAGE IN ORDER TO LOOK FOR A HOUSE WHERE HE COULD ASK THE WAY
THE TALK THAT THEY HAD WITH THE SHINING ONES WAS ABOUT THE GLORY OF THE PLACE WHO TOLD THEM THAT THE BEAUTY AND GLORY OF IT WAS INEXPRESSIBLE
AND I PILED ALL THE EMPTY CHESTS AND CASKS UP IN A CIRCLE ROUND THE TENT TO FORTIFY IT FROM ANY SUDDEN ATTEMPT EITHER FROM MAN OR BEAST
WE SHALL MEET AGAIN I TRUST SAID THE DEFEATED CHAMPION AS HE EXTRICATED HIMSELF FROM THE STIRRUPS AND FALLEN STEED
WHEN HE WAS OLD ENOUGH TO LEARN A TRADE HIS FATHER TOOK HIM INTO HIS OWN SHOP AND TAUGHT HIM HOW TO USE HIS NEEDLE
AS INDEED I EXPECTED
I SAT DOWN UPON THE GRASS TO RECOVER MYSELF FROM MY FATIGUE AFTER WHICH I WENT INTO THE ISLAND TO EXPLORE IT
SO HE WENT IN AND WAS CLOATHED WITH SUCH GARMENTS AS THEY
FOR THE SHIP WAS LEAKY AND VERY MUCH DISABLED AND HE WAS FOR GOING DIRECTLY BACK TO THE COAST OF BRAZIL
SO THERE WAS NO HOPE FROM HER
THE NEIGHBORS ALSO CAME OUT TO SEE HIM RUN
BUT AT ONCE SUMMONING UP ALL HER ENERGIES SHE PLACED UPON THE DROOPING HEAD OF THE VICTOR THE SPLENDID CHAPLET WHICH WAS THE DESTINED REWARD OF THE DAY
THE GENIE LED HIM THROUGH ALL THE APARTMENTS WHERE HE FOUND OFFICERS AND SLAVES HABITED ACCORDING TO THEIR RANK AND THE SERVICES TO WHICH THEY WERE APPOINTED
AND LOOKING AT COGIA HOUSSAIN KNEW HIM AT FIRST SIGHT NOTWITHSTANDING HIS DISGUISE TO BE THE CAPTAIN OF THE ROBBERS AND EXAMINING HIM VERY CAREFULLY PERCEIVED THAT HE HAD A DAGGER UNDER HIS GARMENT
OR IF I ESCAPED THESE DANGERS FOR A DAY OR TWO WHAT COULD I EXPECT BUT A MISERABLE DEATH OF COLD AND HUNGER
I AT LAST ARRIVED SAFE AT BAGDAD AND IMMEDIATELY WAITED UPON THE CALIPH TO GIVE HIM AN ACCOUNT OF MY EMBASSY
AT LAST WHEN ALL THEIR SIGNALS AND FIRING PROVED FRUITLESS AND THEY FOUND THE BOAT DID NOT STIR WE SAW THEM BY THE HELP OF MY GLASSES HOIST ANOTHER BOAT OUT AND ROW TOWARDS THE SHORE
I LET THEM KNOW THAT BY MY DIRECTION THE SHIP HAD BEEN SEIZED
HE AS WELL AS HIS BROTHER ALWAYS CARRIED A GEOMANTIC SQUARE INSTRUMENT ABOUT HIM
THE PEOPLE WHO GATHERED PEPPER CAME TO MEET ME AS SOON AS THEY SAW ME AND ASKED ME IN ARABIC WHO I WAS AND WHENCE I CAME
AND AS THE EARTH WAS LIGHT THEY WERE NOT LONG IN DOING IT
OH WHAT RIDICULOUS RESOLUTIONS MEN TAKE WHEN POSSESSED WITH FEAR
WHEN THE VISITOR HAD GONE MRS BERTRAM THE MOTHER OF THE BABY BOY WAS VERY ANXIOUS TO READ THE PAPER FOR SHE WAS A SUPERSTITIOUS LADY
MASTER GOD PRESERVE YOU
AND BEFORE HE RELEASED HER FROM THE ENCHANTMENT HE PERSUADED HER TO GIVE HIM THE LITTLE INDIAN BOY HE SO MUCH DESIRED TO HAVE
HE NOTICED TOO THAT THERE WAS A ROLL OF LINEN ABOUT THE DYING MAN'S HEAD WHICH WAS DEEPLY STAINED WITH BLOOD
BUT WHEN THE ROBBER AND HIS CAPTAIN CAME TO THE STREET THEY FOUND THE SAME DIFFICULTY
AND THE FIRST THING DEMETRIUS SAW WHEN HE WOKE WAS ALSO HELENA
THE RUFFIAN WHO INSTANTLY SAW HE WAS BETRAYED TURNED HIS FIRST VENGEANCE ON MEG MERRILIES AT WHOM HE DISCHARGED A PISTOL
BUT THE ONLY EFFECT OF THEIR WORDS WAS TO MAKE HIM WISH MORE TO COME OFF WELL IN THE ENCOUNTER SO AS TO WIN PRAISE FROM SUCH SWEET LADIES
THE SNOW LAY ON THE GROUND AS HE AND THE GIPSY CAME OUT AND AS HE FOLLOWED HER HE NOTICED THAT SHE CHOSE THE TRACK THE MEN HAD TAKEN SO THAT HER FOOTPRINTS MIGHT NOT BE SEEN
WHEN ALL THE MONEY WAS SPENT ALADDIN HAD RECOURSE AGAIN TO THE LAMP
WELL GO YOUR WAYS SAID OBERON
SCRATCH MY HEAD PEASEBLOSSOM SAID THE CLOWN
IT WAS PLAIN TOO FROM THE THICK CLOUDS OF SMOKE THAT ROLLED PAST THE WINDOW THAT THE PRISON WAS ITSELF ON FIRE
FROM WHENCE ONE OF THEM WHO SEEMED TO BE A PERSON OF QUALITY MADE ME A LONG SPEECH WHEREOF I UNDERSTOOD NOT ONE SYLLABLE
AND THEY DID NOT KNOW BUT THAT HE STOOD SENTINEL OVER THEM AT THE ENTRANCE
FOR THE SEA HAVING HURRIED ME ALONG AS BEFORE LANDED ME OR RATHER DASHED ME AGAINST A PIECE OF A ROCK AND THAT WITH SUCH FORCE AS IT LEFT ME SENSELESS AND INDEED HELPLESS AS TO MY OWN DELIVERANCE
THERE WERE SIX AMBASSADORS WITH A TRAIN OF ABOUT FIVE HUNDRED PERSONS AND THEIR ENTRY WAS VERY MAGNIFICENT SUITABLE TO THE GRANDEUR OF THEIR MASTER AND THE IMPORTANCE OF THEIR BUSINESS
AND AFTER SOME TIME I THINK IT WAS A YEAR AND A HALF I RAISED RAFTERS FROM IT LEANING TO THE ROCK AND THATCHED OR COVERED IT WITH BOUGHS OF TREES AND SUCH THINGS AS I COULD GET TO KEEP OUT THE RAIN
BUT I MIGHT HAVE FORESEEN THAT I COULD NO MORE TURN HER AND SET HER UPRIGHT UPON HER BOTTOM THAN I COULD REMOVE THE ISLAND
AFTER THIS HE INCREASED HIS ASSIDUITIES CARESSED HIM IN THE MOST ENGAGING MANNER MADE HIM SOME SMALL PRESENTS AND OFTEN ASKED HIM TO DINE AND SUP WITH HIM WHEN HE TREATED HIM VERY HANDSOMELY
WE MADE A LONG MARCH THE REMAINING PART OF THAT DAY AND RESTED AT NIGHT WITH FIVE HUNDRED GUARDS ON EACH SIDE OF ME HALF WITH TORCHES AND HALF WITH BOWS AND ARROWS READY TO SHOOT ME IF I SHOULD OFFER TO STIR
NEITHER DID ANY MAN MEET HIM WITH THE LEAST ENCOURAGEMENT
THAT IF HE WOULD LET ONE OF THE CREW BRING MY CLOSET INTO HIS CABIN I WOULD OPEN IT THERE BEFORE HIM AND SHOW HIM MY GOODS
HE ENDEAVOURED TO STRUGGLE TO THE SIDE OF THE SLOUGH BUT COULD NOT GET OUT BECAUSE OF THE BURDEN THAT WAS UPON HIS BACK
HE PROMISED THE FRIAR A LARGE REWARD FOR DOING THE ERRAND AND AS THEY PARTED AT THE POSTERN DOOR HE THRUST INTO CEDRIC'S RELUCTANT HAND A PIECE OF GOLD ADDING REMEMBER I WILL FLAY OFF THY COWL AND SKIN IF THOU FAILEST IN THY PURPOSE WHEN FRONT-DE-BOEUF REJOINED HIS FRIENDS AND FOUND OUT THE TRICK WHICH HAD BEEN PLAYED UPON HIM AND THAT CEDRIC HAD ESCAPED HIS RAGE WAS UNBOUNDED AND IT WAS ONLY ON DE BRACY INTERCEDING FOR HIM THAT HE CONSENTED TO SPARE THE LIFE OF THE POOR JESTER
SO DID THE EMPRESS AND YOUNG PRINCES OF THE BLOOD
GO SAID HE FOLLOW THEM AND ACT AS YOU SEE THEM DO
AND WHITHER ARE YOU BOUND
AND LEARNING THAT SHE WAS LIKELY TO BE FOUND WITH A PARTY OF SKATERS ON A LAKE IN THE NEIGHBOURHOOD HE PROCEEDED IN THAT DIRECTION

THE BARON'S WONDERFUL DOG BY R
THUS MANY DAYS PASSED PLEASANTLY AWAY

BUT AS HE HAD TAKEN ME IN HIS ARMS I HELD FAST BY HIM OR I SHOULD HAVE FALLEN TO THE GROUND
AND WITHOUT INDULGING IN IDLE WORDS AGAINST THE SULTAN THE VIZIER OR HIS SON HE DETERMINED IF POSSIBLE TO PREVENT THE MARRIAGE

I'D RATHER HAVE A HANDFUL OR TWO OF GOOD DRIED PEAS SAID THE CLOWN
AND WHEN YOU HAVE DONE I WILL GIVE YOU ANOTHER PIECE OF GOLD AFTER BABA MUSTAPHA HAD FINISHED HIS TASK SHE BLINDFOLDED HIM AGAIN GAVE HIM THE THIRD PIECE OF GOLD AS SHE HAD PROMISED AND RECOMMENDING SECRECY TO HIM CARRIED HIM BACK TO THE PLACE WHERE SHE FIRST BOUND HIS EYES PULLED OFF THE BANDAGE AND LET HIM GO HOME BUT WATCHED HIM THAT HE RETURNED TOWARD HIS STALL TILL HE WAS QUITE OUT OF SIGHT FOR FEAR HE SHOULD HAVE THE CURIOSITY TO RETURN AND DODGE HER
AND HAVING SAID FAREWELL THE TWO JEWS PARTED ISAAC TO SEEK OUT IVANHOE AND THE RABBI TO GO TO YORK TO LOOK FOR OTHER ASSISTANCE
THE WORLD IS STILL DECEIVED WITH ORNAMENT AND SO NO GAUDY GOLD OR SHINING SILVER FOR ME
THEY DROVE AWAY THE MULES WHO STRAYED THROUGH THE FOREST SO FAR THAT THEY WERE SOON OUT OF SIGHT AND WENT DIRECTLY WITH THEIR NAKED SABRES IN THEIR HANDS TO THE DOOR WHICH ON THEIR CAPTAIN PRONOUNCING THE PROPER WORDS IMMEDIATELY OPENED
AND SO I MADE SIGNS TO HIM AGAIN TO DO SO
UNDER THAT PALMER'S GOWN REPLIED THE JEW IS HIDDEN A KNIGHT'S CHAIN AND SPURS OF GOLD
SOMETIMES THE MINISTER HAS IT ENTIRELY TO HIMSELF
THE SHORT TIME I CONTINUED IN ENGLAND I MADE A CONSIDERABLE PROFIT BY SHOWING MY CATTLE TO MANY PERSONS OF QUALITY AND OTHERS
A PILGRIM AT LENGTH WHO SAT BY THE CHIMNEY TOOK COMPASSION UPON HIM AND RESIGNED HIS SEAT SAYING BRIEFLY OLD MAN MY GARMENTS ARE DRIED MY HUNGER IS APPEASED THOU ART BOTH WET AND FASTING AND SO SAYING HE PLACED SOME FOOD BEFORE THE JEW ON THE SMALL TABLE AT WHICH HE HAD HIMSELF SUPPED AND WITHOUT WAITING FOR THE OLD MAN'S THANKS WENT TO THE OTHER SIDE OF THE HALL
HIS ONLY COMFORT NOW WAS IN HEARING OF THE SERIOUS LOSSES WHICH HAD BEFALLEN ANTONIO SOME OF WHOSE SHIPS WERE WRECKED
IN THAT VERY MOMENT THIS POOR WRETCH SEEING HIMSELF A LITTLE AT LIBERTY AND UNBOUND NATURE INSPIRED HIM WITH HOPES OF LIFE AND HE STARTED AWAY FROM THEM AND RAN WITH INCREDIBLE SWIFTNESS ALONG THE SANDS DIRECTLY TOWARDS ME
IT WAS NOT HOWEVER SUCH AN EASY MATTER TO MAKE THEIR EXIT FROM THE MANSION
NOW THIS WOOD WHERE LYSANDER WAS TO MEET HERMIA AND WHERE THE OTHER TWO HAD DECIDED TO FOLLOW THEM WAS FULL OF FAIRIES AS MOST WOODS ARE IF ONE ONLY HAD THE EYES TO SEE THEM AND IN THIS WOOD ON THIS NIGHT WERE THE KING AND QUEEN OF THE FAIRIES OBERON AND TITANIA
FOLLOW THINE OWN FATE AND LEAVE ME TO MINE AS SHE SPOKE SHE VANISHED THROUGH A PRIVATE DOOR AND FRONT-DE BOEUF ENTERED THE APARTMENT
THEN I KNEW THAT MY GOATS WANTED TO BE MILKED TOO WHICH USUALLY WAS MY EVENING DIVERSION AND THE POOR CREATURES WERE IN GREAT PAIN AND INCONVENIENCE FOR WANT OF IT
WHEN HE HAD SOLD THE LAST DISH HE HAD RECOURSE TO THE TRAY WHICH WEIGHED TEN TIMES AS MUCH AS THE DISHES AND WOULD HAVE CARRIED IT TO HIS OLD PURCHASER BUT THAT IT WAS TOO LARGE AND CUMBERSOME
THE OFFICER WHO IS BEFORE HIM ON THE SAME ELEPHANT CRIES FROM TIME TO TIME WITH A LOUD VOICE BEHOLD THE GREAT MONARCH THE POTENT AND REDOUBTABLE SULTAN OF THE INDIES THE MONARCH GREATER THAN SOLOMON AND THE POWERFUL MAHARAJA AFTER HE HAS PRONOUNCED THOSE WORDS THE OFFICER BEHIND THE THRONE CRIES IN HIS TURN THIS MONARCH SO GREAT AND SO POWERFUL MUST DIE MUST DIE MUST DIE AND THE OFFICER BEFORE REPLIES PRAISE ALONE BE TO HIM WHO LIVETH FOR EVER AND EVER THE CALIPH WAS MUCH PLEASED WITH MY ACCOUNT AND SENT ME HOME WITH A RICH PRESENT
I THEN ADVANCED FORWARD NEAR HALF A MILE BUT COULD NOT DISCOVER ANY SIGN OF HOUSES OR INHABITANTS
LITTLE MORE REMAINS TO BE TOLD
SO EVERY DAY AT LOW WATER I WENT ON BOARD AND BROUGHT AWAY SOMETHING OR OTHER
TAKE HER HE SAID SHE IS THINE OWN IN THE MEANTIME ANTONIO AND SEBASTIAN IN ANOTHER PART OF THE ISLAND WERE PLOTTING THE MURDER OF ALONSO THE KING OF NAPLES FOR FERDINAND BEING DEAD AS THEY THOUGHT SEBASTIAN WOULD SUCCEED TO THE THRONE ON ALONSO'S DEATH
HE SHALL NOT PRESUME TO COME INTO OUR METROPOLIS WITHOUT OUR EXPRESS ORDER
I CANNOT EXPRESS THE JOY IT AFFORDS ME
IT WAS RUMOURED TOO AMONGST THE COUNTRY-FOLK THAT GLOSSIN WAS THE MAN OF ALL OTHERS WHO WAS MOST EAGER TO TURN THE BERTRAMS OUT OF THEIR HOUSE IN ORDER THAT HE MIGHT BUY THE PROPERTY HIMSELF AND BECOME THE LAIRD OF ELLANGOWAN
THESE HOOKS WERE TIED BY A LONG CORD TO THE HARNESS AND THUS MY HAT WAS DRAGGED ALONG FOR ABOVE HALF AN ENGLISH MILE
I LONGED TO SEE THE OCEAN WHICH MUST BE THE ONLY SCENE OF MY ESCAPE IF EVER IT SHOULD HAPPEN
AND AFTER MANY GRACIOUS EXPRESSIONS WHICH TO AVOID THE CENSURE OF VANITY I SHALL NOT REPEAT HE ADDED THAT HE HOPED I SHOULD PROVE A USEFUL SERVANT AND WELL DESERVE ALL THE FAVORS HE HAD ALREADY CONFERRED UPON ME OR MIGHT DO FOR THE FUTURE
I TOOK OUT ONE OF THE FOWLING-PIECES AND ONE OF THE PISTOLS AND A HORN OF POWDER
SO I POINTED TO HIM AND SHOWED HIM THE SAVAGE THAT HE WAS NOT DEAD
JOY AND GLADNESS SUCCEEDED TO SORROW AND GRIEF
HIS FAILURE TO OPEN IT REMINDED HIM PAINFULLY THAT HE WAS NOW A PRISONER
THE SERPENT FAILED NOT TO COME AT THE USUAL HOUR AND WENT ROUND THE TREE SEEKING FOR AN OPPORTUNITY TO DEVOUR ME BUT WAS PREVENTED BY THE RAMPART I HAD MADE
SO I WENT TO WORK AND WITH A CARPENTER'S SAW I CUT A SPARE TOPMAST INTO THREE LENGTHS AND ADDED THEM TO MY RAFT WITH A GREAT DEAL OF LABOR AND PAINS
SO THEY TOLD THE KING BUT HE WOULD NOT COME DOWN TO SEE HIM BUT COMMANDED THE TWO SHINING ONES THAT CONDUCTED CHRISTIAN AND HOPEFUL TO THE CITY TO GO OUT AND TAKE IGNORANCE AND BIND HIM HAND AND FOOT AND HAVE HIM AWAY
AFTER THIS IT COST ME A MONTH TO SHAPE IT AND DUB IT TO A PROPORTION AND TO SOMETHING LIKE THE BOTTOM OF A BOAT THAT IT MIGHT SWIM UPRIGHT AS IT OUGHT TO DO
I LEFT THEM MY FIRE-ARMS
WITH WHOM I CONTINUED THREE YEARS AND A HALF MAKING A VOYAGE OR TWO INTO THE LEVANT AND SOME OTHER PARTS
SO HE WENT HIS WAY AND I CAME MINE
WHEN REQUIRED TO GIVE SOME PROOF OF HIS RANK IN THE ARMY HE STATED THAT HIS LUGGAGE HAD BEEN STOLEN
AT WHICH THE CAPTAIN WAS ENRAGED AND THE ROBBER IN AS GREAT CONFUSION AS HIS PREDECESSOR
TAKE AND DO WITH THEM AS YOU PLEASE I TOOK OUT WHAT WAS MOST VALUABLE IN MY BALES AND PRESENTED THEM TO THE MAHARAJA WHO KNOWING MY MISFORTUNE ASKED ME HOW I CAME BY SUCH RARITIES
THE POOR GIRL WAS ALMOST DISTRACTED
COME LET ME BLIND YOUR EYES AT THE SAME PLACE
WHEN THIS WAS DONE I STUCK ALL THE GROUND WITHOUT MY WALL FOR A GREAT LENGTH EVERY WAY AS FULL WITH STAKES OR STICKS OF THE OSIER-LIKE WOOD WHICH I FOUND SO APT TO GROW AS THEY COULD WELL STAND
YES AND THEY PUT ME IN HOPE AND FEAR
DURING THE CONFUSION WHICH REIGNED AMONGST THE FOLLOWERS OF FRONT DE-BOEUF WHEN THE ATTACK HAD COMMENCED REBECCA HAD BEEN ALLOWED TO TAKE THE PLACE OF THE OLD CRONE ULRICA WHO WAS IN CLOSE ATTENDANCE ON THE WOUNDED MAN WHO HAD BEEN BROUGHT INTO THE CASTLE IN COMPANY WITH ISAAC OF YORK AND THE OTHER CAPTIVES
BUT FOR ME THAT WAS THUS ENTERED AND ESTABLISHED AND HAD NOTHING TO DO BUT TO GO ON AS I HAD BEGUN FOR THREE OR FOUR YEARS MORE AND TO HAVE SENT FOR THE OTHER HUNDRED POUNDS FROM ENGLAND AND WHO IN THAT TIME AND WITH THAT LITTLE ADDITION COULD SCARCE HAVE FAILED OF BEING WORTH THREE OR FOUR THOUSAND POUNDS STERLING AND THAT INCREASING TOO
AND WHEN HE RETURNED INTO THE HALL HE FOUND INSTEAD OF HIS OWN POOR RAIMENT A ROBE THE MAGNIFICENCE OF WHICH ASTONISHED HIM
AND HAVING SATISFIED OUR HUNGER WITH FRUIT WE MOUNTED IT ACCORDINGLY
ONE CREATURE ALONE HE FOUND IT NECESSARY TO TREAT WITH HARSHNESS
I ALSO SOUGHT TO HIDE MYSELFS BUT I COULD NOT FOR THE MAN THAT SAT UPON THE CLOUD STILL KEPT HIS EYE UPON ME
THE STACK I WAS REPOSING ON WAS THE LARGEST IN THE YARD CONTAINING ABOUT FIVE HUNDRED LOAD
BUT PASSING BY A GOLDSMITH'S SHOP THE GOLDSMITH PERCEIVING HIM CALLED TO HIM AND SAID MY LAD I IMAGINE THAT YOU HAVE SOMETHING TO SELL TO THE JEW WHOM I OFTEN SEE YOU VISIT
THIS WAS WHAT I WISHED FOR AND IMMEDIATELY LEAVING FRIDAY AND THE CAPTAIN'S MATE TO THEIR BUSINESS I TOOK THE REST WITH ME
WE IMMEDIATELY LEFT THE PALACE AND CAME TO THE SHORE WHERE WE MADE SOME RAFTS EACH LARGE ENOUGH TO CARRY THREE MEN WITH SOME TIMBER THAT LAY ABOUT IN GREAT QUANTITIES
I RESOLVED TO WAIT TO SEE IF THEY DID NOT SEPARATE
FOR MY CONSCIENCE WOULD NOT SUFFER ME TO IMITATE THE BAD PRACTICE OF TOO MANY AMONG MY BRETHREN
AND SO BY SWIMMING TO PRESERVE MY BREATHING AND PILOT MYSELF TOWARD THE SHORE IF POSSIBLE MY GREATEST CONCERN NOW BEING THAT THE WAVE AS IT WOULD CARRY ME A GREAT WAY TOWARD THE SHORE WHEN IT CAME ON MIGHT NOT CARRY ME BACK AGAIN WITH IT WHEN IT GAVE BACK TOWARD THE SEA
NOW THE MONSTER WAS HIDEOUS TO BEHOLD
THE CABLE WAS ABOUT AS THICK AS PACKTHREAD AND THE BARS OF THE LENGTH AND SIZE OF A KNITTING NEEDLE
IN BAGDAD AND CAIRO TO-DAY THAT CAFE NEVER LACKS CUSTOMERS WHERE THE BLIND STORYTELLER RELATES TO THE SPELL-BOUND ARABS SOME CHAPTER FROM THE IMMORTAL ARABIAN NIGHTS THE KING OF ALL WONDER BOOKS
BUT THE REMEMBRANCE OF WHAT I HAD FELT WHICH PROBABLY MIGHT NOT BE THE WORST THEY COULD DO AND THE PROMISE OF HONOR I MADE THEM FOR SO I INTERPRETED MY SUBMISSIVE BEHAVIOR SOON DROVE OUT THESE IMAGINATIONS
BUT BEING PERSUADED THAT I WAS NOT ASLEEP I RECITED THE FOLLOWING WORDS IN ARABIC ALOUD
SIR WHAT THINK YOU
ON MY RETURN I ASKED FOR DIANA MY SETTER
AND COGIA HOUSSAIN SEEING THAT SHE WAS COMING TO HIM HAD PULLED HIS PURSE OUT OF HIS BOSOM TO MAKE HER A PRESENT
NOT ONLY BECAUSE HE WOULD NOT DISOBEY HIS FATHER BUT ALSO BECAUSE IT WAS AGREEABLE TO HIS INCLINATION
THE SHIP IN WHICH I SAILED WAS THE FIRST KNOWN TO BE DRIVEN WITHIN SIGHT OF THAT COAST AND THE KING HAD GIVEN STRICT ORDERS THAT IF AT ANY TIME ANOTHER APPEARED IT SHOULD BE TAKEN ASHORE AND WITH ALL ITS CREW AND PASSENGERS BROUGHT IN A TUMBREL TO LORBRULGRUD
WHERE AND IN WHAT CONDITION DID YOU LEAVE HIM I KNOW LITTLE OF THE KNIGHT OF IVANHOE ANSWERED THE PALMER WITH A TROUBLED VOICE
AND ABOUT FOUR YARDS FROM ME OVER AGAINST MY RIGHT EAR I HEARD A KNOCKING FOR ABOVE AN HOUR LIKE THAT OF PEOPLE AT WORK
I AM NOT FRIENDS WITH HIM NOW IT RESTS WITH YOU TO MAKE UP THE QUARREL SAID THE KING
THE TRUMPETS INSTANTLY SOUNDED WHILE THE HERALDS PROCLAIMED THE LADY ROWENA THE QUEEN OF BEAUTY AND OF LOVE FOR THE ENSUING DAY
THE INVESTIGATION WAS CONCLUDED BY BOTH HATTERAICK AND GLOSSIN BEING SENT TO GAOL
TO FINISH THE DESCRIPTION OF THIS PLACE IT IS NOT POSSIBLE FOR SHIPS TO GET OFF WHEN ONCE THEY APPROACH WITHIN A CERTAIN DISTANCE
SO BASSANIO WAS FORGIVEN AND MADE HAPPIER THAN EVER TO KNOW HOW RICH A PRIZE HE HAD DRAWN IN THE LOTTERY OF THE CASKETS

AND SHORTLY AFTER BRIAN DE BOIS-GUILBERT ENTERED THE APARTMENT
NOW I BEGAN SORELY TO REPENT THAT I HAD DUG MY CAVE SO LARGE AS TO BRING A DOOR THROUGH AGAIN WHICH DOOR AS I SAID CAME OUT BEYOND WHERE MY FORTIFICATION JOINED TO THE ROCK
THE TRUMPETS HAD NO SOONER GIVEN THE SIGNAL THAN THE COMBATANTS VANISHED FROM THEIR POSTS WITH THE SPEED OF LIGHTNING AND CLOSED IN THE CENTRE OF THE LISTS WITH THE SHOCK OF A THUNDERBOLT
BEAUMANOIR TORE OPEN THE SEAL AND PERUSED THE LETTER IN HASTE WITH AN EXPRESSION OF SURPRISE AND HORROR
I DISCOVERED NOTHING ALL THAT DAY
I TOOK THE KING OF SERENDIB'S LETTER AND WENT TO PRESENT MYSELF AT THE GATE OF THE COMMANDER OF THE FAITHFUL AND WAS IMMEDIATELY CONDUCTED TO THE THRONE OF THE CALIPH
WHEREUPON SEVEN MONSTERS LIKE HIMSELF CAME TOWARD HIM WITH REAPING-HOOKS IN THEIR HANDS EACH HOOK ABOUT THE LARGENESS OF SIX SCYTHES
NONE KNOW BETTER HOW DIFFICULT IT IS TO FIND WRITERS WITH A GOOD NARRATIVE STYLE THAN THOSE EDITORS WHOSE TRAINING AND EXPERIENCE HAVE MADE THEM REALIZE ITS VALUE AND IMPORTANCE
AT LAST HE RECOLLECTED ME HIMSELF AND EMBRACING ME HEAVEN BE PRAISED SAID HE FOR YOUR HAPPY ESCAPE

THEY NEEDED VERY FEW ARGUMENTS TO PERSUADE A SINGLE MAN TO YIELD WHEN HE SAW FIVE MEN UPON HIM AND HIS COMRADE KNOCKED DOWN
BUT INSTEAD OF DOING SO WHICH I LAUGH AT EVERY TIME I THINK OF IT THE OLD MAN WHO TO ME APPEARED QUITE DECREPIT THREW HIS LEGS NIMBLY ABOUT MY NECK

NOR IS IT EVEN FOR THAT POOR OLD MAN
THIS ENTERTAINMENT LASTED TILL NIGHT WHEN ALADDIN WOULD HAVE TAKEN LEAVE OF HIS UNCLE TO GO HOME

HE ROSE ACCORDINGLY IN HASTE
FOR AS FOR MYSELF I HAD RESOLVED TO QUIT THE ISLAND WITH ALL MY MEN AND HAD TAKEN PASSAGE WITH THE CAPTAIN TO GO TO ENGLAND

THEN I THOUGHT THAT IT IS EASIER GOING OUT OF THE WAY WHEN WE ARE IN THAN GOING IN WHEN WE ARE OUT YET THEY ADVENTURED TO GO BACK
THESE THOUGHTS TOOK ME UP MANY HOURS DAYS NAY I MAY SAY WEEKS AND MONTHS
WE SET IN THE LEE BRACES AND HAULED FORWARD BY THE WEATHER-BOWLINGS AND HAULED THEM TIGHT AND BELAYED THEM AND HAULED OVER THE MIZZEN TACK TO WINDWARD AND KEPT HER FULL AND BY AS NEAR AS SHE WOULD LIE
WHEN HE RETURNED FROM THE BATHS HE WAS VERY MUCH SURPRISED TO SEE THE OIL JARS AND THAT THE MERCHANT WAS NOT GONE WITH THE MULES
HE FANCIED AT FIRST THAT HE WAS MISTAKEN AND EXAMINED THE TWO WINDOWS ON EACH SIDE AND AFTERWARD ALL THE FOUR AND TWENTY
THE TEMPEST RETOLD BY E
THY PENITENTS FATHER HE SAID HAVE MADE A LONG SHRIFT
I SHOULD LIKE SOME GOOD DRY OATS SAID THE CLOWN-FOR HIS DONKEY'S HEAD MADE HIM DESIRE DONKEY'S FOOD--"AND SOME HAY TO FOLLOW SHALL SOME OF MY FAIRIES FETCH YOU NEW NUTS FROM THE SQUIRREL'S HOUSE ASKED THE QUEEN
HAVING LADEN OUR VESSEL WITH COCOANUTS WE SET SAIL AND PASSED BY THE ISLANDS WHERE PEPPER GROWS IN GREAT PLENTY
NEITHER DID I SEE ANY PROSPECT BEFORE ME BUT THAT OF PERISHING WITH HUNGER OR BEING DEVOURED BY WILD BEASTS
CEDRIC STARTED BACK IN AMAZEMENT
ANOTHER TIME ONE OF THE SERVANTS WHOSE OFFICE IT WAS TO FILL MY TROUGH EVERY THIRD DAY WITH FRESH WATER WAS SO CARELESS TO LET A HUGE FROG NOT PERCEIVING IT SLIP OUT OF HIS PAIL
BUT A LITTLE EASING THEM WHERE HE COMPLAINED THEY HURT HIM AND USING HIMSELF TO THEM HE TOOK TO THEM AT LENGTH VERY WELL
COME WITH ME AND I WILL GIVE YOU FAIRIES TO ATTEND ON YOU SO SHE CALLED FOUR FAIRIES WHOSE NAMES WERE PEASEBLOSSOM COBWEB MOTH AND MUSTARDSEED
SO THAT AS WE NEVER SUFFERED THEM TO SEE ME AS GOVERNOR I NOW APPEARED AS ANOTHER PERSON AND SPOKE OF THE GOVERNOR THE GARRISON THE CASTLE AND THE LIKE UPON ALL OCCASIONS
I TOLD HIM IT WAS WHAT I HAD BEEN USED TO FOR ABOVE TWO YEARS PAST AND THAT I ADMIRED AS MUCH AT THE VOICES OF HIM AND HIS MEN WHO SEEMED TO ME ONLY TO WHISPER AND YET I COULD HEAR THEM WELL ENOUGH
HIS SON DESERTED AND DECEIVED HIM AS ROBINSON CRUSOE DESERTED AND DECEIVED HIS FATHER AND IT ALMOST BROKE THE OLD MAN'S HEART
WE HAD ANOTHER BOAT ON BOARD
IN THIS COMBAT NO MAN CAN IMAGINE UNLESS HE HAD SEEN AND HEARD AS I DID WHAT YELLING AND HIDEOUS ROARING APOLLYON MADE ALL THE TIME OF THE FIGHT HE SPAKE LIKE A DRAGON
WHAT OUR COUNTRY WILL AFFORD I DO HERE PROMISE TO GIVE THEE
I TOOK THE ROUTE OF PERSIA TRAVELLED OVER SEVERAL PROVINCES AND THEN ARRIVED AT A PORT WHERE I EMBARKED
THOUGH ALADDIN AND HIS MOTHER HAD AN INEXHAUSTIBLE TREASURE IN THEIR LAMP AND MIGHT HAVE HAD WHATEVER THEY WISHED FOR YET THEY LIVED WITH THE SAME FRUGALITY AS BEFORE AND IT MAY EASILY BE SUPPOSED THAT THE MONEY FOR WHICH ALADDIN HAD SOLD THE DISHES AND TRAY WAS SUFFICIENT TO MAINTAIN THEM SOME TIME
I LAMENTED MY OWN FOLLY AND WILFULNESS IN ATTEMPTING A SECOND VOYAGE AGAINST THE ADVICE OF ALL MY FRIENDS AND RELATIONS
THE NEXT DAY I MADE ANOTHER VOYAGE AND NOW HAVING PLUNDERED THE SHIP OF WHAT WAS PORTABLE AND FIT TO HAND OUT I BEGAN WITH THE CABLES
I HAVE SEEN HIM AND SPOKEN WITH HIM PRINCE JOHN TURNED PALE TOTTERED AND CAUGHT AT THE BACK OF AN OAKEN BENCH TO SUPPORT HIMSELF
OBERON TOOK OFF THE ASS'S HEAD FROM THE CLOWN AND LEFT HIM TO FINISH HIS SLEEP WITH HIS OWN SILLY HEAD LYING ON THE THYME AND VIOLETS
THAT SHE LAY NOW IN THE ROAD
AND WHAT GRIEVES ME MOST IS THAT I HAVE BEEN THE CAUSE OF IT
THAT EITHER THERE WERE INHABITANTS IN IT AND THEY SHOULD ALL BE MURDERED OR ELSE THERE WERE DEVILS AND SPIRITS IN IT AND THEY SHOULD BE ALL CARRIED AWAY AND DEVOURED
SPEAK BOLDLY WHEN ALADDIN'S MOTHER HAD TAKEN ALL THESE PRECAUTIONS FOR FEAR OF THE SULTAN'S ANGER SHE TOLD HIM FAITHFULLY THE ERRAND ON WHICH HER SON HAD SENT HER AND THE EVENT WHICH LED TO HIS MAKING SO BOLD A REQUEST IN SPITE OF ALL HER REMONSTRANCES

NEAR THESE HE AND THE SLAVE ABDALLA DUG A TRENCH LONG AND WIDE ENOUGH TO HOLD THE BODIES OF THE ROBBERS

PASSION SEEMED TO BE MUCH DISCONTENT
AND HE WAS THE APTEST SCHOLAR THAT EVER WAS
NESBIT PROSPERO THE DUKE OF MILAN WAS A LEARNED AND STUDIOUS MAN WHO LIVED AMONG HIS BOOKS LEAVING THE MANAGEMENT OF HIS DUKEDOM TO HIS BROTHER ANTONIO IN WHOM INDEED HE HAD COMPLETE TRUST
I PUT MY COWS AND SHEEP INTO MY COAT-POCKETS AND GOT ON BOARD WITH ALL MY LITTLE CARGO OF PROVISIONS
THE VILLAGE OF KIPPLETRINGAN WAS SITUATED A LITTLE DISTANCE FROM THE SEA
THE DUKE GAVE HER WELCOME ON ACCOUNT OF THE GREAT BELLARIO'S INTRODUCTION AND LEFT THE SETTLEMENT OF THE CASE TO HER
FOR INDEED AT FIRST I WAS IN TOO MUCH HURRY AND NOT ONLY HURRY AS TO LABOR BUT IN TOO MUCH DISCOMPOSURE OF MIND
BUT WHEN THEY PERCEIVED THE WHOLE FLEET MOVING IN ORDER AND SAW ME PULLING AT THE END THEY SET UP SUCH A SCREAM OF GRIEF AND DESPAIR THAT IT IS ALMOST IMPOSSIBLE TO DESCRIBE OR CONCEIVE
TO WHICH THE COURT IMPATIENT TO HAVE ME GONE VERY READILY CONTRIBUTED
ALADDIN HAVING THUS LOADED HIMSELF WITH RICHES OF WHICH HE KNEW NOT THE VALUE RETURNED THROUGH THE THREE HALLS WITH THE UTMOST PRECAUTION AND SOON ARRIVED AT THE MOUTH OF THE CAVE WHERE THE AFRICAN MAGICIAN AWAITED HIM WITH THE UTMOST IMPATIENCE
I SHALL NOT TROUBLE THE READER WITH A PARTICULAR ACCOUNT OF THIS VOYAGE WHICH WAS VERY PROSPEROUS FOR THE MOST PART

SHE PLACED HERSELF JUST BEFORE THE SULTAN GRAND VIZIER AND THE GREAT LORDS WHO SAT IN COUNCIL ON HIS RIGHT AND LEFT HAND
JEALOUS OBERON ANSWERED THE QUEEN
HE HERE FELL IN WITH A FARMER NAMED DANDIE DINMONT A BIG ROLLICKING FELLOW WITH AN HONEST FACE AND KINDLY WAYS WITH WHOM HE BECAME FRIENDS IN A VERY LITTLE TIME
HOWEVER I DESIRED GLUMDALCLITCH TO LET ME DEAL WITH IT ALONE
HIS ART HAD ALSO TOLD HIM THAT HE WAS NOT PERMITTED TO TAKE IT HIMSELF BUT MUST RECEIVE IT AS A VOLUNTARY GIFT FROM THE HANDS OF ANOTHER PERSON
THEIR GRAVE WALK AT AN EQUAL DISTANCE FROM EACH OTHER
BUT MY GOOD LUCK BEGAN NOW TO LEAVE ME
THEN SAID CHRISTIAN IS THERE NO HOPE BUT YOU MUST BE KEPT IN THE IRON CAGE OF DESPAIR
AND I GAVE HIM A CAP WHICH I MADE OF HARE'S SKIN VERY CONVENIENT AND FASHIONABLE ENOUGH
I HAVE GIVEN HIM MY FAITH AND SWORN MY ALLEGIANCE TO HIM
AND THEY SUPPLIED US WITH RICE TO FATTEN US
HIS MAJESTY MOUNTED IMMEDIATELY AND WAS SO PLEASED WITH THEM THAT HE TESTIFIED HIS SATISFACTION BY LARGE PRESENTS
HENCE HE SUSPECTED THAT HIS PLOT TO MURDER ALI BABA AND PLUNDER HIS HOUSE WAS DISCOVERED
I THUS GRADUALLY COLLECTED AS MANY COCOANUTS AS PRODUCED ME A CONSIDERABLE SUM
BUT AS TO MY CARGO IT WAS A GREAT PART OF IT LOST ESPECIALLY THE IRON WHICH I EXPECTED WOULD HAVE BEEN OF GREAT USE TO ME
I ASKED HIM WHAT HE THOUGHT OF THE CIRCUMSTANCES OF MY LIFE AND WHETHER A DELIVERANCE WERE NOT WORTH VENTURING FOR
I ATTEMPTED TO ESCAPE BUT THAT ONLY ADDED IF AN ADDITION COULD BE MADE TO MY DISTRESS
AND WERE VERY UNEASY WHEN AFTER LONG CONSULTATION WE SAW THEM ALL START UP AND MARCH DOWN TOWARDS THE SEA
I THEN ASKED THE CAPTAIN HOW FAR HE RECKONED WE MIGHT BE FROM LAND
THEN SAID THE INTERPRETER THE COMFORTER BE ALWAYS WITH THEE GOOD CHRISTIAN TO GUIDE THEE IN THE WAY THAT LEADS TO THE CITY
HE RECEIVED ONE LETTER WHICH DISPLEASED HIM VERY MUCH FROM A GREAT FRIEND OF HIS WHO WAS LIVING IN THE NORTH OF ENGLAND MR MERVYN BY NAME IN WHOSE CARE HE HAD LEFT HIS DAUGHTER JULIA MANNERING WHEN HE WAS STARTING FOR KIPPLETRINGAN
THE OTHER ANSWERED AY AY
FOR THE CARRIAGE BEING STOPPED A WHILE TO ADJUST SOMETHING THAT WAS OUT OF ORDER TWO OR THREE OF THE YOUNG NATIVES HAD THE CURIOSITY TO SEE HOW I LOOKED WHEN I WAS ASLEEP
SOMETIMES THE EMPEROR HOLDS ONE END OF THE STICK AND HIS FIRST MINISTER THE OTHER
HIS END WAS ANSWERED
IN THE MIDST OF DINNER MY MISTRESS'S FAVORITE CAT LEAPED INTO HER LAP I HEARD A NOISE BEHIND ME LIKE THAT OF A DOZEN STOCKING WEAVERS AT WORK
I ANSWERED IN A FEW WORDS BUT IN THE MOST SUBMISSIVE MANNER LIFTING UP MY LEFT HAND AND BOTH MY EYES TO THE SUN AS CALLING HIM FOR A WITNESS
I TOLD HIM THAT SINCE FORTUNE WHETHER GOOD OR EVIL HAD THROWN A VESSEL IN MY WAY I WAS RESOLVED TO VENTURE MYSELF ON THE OCEAN RATHER THAN BE AN OCCASION OF DIFFERENCE BETWEEN TWO SUCH MIGHTY MONARCHS
WE CAME TO A THICK FOREST OF COCOA TREES VERY LOFTY WITH TRUNKS SO SMOOTH THAT IT WAS NOT POSSIBLE TO CLIMB TO THE BRANCHES THAT BORE THE FRUIT
ALADDIN WHO KNEW THAT ALL THE SULTAN'S ENDEAVORS TO MAKE THIS WINDOW LIKE THE REST WERE IN VAIN SENT FOR THE JEWELLERS AND GOLDSMITHS AND NOT ONLY COMMANDED THEM TO DESIST FROM THEIR WORK BUT ORDERED THEM TO UNDO WHAT THEY HAD BEGUN AND TO CARRY ALL THEIR JEWELS BACK TO THE SULTAN AND TO THE VIZIER
HAD THEY THOUGHT FIT TO HAVE GONE TO SLEEP THERE AS THE OTHER PART OF THEM HAD DONE THEY HAD DONE THE JOB FOR US
AND THEN RESUMED HER SONG
THEN FOR THEIR ENCOURAGEMENT THEY HEARD THE VOICE OF ONE SAYING LET THINE HEART BE TOWARDS THE HIGH-WAY EVEN THE WAY THAT THOU WENTEST TURN AGAIN BUT BY THIS TIME THE WATERS WERE GREATLY RISEN
CASSIM HAD NEVER EXPECTED SUCH AN INCIDENT AND WAS SO ALARMED AT THE DANGER HE WAS IN THAT THE MORE HE ENDEAVORED TO REMEMBER THE WORD SESAME THE MORE HIS MEMORY WAS CONFOUNDED AND HE HAD AS MUCH FORGOTTEN IT AS IF HE HAD NEVER HEARD IT MENTIONED HE THREW DOWN THE BAGS HE HAD LOADED HIMSELF WITH AND WALKED DISTRACTEDLY UP AND DOWN THE CAVE WITHOUT HAVING THE LEAST REGARD TO THE RICHES THAT WERE ROUND HIM
AND SPREADING ONE OF THE BEDS UPON THE GROUND LAYING MY TWO PISTOLS JUST AT MY HEAD AND MY GUN AT LENGTH BY ME I WENT TO BED FOR THE FIRST TIME AND SLEPT VERY QUIETLY ALL NIGHT FOR I WAS VERY WEARY AND HEAVY
ON OUR FIRST LANDING WE HAD DIVIDED OUR PROVISIONS AS EQUALLY AS WE COULD AND THUS EVERY ONE LIVED A LONGER OR SHORTER TIME ACCORDING TO HIS TEMPERANCE AND THE USE HE MADE OF HIS PROVISIONS
IN A FEW MINUTES AFTER A WARDER ANNOUNCED THAT THE PRIOR AYMER OF JORVAULX AND THE GOOD KNIGHT BRIAN DE BOIS-GUILBERT COMMANDER OF THE VALIANT ORDER OF KNIGHTS TEMPLARS WITH A SMALL RETINUE REQUESTED HOSPITALITY AND LODGING FOR THE NIGHT BEING ON THEIR WAY TO A TOURNAMENT WHICH WAS TO BE HELD NOT FAR FROM ASHBY-DE-LA-ZOUCHE

WELL SAID CHRISTIAN THIS IS FEARFUL
BUT I SPEEDILY SET FORWARD AGAIN AND TRAVELLED SEVEN DAYS AVOIDING THOSE PLACES WHICH SEEMED TO BE INHABITED AND LIVED FOR THE MOST PART UPON COCOANUTS WHICH SERVED ME BOTH FOR MEAT AND DRINK
BUT THE MONKEY LOOKING IN AT EVERY SIDE PUT ME INTO SUCH A FRIGHT THAT I WANTED PRESENCE OF MIND TO CONCEAL MYSELF UNDER THE BED AS I MIGHT EASILY HAVE DONE
AFTER HIM CAME THE HAUGHTY PRINCE OF ARRAGON AND SAYING LET ME HAVE WHAT I DESERVE--SURELY I DESERVE THE LADY HE CHOSE THE SILVER ONE AND FOUND INSIDE A FOOL'S HEAD

THEY THEREFORE WENT UP HERE WITH MUCH AGILITY AND SPEED THOUGH THE FOUNDATION UPON WHICH THE CITY WAS FRAMED WAS HIGHER THAN THE CLOUDS

AFTER SUCH A DISCOVERY I CAN TREAT YOU NO MORE AS A SLAVE BUT AS A BROTHER
AND BETTER HELP THAN THINE AND THY RANGERS WOULD I NEVER SEEK WERE IT AT MY UTMOST NEED SO SAYING HE MOUNTED HIS STRONG WAR-HORSE AND RODE OFF THROUGH THE FOREST

WE HUNTED AGAIN IN THE FINE FOREST I HAD THEN TRAVERSED WITH A GAY PARTY OF FRENCH NOBLES AND SPORTSMEN
FOR I SAW EVIDENTLY THAT IF WE HAD KEPT ON BOARD WE HAD BEEN ALL SAFE THAT IS TO SAY WE HAD ALL GOT SAFE ON SHORE AND I HAD NOT BEEN SO MISERABLE AS TO BE LEFT ENTIRELY DESTITUTE OF ALL COMFORT AND COMPANY AS I NOW WAS
WHILE I WAS THUS EMPLOYED THE ENEMY DISCHARGED SEVERAL THOUSAND ARROWS MANY OF WHICH STUCK IN MY HANDS AND FACE

I VENTURED TO UNSCREW ONE OF MY CHAIRS WHICH WERE ALWAYS FASTENED TO THE FLOOR
FOR FIRST MUST GIVE PLACE TO LAST BECAUSE LAST MUST HAVE HIS TIME TO COME
THEY MOUNTED THEIR HORSES WENT TO BEAT THE ROADS AGAIN AND TO ATTACK THE CARAVANS THEY MIGHT MEET

WE ARRIVED IN THE DOWNS ON THE 13TH OF APRIL 1702

THE NUMBER OF THEM BROKE ALL MY MEASURES
I HEARD A NOISE OVER MY HEAD LIKE THE CLAPPING OF WINGS AND THEN BEGAN TO PERCEIVE THE WOFUL CONDITION I WAS IN
THE STORM CONTINUED SEVERAL DAYS AND BROUGHT US BEFORE THE PORT OF AN ISLAND WHICH THE CAPTAIN WAS VERY UNWILLING TO ENTER
THEY CLOSED ROUND THE FIRE AND COMMENCED TO DRINK HOLDING CONSULTATION TOGETHER IN A STRANGE GIBBERISH WHICH HE COULD NOT ALTOGETHER UNDERSTAND
BUT AS SOON AS IT WAS DAY I BECKONED TO HIM TO COME WITH ME AND LET HIM KNOW I WOULD GIVE HIM SOME CLOTHES
HE FOUND BY THEIR EXAMPLE THAT THEIR HEADS WERE NOT SO GOOD AS THEIR HANDS ON SUCH OCCASIONS AND THEREFORE RESOLVED TO TAKE UPON HIMSELF THE IMPORTANT COMMISSION
THIS WAS ALL MY PROVISION
HERE I FOUND THAT THE SHIP WAS BULGED AND HAD A GREAT DEAL OF WATER IN HER HOLD BUT THAT SHE LAY SO ON THE SIDE OF A BANK OF HARD SAND OR RATHER EARTH THAT HER STERN LAY LIFTED UP UPON THE BANK AND HER HEAD LOW ALMOST TO THE WATER
FAR FROM LESSENING YOUR WEALTH I DESIGN TO AUGMENT IT AND WILL NOT LET YOU QUIT MY DOMINIONS WITHOUT MARKS OF MY LIBERALITY HE THEN CHARGED ONE OF HIS OFFICERS TO TAKE CARE OF ME AND ORDERED PEOPLE TO SERVE ME AT HIS OWN EXPENSE
TO WHICH HE REPLIED THEY ARE STURDY ROGUES THEY CHUSE RATHER TO BEAR ALL HARDSHIP THAN TO MAKE AWAY THEMSELVES
NOR COULD ANYTHING HAVE PRESERVED THE WINDOWS BUT THE STRONG LATTICE WIRES PLACED ON THE OUTSIDE AGAINST ACCIDENTS IN TRAVELLING
THE DECREE CAUSED SO MUCH DISCONTENT AMONG THE PEOPLE WHOSE AFFECTION ALADDIN HAD SECURED BY HIS LARGESSES AND CHARITIES THAT THE SULTAN FEARFUL OF AN INSURRECTION WAS OBLIGED TO GRANT HIM HIS LIFE
THEN SAID APOLLYON I AM SURE OF THEE NOW AND WITH THAT HE HAD ALMOST PRESSED HIM TO DEATH SO THAT CHRISTIAN BEGAN TO DESPAIR OF LIFE
I COULD GIVE MORE BUT THAT MY HAND LACKS MEANS ROSALIND AND CELIA WHEN THEY WERE ALONE BEGAN TO TALK ABOUT THE HANDSOME WRESTLER AND ROSALIND CONFESSED THAT SHE LOVED HIM AT FIRST SIGHT
NO ONE KNEW ANYTHING ABOUT HER
YET I SAW ABUNDANCE OF FOWLS BUT KNEW NOT THEIR KINDS
BUT WITHAL I TOOK CARE TO MAKE MY COURT REGULARLY TO THE MAHARAJA AND CONVERSED WITH THE GOVERNORS AND PETTY KINGS HIS TRIBUTARIES THAT WERE ABOUT HIM
BUT HIS ANTAGONIST AROSE NOT
SHE TOOK THE CHINA DISH WHICH SHE HAD SET DOWN AT THE FOOT OF THE THRONE UNTIED IT AND PRESENTED IT TO THE SULTAN
SEA-NYMPHS HOURLY RING HIS KNELL

HE STARTED UP ON HEARING IT AND TURNING TOWARDS GLOSSIN HE ADDRESSED HIM IN TONES OF PASSION AND INDIGNATION

TRULY SAID CHRISTIAN I DO NOT KNOW

AFTERWARDS I VISITED RUSSIA AND REMAINED THERE FOR ABOUT A YEAR
IN THIS EXERCISE I ONCE MET AN ACCIDENT WHICH HAD LIKE TO HAVE COST ME MY LIFE
AFTER HE WENT TO THE IRON GATE FOR THAT MUST BE OPENED TOO BUT THAT LOCK WENT DAMNABLE HARD YET THE KEY DID OPEN IT
AT LAST IT BROKE OUT INTO TEARS AND IN A LITTLE WHILE AFTER I RECOVERED MY SPEECH
WOULD TO GOD SHE THEN SAID HE WERE HERE SAFELY ARRIVED AND ABLE TO BEAR ARMS IN THE APPROACHING TOURNEY
BUT FOR MYSELF AND THE REST WHO WERE NOT SO IMPRUDENT THE PIRATES SAVED US AND CARRIED US INTO A REMOTE ISLAND WHERE THEY SOLD US
THE RESULT OF HIS CONSULTATION INFORMED HIM TO HIS GREAT JOY THAT THE LAMP WAS IN THE PALACE
I SOON EMPTIED THE HOGSHEAD OF THE BREAD AND WRAPPED IT UP PARCEL BY PARCEL IN PIECES OF THE SAILS WHICH I CUT OUT
ONE DAY AS ALADDIN WAS WALKING ABOUT THE TOWN HE HEARD AN ORDER PROCLAIMED COMMANDING THE PEOPLE TO SHUT UP THEIR SHOPS AND HOUSES AND KEEP WITHIN DOORS WHILE THE PRINCESS BUDDIR AL BUDDOOR THE SULTAN'S DAUGHTER WENT TO THE BATH AND RETURNED

I ANSWERED THAT WAS NEEDLESS AND WOULD TAKE UP TOO MUCH TIME

THIS DONE THEY SANG AS FOLLOWS
ALADDIN'S MOTHER EMBOLDENED BY THE SIGHT OF THESE RICH JEWELS AND FEARFUL LEST HER SON SHOULD BE GUILTY OF GREATER EXTRAVAGANCE COMPLIED WITH HIS REQUEST AND PROMISED TO GO EARLY IN THE NEXT MORNING TO THE PALACE OF THE SULTAN
HAVING GREETED HIM AND HIS FRIENDS WITH THE MOURNFUL CEREMONY SUITED TO THE OCCASION CEDRIC LED HIS KNIGHTLY GUEST TO ANOTHER APARTMENT WHERE HE WAS ABOUT TO LEAVE HIM WHEN THE BLACK KNIGHT TOOK HIS HAND
BUT THE THINGS THAT ARE NOT SEEN ARE ETERNAL
BUT OUR VOYAGE WAS OTHERWISE DETERMINED

AND BESIDES THEY SHOT ANOTHER FLIGHT INTO THE AIR AS WE DO BOMBS IN EUROPE WHEREOF MANY I SUPPOSE FELL ON MY BODY THOUGH I FELT THEM NOT AND SOME ON MY FACE WHICH I IMMEDIATELY COVERED WITH MY LEFT HAND
I WOULD THEREFORE SPEAK WITH THE MASTER OF THE HOUSE
THE CASKETS WERE OF GOLD SILVER AND LEAD
WRETCHED WOMAN WHO HAS DONE THIS EXCLAIMED BROWN
NOTWITHSTANDING MY FAINTING THE ILL-NATURED OLD FELLOW STILL KEPT HIS SEAT UPON MY NECK
AND SEPARATING US AS WELL FROM THE BOAT AS FROM ONE ANOTHER GAVE US NOT TIME HARDLY TO SAY O GOD FOR WE WERE ALL SWALLOWED UP IN A MOMENT
AND PRESENTLY STARTING UP I HEARD A MAN CALL ME BY THE NAME OF GOVERNOR
I WAS BUT LIGHTLY CLOTHED AND OF THIS I FELT THE INCONVENIENCE THE MORE I ADVANCED NORTHEAST
HERE I GAVE HIM BREAD AND A BUNCH OF RAISINS TO EAT AND A DRAUGHT OF WATER WHICH I FOUND HE WAS INDEED IN GREAT DISTRESS FOR FROM HIS RUNNING
THE ARMS AND THE BODY OF THE DECEASED KNIGHT ARE AT THE WILL OF THE VICTOR HIS FURTHER SPEECH WAS INTERRUPTED BY A CLATTERING OF HORSES FEET AND THE BLACK KNIGHT FOLLOWED BY A NUMEROUS BAND OF MEN AT-ARMS GALLOPED INTO THE LISTS
WHICH BY THIS METHOD INDEED I SO EFFECTUALLY SECURED THAT WHEN THESE LITTLE STAKES BEGAN TO GROW I HAD PLANTED THEM SO VERY THICK THAT I WAS FORCED TO PULL SOME OF THEM UP AGAIN
THEY ASSURED ME THAT EVERY NIGHT A NOISE OF DRUMS WAS HEARD THERE WHENCE THE MARINERS FANCIED THAT IT WAS THE RESIDENCE OF DEGIAL
NIGHT AND DARKNESS OVERTOOK ME
I CANNOT TELL HOW LONG I CONTINUED SO
HOW I LIKED THE VICTUALS HE GAVE ME
UPON THE ENTRANCE OF RICHARD THE SAXON AROSE GRAVELY TO BID HIM WELCOME

SHE WILL PRESENTLY RETURN FROM THE BATH

BUT IN THE MORNING I FELL ASLEEP
I FELL INTO THE HANDS OF A RICH MERCHANT WHO AS SOON AS HE BOUGHT ME TOOK ME TO HIS HOUSE TREATED ME WELL AND CLAD ME HANDSOMELY AS A SLAVE
AND THE CAUSE OF ALL THIS TROUBLE WAS A LITTLE INDIAN BOY WHOM TITANIA HAD TAKEN TO BE ONE OF HER FOLLOWERS
THIS PROCLAMATION INSPIRED ALADDIN WITH AN EAGER DESIRE TO SEE THE PRINCESS'S FACE WHICH HE DETERMINED TO GRATIFY BY PLACING HIMSELF BEHIND THE DOOR OF THE BATH SO THAT HE COULD NOT FAIL TO SEE HER FACE
THE CAPTAIN FINDING THAT THEIR DESIGN HAD PROVED ABORTIVE WENT DIRECTLY TO THE PLACE OF RENDEZVOUS AND TOLD HIS TROOP THAT THEY HAD LOST THEIR LABOR AND MUST RETURN TO THEIR CAVE
IT CANNOT BE THEN--IT CANNOT BE
WHEN THE MORNING OF THE TOURNAMENT ARRIVED THE FIELD OF CONTEST AT ASHBY-DE-LA-ZOUCHE PRESENTED A BRILLIANT AND ROMANTIC SCENE
THE FEATURES WHICH WERE EXPOSED WERE THOSE OF A YOUNG MAN OF TWENTY-FIVE
I STAYED WITH THEM TILL THEY HAD GATHERED THEIR QUANTITY OF PEPPER AND THEN SAILED WITH THEM TO THE ISLAND FROM WHENCE THEY HAD COME
BUT THERE WAS MORE WORK TO DO YET FOR I PERCEIVED THE SAVAGE WHOM I HAD KNOCKED DOWN WAS NOT KILLED BUT STUNNED WITH THE BLOW AND BEGAN TO COME TO HIMSELF
AND AS HE READ HE WEPT AND TREMBLED
BUT YOU HAD BETTER HEAR THE STORY IN YOUR OWN CHAMBER
IF I SHOULD NOT BE TROUBLESOME TO YOU DO ME THE FAVOR TO LET ME PASS THE NIGHT WITH YOU AND I SHALL BE VERY MUCH OBLIGED BY YOUR HOSPITALITY THOUGH ALI BABA HAD SEEN THE CAPTAIN OF THE ROBBERS IN THE FOREST AND HAD HEARD HIM SPEAK IT WAS IMPOSSIBLE TO KNOW HIM IN THE DISGUISE OF AN OIL MERCHANT
AND THROUGH THIS RIOTOUS CROWD RICHARD AND HIS FOLLOWERS WITH DIFFICULTY MADE THEIR WAY

I SHALL NEVER FORGET WITH WHAT UNWILLINGNESS GLUMDALCLITCH CONSENTED NOR THE STRICT CHARGE SHE GAVE THE PAGE TO BE CAREFUL OF ME BURSTING AT THE SAME TIME INTO A FLOOD OF TEARS AS IF SHE HAD SOME FOREBODING OF WHAT WAS TO HAPPEN
WE FOUND IT TO BE A PALACE ELEGANTLY BUILT AND VERY LOFTY WITH A GATE OF EBONY OF TWO LEAVES WHICH WE OPENED
I HAVE ALSO MADE A VOW NEVER TO LEAVE BAGDAD PERCEIVING THAT THE CALIPH INSISTED UPON MY COMPLIANCE I SUBMITTED AND TOLD HIM THAT I WAS WILLING TO OBEY
I HAVE GOOD REASON TO BELIEVE THAT HE TOOK ME FOR A YOUNG ONE OF HIS OWN SPECIES BY HIS OFTEN STROKING MY FACE VERY GENTLY WITH HIS OTHER PAW
THEN SHE COUNSELLED HIM THAT WHEN HE AROSE IN THE MORNING HE SHOULD BEAT THEM WITHOUT ANY MERCY
LIVED TO UNITE THYSELF WITH THE VILE TYRANT WHO SLEW THY NEAREST AND DEAREST I HATED HIM WITH ALL MY SOUL REPLIED ULRICA
THE ALARM HAD NOW SPREAD THROUGH THE COUNTRYSIDE THAT KENNEDY'S MURDERER HAD BEEN TAKEN ON THE VERY SPOT WHERE THE MURDER HAD BEEN COMMITTED YEARS BEFORE
BUT WE WERE OBLIGED TO CAST ANCHOR
BUT THE DANGER IS MUCH GREATER WHEN THE MINISTERS THEMSELVES ARE COMMANDED TO SHOW THEIR DEXTERITY
YOU WILL FIND IT WILL COME EASILY ALADDIN DID AS THE MAGICIAN BADE HIM RAISED THE STONE WITH EASE AND LAID IT ON ONE SIDE
HE HAD HEARD TOO ALL THE PERSONS OF REPUTE IN THE CITY TALKING OF A WOMAN CALLED FATIMA WHO WAS RETIRED FROM THE WORLD AND OF THE MIRACLES SHE WROUGHT
BUT HE BADE HER NOT TO BE AFRAID
IT WAS FURTHER INTIMATED TO HER THAT SHOULD SHE FAIL TO DO SO OR IF HER CHAMPION SHOULD BE DISCOMFITED SHE SHOULD DIE THE DEATH OF A SORCERESS ACCORDING TO DOOM
AND THIS WAS THE FIRST TIME I BEGAN TO CONCEIVE SOME IMPERFECT IDEA OF COURTS AND MINISTERS
AND THIS I THOUGHT SO JUST A REPROOF THAT I RESOLVED FOR THE FUTURE TO HAVE TWO OR THREE YEARS CORN BEFOREHAND
HE RETURNED TO THE PRINCESS'S APARTMENT AND WITHOUT MENTIONING A WORD OF WHAT HAD HAPPENED SAT DOWN AND COMPLAINED OF A GREAT PAIN WHICH HAD SUDDENLY SEIZED HIS HEAD
IN THIS ISLAND IS ALSO FOUND THE RHINOCEROS AN ANIMAL LESS THAN THE ELEPHANT BUT LARGER THAN THE BUFFALO
THIS BEING WITHIN ABOUT A MILE FROM THE SHORE WHERE I WAS AND THE SHIP SEEMING TO STAND UPRIGHT STILL I WISHED MYSELF ON BOARD THAT AT LEAST I MIGHT SAVE SOME NECESSARY THINGS FOR MY USE
BUT I COULD NOT SEE HOW THIS COULD BE DONE IN THEIR COUNTRY WHERE THE SMALLEST WHERRY WAS EQUAL TO A FIRST-RATE MAN-OF-WAR AMONG US
AS SOON AS I ENTERED THE CAVERN I LOST ALL LIGHT AND THE STREAM CARRIED ME I KNEW NOT WHITHER
PLEASANT AS THE SPRING COMFORTABLE AS THE SUMMER FRUITFUL AS AUTUMN DREADFUL AS WINTER
LASTLY THAT UPON HIS SOLEMN OATH TO OBSERVE ALL THE ABOVE ARTICLES THE SAID MAN-MOUNTAIN SHALL HAVE A DAILY ALLOWANCE OF MEAT AND DRINK SUFFICIENT FOR THE SUPPORT OF 1724 OF OUR SUBJECTS WITH FREE ACCESS TO OUR ROYAL PERSON AND OTHER MARKS OF OUR FAVOR
AND THROUGH THE SEVEN HOLES I CONTRIVED TO PLANT THE MUSKETS OF WHICH I TOOK NOTICE THAT I HAD GOT SEVEN ON SHORE OUT OF THE SHIP

GOD ORDERED IT OTHERWISE
SO HE SAID TO PUCK THESE TWO YOUNG MEN ARE GOING TO FIGHT
THEY PROCEEDED TO A HIGH MOUNTAIN AND WHEN THEY HAD REACHED THE PLACE OF THEIR DESTINATION THEY TOOK UP A LARGE STONE WHICH FORMED THE MOUTH OF A DEEP PIT AND LET DOWN THE BODY WITH ALL ITS APPAREL AND JEWELS
BUT HERE A RIVER OF FRESH WATER RUNS FROM THE SEA INTO A DARK CAVERN WHOSE ENTRANCE IS VERY HIGH AND SPACIOUS
ON THE 16TH DAY OF JUNE 1703 A BOY ON THE TOPMAST DISCOVERED LAND
THEY BEGAN WITH MANY COMPLIMENTS UPON MY VALOR AND GENEROSITY INVITED ME TO THAT KINGDOM IN THE EMPEROR THEIR MASTER'S NAME AND DESIRED ME TO SHOW THEM SOME PROOFS OF MY PRODIGIOUS STRENGTH OF WHICH THEY HAD HEARD SO MANY WONDERS
LET THERE BE ALSO KITCHENS AND STOREHOUSES STABLES FULL OF THE FINEST HORSES WITH THEIR EQUERRIES AND GROOMS AND HUNTING EQUIPAGE OFFICERS ATTENDANTS AND SLAVES BOTH MEN AND WOMEN TO FORM A RETINUE FOR THE PRINCESS AND MYSELF
WE MARCHED TILL WE CAME TO THE CAPITAL OF SERENDIB FOR IT WAS IN THAT ISLAND I HAD LANDED
THIS PALACE IS ONE OF THE WONDERS OF THE WORLD
WHEN THE TEMPLAR REACHED THE HALL OF THE CASTLE HE FOUND DE BRACY THERE ALREADY
WHICH WAS AGAIN LAID ACROSS WITH SMALLER STICKS INSTEAD OF LATHS AND THEN THATCHED OVER A GREAT THICKNESS WITH THE RICE-STRAW WHICH WAS STRONG LIKE REEDS
TO WHICH BABA MUSTAPHA REPLIED THAT AS HE DID NOT LIVE IN THAT NEIGHBORHOOD HE COULD NOT TELL
THERE ALSO YOU SHALL SERVE HIM CONTINUALLY WITH PRAISE WITH SHOUTING AND THANKSGIVING WHOM YOU DESIRED TO SERVE IN THE WORLD THOUGH WITH MUCH DIFFICULTY BECAUSE OF THE INFIRMITY OF YOUR FLESH
SHYLOCK'S GRIEF AND ANGER WERE TERRIBLE TO SEE

1ST
I MENTION THIS CEREMONY THE MORE PARTICULARLY BECAUSE I WAS IN A FEW WEEKS TIME TO BE THE PRINCIPAL ACTOR ON A SIMILAR OCCASION
THAT I HAD FLED FROM JUSTICE AND IF I DID NOT RETURN IN TWO HOURS I SHOULD BE DEPRIVED OF MY TITLE OF NARDAC AND DECLARED A TRAITOR
WE CAME UPON THEM INDEED IN THE DARK SO THAT THEY COULD NOT SEE OUR NUMBER
DURING WHICH TIME WE WERE DRIVEN A LITTLE TO THE EAST OF THE MOLUCCA ISLANDS AND ABOUT THREE DEGREES NORTHWARD OF THE LINE AS OUR CAPTAIN FOUND BY AN OBSERVATION HE TOOK THE 2D OF MAY AT WHICH TIME THE WIND CEASED AND IT WAS A PERFECT CALM WHEREAT I WAS NOT A LITTLE REJOICED
FOR I HAD HEARD THAT THE PEOPLE OF THE CARIBBEAN COAST WERE CANNIBALS OR MAN-EATERS AND I KNEW BY THE LATITUDE THAT I COULD NOT BE FAR FROM THAT SHORE
THE FARTHER I WAS FROM THE OCCASION OF MY FRIGHT THE GREATER MY APPREHENSIONS WERE WHICH IS SOMETHING CONTRARY TO THE NATURE OF SUCH THINGS AND ESPECIALLY TO THE USUAL PRACTICE OF ALL CREATURES IN FEAR
FOR WHAT WAS IT TO ME IF WHEN I HAD CHOSEN A VAST TREE IN THE WOODS AND WITH MUCH TROUBLE CUT IT DOWN IF I HAD BEEN ABLE WITH MY TOOLS TO HEW AND DUB THE OUTSIDE INTO THE PROPER SHAPE OF A BOAT AND BURN OR CUT OUT THE INSIDE TO MAKE IT HOLLOW SO AS TO MAKE A BOAT OF IT--IF AFTER ALL THIS I MUST LEAVE IT JUST THERE WHERE I FOUND IT AND NOT BE ABLE TO LAUNCH IT INTO THE WATER
APOLLYON COULD NOT CRUSH THEE NOR COULD ALL THAT THOU DIDST HEAR OR SEE OR FEEL IN THE VALLEY OF THE SHADOW OF DEATH
AND HIMSELF HIS MATE AND FIVE MORE WENT IN THE OTHER
MONARCH OF ALL MONARCHS TALLER THAN THE SONS OF MEN
THEN EACH MAN WILL HAVE THE LADY WHO LOVES HIM AND THEY WILL ALL THINK THAT THIS HAS BEEN ONLY A MIDSUMMER-NIGHT'S DREAM
I WENT DOWN UNDER THE TEMPLAR'S SWORD STUNNED INDEED BUT UNWOUNDED FOR THE BLADE STRUCK ME FLATLINGS BEING AVERTED BY THE GOOD MACE WITH WHICH I WARDED THE BLOW
BUT SOON THE CONFLICT BECAME EVEN MORE DESPERATE WHEN THE BLACK KNIGHT AT THE HEAD OF A BODY OF HIS FOLLOWERS LED AN ATTACK UPON THE OUTER BARRIER OF THE BARBICAN
ACCORDINGLY I GAVE THEM THE WHOLE HISTORY OF THE PLACE AND OF MY COMING TO IT
TALL AND WELL-SHAPED
AND THE MAGICIAN SAID THIS IS NOT WELL NEPHEW
I HAD NEVER HANDLED A TOOL IN MY LIFE
HE HAD HITHERTO FEARED FOR HIS DAUGHTER'S HONOUR
MY GOOD MASTER ANSWERED SHE GOD PRESERVE YOU AND ALL YOUR FAMILY
AND AS TRUTH ALWAYS FORCES ITS WAY INTO RATIONAL MINDS SO THIS HONEST WORTHY GENTLEMAN WHO HAD SOME TINCTURE OF LEARNING AND VERY GOOD SENSE WAS IMMEDIATELY CONVINCED OF MY CANDOR AND VERACITY
AND I BADE HIM GO AS WELL AS I COULD
HE DETERMINED TO LEAVE HIS ASSES TO SAVE HIMSELF
SOME OF GULLIVER'S ADVENTURES BY JONATHAN SWIFT JUSTLY MAY I SAY THAT I SHOULD HAVE LIVED HAPPY ENOUGH IN THE COUNTRY IF MY LITTLENESS HAD NOT EXPOSED ME TO SEVERAL RIDICULOUS AND TROUBLESOME ACCIDENTS
AT THE NOISE OF THE FIRE I IMMEDIATELY ADVANCED WITH MY WHOLE ARMY WHICH WAS NOW EIGHT MEN VIZ MYSELF GENERALISSIMO
THEY DREW NEAR TO A VERY MIRY SLOUGH THAT WAS IN THE MIDST OF THE PLAIN
THE SILVER ONE HAD THIS:--"WHO CHOOSETH ME SHALL GET AS MUCH AS HE DESERVES
I TOOK PART OF A SMALL HOUSE IN THE OLD JEWRY
THOSE ARE PEARLS THAT WERE HIS EYES NOTHING OF HIM THAT DOTH FADE BUT DOTH SUFFER A SEA-CHANGE INTO SOMETHING RICH AND STRANGE
I LEFT FIFTEEN HUNDRED POUNDS WITH MY WIFE AND FIXED HER IN A GOOD HOUSE AT REDRIFF
FOR THREE DAYS HE WANDERED ABOUT THE CITY EXCITING THE WONDER AND COMPASSION OF THE MULTITUDE BY ASKING EVERYBODY HE MET IF THEY HAD SEEN HIS PALACE OR COULD TELL HIM ANYTHING OF IT
THE BANK WAS HIGH AND RUGGED SO THAT I COULD SCARCELY HAVE GOT UP HAD IT NOT BEEN FOR SOME ROOTS OF TREES WHICH I FOUND WITHIN REACH
AND IT WAS REALLY IN ITS OWN NATURE MORE EASY FOR ME TO GUIDE IT OVER FORTY-FIVE MILES OF SEA THAN ABOUT FORTY-FIVE FATHOMS OF LAND WHERE IT LAY TO SET IT AFLOAT IN THE WATER
I GAVE THEM A DESCRIPTION OF THE WAY I MANAGED THE GOATS AND DIRECTIONS TO MILK AND FATTEN THEM AND TO MAKE BOTH BUTTER AND CHEESE
LET ITS MATERIALS BE MADE OF NOTHING LESS THAN PORPHYRY JASPER AGATE LAPIS-LAZULI AND THE FINEST MARBLE
THEY SPOKE TO ME BUT I DID NOT UNDERSTAND THEIR LANGUAGE
I KNOW WHAT I AM ASKING AND I KNOW IT HAS BEEN THE WILL OF GOD TO PRESERVE YOU IN STRANGE DANGERS AND THAT I SHALL BE THE MEANS TO SET YOU IN YOUR FATHER'S SEAT AGAIN
THESE MEN ASKED THE PILGRIMS WHENCE THEY CAME
THE SHERIFF OF THE COUNTY ARRIVED NEXT MORNING AND OPENED AN INQUIRY
IN THIS MEADOW THEY LAY DOWN AND SLEPT FOR HERE THEY MIGHT LIE DOWN SAFELY WHEN THEY AWOKE THEY GATHERED AGAIN OF THE FRUIT OF THE TREES AND DRANK AGAIN OF THE WATER OF THE RIVER AND THEN LAY DOWN AGAIN TO SLEEP
I CRIED OUT IN AGONY BEAT MY HEAD AND BREAST AND THREW MYSELF UPON THE GROUND WHERE I LAY SOME TIME IN DESPAIR
IT WAS PLAIN TOO THAT HE HAD SOME OTHER MOTIVE FOR APPREHENDING HIM THAN MERELY THE DESIRE TO DO HIS DUTY AS A MAGISTRATE OF THE COUNTY WHICH HE HAD NOW BECOME
COOKS AND MENDICANTS STROLLING SOLDIERS FROM PALESTINE PEDLARS MECHANICS WANDERING PALMERS HEDGE-PRIESTS SAXON MINSTRELS AND WELSH BARDS TOGETHER WITH JESTERS AND JUGGLERS FORMED A MOTLEY AND HUNGRY GATHERING SUCH AS COULD ONLY BE SEEN ON THE OCCASION WHICH NOW BROUGHT THEM TOGETHER
THEY KNEW BESIDES THAT THE OUTLAWS WERE CHIEFLY PEASANTS AND YEOMEN OF SAXON DESCENT AND WERE GENERALLY SUPPOSED TO RESPECT THE PERSONS AND PROPERTY OF THEIR COUNTRYMEN

WHAT WAS TO BE DONE IN THIS HORRIBLE DILEMMA
ON EACH SIDE OF THE GATE WAS A SMALL WINDOW NOT ABOVE SIX INCHES FROM THE GROUND
FLIMNAP THE TREASURER IS ALLOWED TO CUT A CAPER ON THE STRAIT ROPE AT LEAST AN INCH HIGHER THAN ANY OTHER LORD IN THE WHOLE EMPIRE
COME COME SAID CELIA WRESTLE WITH THY AFFECTIONS OH ANSWERED ROSALIND THEY TAKE THE PART OF A BETTER WRESTLER THAN MYSELF
IT WAS SEVERAL HOURS AFTER FRIDAY CAME BACK TO ME BEFORE THEY CAME BACK TO THEIR BOAT
ISAAC I WOULD I HAD KNOWN OF THIS
HER EYES WERE LARGE LIVELY AND SPARKLING
AND THE TIDE BEING UP THE CAPTAIN HAD BROUGHT THE PINNACE IN NEAR THE PLACE WHERE I HAD FIRST LANDED MY RAFTS AND SO LANDED JUST AT MY DOOR
DIRECTLY HE SAW THE WONDERFUL FABRIC HE KNEW THAT NONE BUT THE GENIES THE SLAVES OF THE LAMP COULD HAVE PERFORMED SUCH WONDERS
AND WRAPPING ALL THIS IN A PIECE OF CANVAS I BEGAN TO THINK OF MAKING ANOTHER RAFT
I COULD ONLY LOOK UPWARDS THE SUN BEGAN TO GROW HOT AND THE LIGHT OFFENDED MY EYES
THE FARMER HAVING AS I SUPPOSE BY THEIR TALK RECEIVED SUCH AN ACCOUNT OF ME AS HIS SERVANT COULD GIVE HIM TOOK A PIECE OF A SMALL STRAW ABOUT THE SIZE OF A WALKING-STAFF AND THEREWITH LIFTED UP THE LAPPETS OF MY COAT WHICH IT SEEMS HE THOUGHT TO BE SOME KIND OF COVERING THAT NATURE HAD GIVEN ME
FOR THE NEGROES HAVING KILLED AND EATEN MY COMPANIONS SEEING ME TO BE WITHERED LEAN AND SICK DEFERRED MY DEATH
AS SOON AS I FOUND WATER ENOUGH--FOR MY RAFT DREW ABOUT A FOOT OF WATER--I THRUST HER UPON THAT FLAT PIECE OF GROUND AND THERE FASTENED OR MOORED HER BY STICKING MY TWO BROKEN OARS INTO THE GROUND ONE ON ONE SIDE NEAR ONE END AND ONE ON THE OTHER SIDE NEAR THE OTHER END
MY NAME IS ORLANDO AND I AM THE YOUNGEST SON OF SIR ROWLAND DE BOYS SAID THE YOUNG MAN
IT HAPPENED ONE DAY ABOUT NOON GOING TOWARDS MY BOAT I WAS EXCEEDINGLY SURPRISED WITH THE PRINT OF A MAN'S NAKED FOOT ON THE SHORE WHICH WAS VERY PLAIN TO BE SEEN ON THE SAND
AND THE IDEA AT ONCE OCCURRED TO HIM THAT HE WOULD BUY THE PROPERTY HIMSELF AND BY DOING SO HELP THE LAIRD
THE KNIGHT BENT LOW AND KISSED THE HAND OF THE LOVELY SOVEREIGN BY WHOM HIS VALOUR HAD BEEN REWARDED
WHEN THE TROOP WAS ALL GOT TOGETHER THE CAPTAIN TOLD THEM THE REASON OF THEIR RETURNING
I ANSWERED THAT I WAS NO MECHANIC BUT A MERCHANT AND THAT THE PIRATES WHO SOLD ME HAD ROBBED ME OF ALL I POSSESSED
BUT THE SMUGGLER KNEW NOTHING OF HIM FROM THE TIME HE WENT THERE
AND IN ALL ABOUT FIVE OR SIX GALLONS OF RACK
BUT GIVE ME LEAVE TO SIT OPPOSITE TO IT THAT ALTHOUGH I SEE NOT THE MASTER OF A FAMILY SO DEAR TO ME I MAY AT LEAST BEHOLD THE PLACE WHERE HE USED TO SIT WHEN THE MAGICIAN HAD MADE CHOICE OF A PLACE AND SAT DOWN HE BEGAN TO ENTER INTO DISCOURSE WITH ALADDIN'S MOTHER
NOR DID HE FORGET TO TAKE WITH HIM THE WONDERFUL LAMP TO WHICH HE OWED ALL HIS GOOD-FORTUNE NOR TO WEAR THE RING WHICH WAS GIVEN HIM AS A TALISMAN
ALI BABA DID NOT WAIT FOR HIS SISTER-IN-LAW TO DESIRE HIM TO GO TO SEE WHAT WAS BECOME OF CASSIM BUT DEPARTED IMMEDIATELY WITH HIS THREE ASSES BEGGING OF HER FIRST TO MODERATE HER AFFLICTION
GUY MANNERING RETOLD BY SIR EDWARD SULLIVAN THE CASTLE OF ELLANGOWAN WAS AN OLD AND MASSIVE STRUCTURE SITUATED BY THE SEASHORE IN THE SOUTHWESTERN PART OF SCOTLAND
AND AS FOR THE CAPTAIN HE COULD NOT CARRY THEM TO ENGLAND OTHER THAN AS PRISONERS IN IRONS TO BE TRIED FOR MUTINY AND RUNNING AWAY WITH THE SHIP
I WAS IN A TERRIBLE FRIGHT AND KEPT AS FAR AS I COULD FROM THE EDGE FOR FEAR OF FALLING
BUT I MIGHT NOW RATHER CALL IT A WALL FOR I RAISED A KIND OF WALL UP AGAINST IT OF TURFS ABOUT TWO FEET THICK ON THE OUTSIDE
BEFORE LONG THE INMATES OF THE CASTLE HAD OTHER THINGS TO OCCUPY THEM
AND LATE AT NIGHT HE ARRIVED AT GODFREY BERTRAM'S HOUSE WHERE HE WAS HOSPITABLY WELCOMED BY THE OWNER
BY THE NEXT NIGHT THEY HAD EATEN ALL THE PROVISIONS THE GENIE HAD BROUGHT
IT DEPRIVES THEM OF THE USE OF THOSE MEANS WHICH REASON OFFERS FOR THEIR RELIEF
GIVE HIM THIS SCROLL AND HE WILL GIVE THEE EVERYTHING THAT CAN FURNISH THEE FORTH FOR THE TOURNAMENT
I REPROACHED MYSELF WITH MY LAZINESS THAT WOULD NOT SOW ANY MORE CORN ONE YEAR THAN WOULD JUST SERVE ME TILL THE NEXT SEASON AS IF NO ACCIDENT COULD INTERVENE TO PREVENT MY ENJOYING THE CROP THAT WAS UPON THE GROUND
AND IF I HAD IT WOULD HAVE BEEN IN VAIN WITH SUCH A VOICE AS MINE AT SO GREAT A DISTANCE AS FROM THE ROOM WHERE I LAY TO THE KITCHEN WHERE THE FAMILY KEPT
AFTER I HAD DRUNK IT I SAT DOWN UPON THE GROUND
WHEN THE SUN AROSE I WAS VERY FEEBLE
WHEN THE STONE WAS PULLED UP THERE APPEARED A STAIRCASE ABOUT THREE OR FOUR FEET DEEP LEADING TO A DOOR
BUT THIS LAST WAS SO HEAVY I COULD NOT HOIST IT UP TO GET IT OVER THE SHIP'S SIDE
WHICH THE CHIEF OFFICER PERCEIVING TOLD HER IT WAS AN EASY MATTER TO BRING HER TO HER IF SHE DESIRED AND COMMANDED IT
PASSION OF THE MEN OF THIS WORLD
I TOLD THEM I THOUGHT THEY HAD MADE A RIGHT CHOICE
ABOUT TWO OR THREE DAYS BEFORE I WAS SET AT LIBERTY AS I WAS ENTERTAINING THE COURT WITH THIS KIND OF FEATS THERE ARRIVED AN EXPRESS TO INFORM HIS MAJESTY THAT SOME OF HIS SUBJECTS RIDING NEAR THE PLACE WHERE I WAS FIRST TAKEN UP HAD SEEN A GREAT BLACK SUBSTANCE LYING ON THE GROUND VERY ODDLY SHAPED EXTENDING ITS EDGES ROUND AS WIDE AS HIS MAJESTY'S BED-CHAMBER AND RISING UP IN THE MIDDLE AS HIGH AS A MAN
THREE OR FOUR DAYS AFTER OUR DEPARTURE WE WERE ATTACKED BY PIRATES WHO EASILY SEIZED UPON OUR SHIP BECAUSE IT WAS NOT A VESSEL OF WAR
ALADDIN GOT UP TREMBLING AND WITH TEARS IN HIS EYES SAID TO THE MAGICIAN
AND THE TIDE FAVORING ME I ADVANCED SO FAR THAT I COULD JUST HOLD UP MY CHIN AND FEEL THE GROUND
NO ONE HAD EVEN RECEIVED A LETTER FROM HIM
SO HE CALLED FOR THE MASTER OF THE HOUSE WHO AFTER A LITTLE TIME CAME TO CHRISTIAN AND ASKED HIM WHAT HE WOULD HAVE
BUT HIS FATHER SNATCHED ME FROM HIM AND AT THE SAME TIME GAVE HIM SUCH A BOX ON THE LEFT EAR AS WOULD HAVE FELLED AN EUROPEAN TROOP OF HORSE TO THE EARTH ORDERING HIM TO BE TAKEN FROM THE TABLE
I SPIT AT THEE AND I DEFY THEE
A LITTLE TIME AFTER THIS AUDIENCE I SOLICITED LEAVE TO DEPART AND WITH MUCH DIFFICULTY OBTAINED IT
THE BLEFUSCUDIANS WHO HAD NOT THE LEAST IMAGINATION OF WHAT I INTENDED WERE AT FIRST CONFOUNDED WITH ASTONISHMENT
I AFTERWARD WENT TO A SMITH WHO MADE ME A BIT ACCORDING TO THE PATTERN I SHOWED HIM AND ALSO SOME STIRRUPS
THE JEWESS INSTANTLY REMEMBERED THE SLIP OF PAPER WHICH SHE CONTINUED TO HOLD IN HER HAND AND LOOKING AT IT WITHOUT BEING OBSERVED SHE READ THE WORDS DEMAND A CHAMPION REBECCA SAID THE GRAND MASTER WHO BELIEVED THE WORDS OF BOIS GUILBERT HAD REFERENCE TO SOME OTHER WRITING HAST THOU AUGHT ELSE TO SAY THERE IS YET ONE CHANCE OF LIFE LEFT TO ME SAID THE JEWESS EVEN BY YOUR OWN FIERCE LAWS
I TOOK ALL POSSIBLE METHODS TO CULTIVATE THIS FAVORABLE DISPOSITION
THE NAME OF THE ELDEST WAS PASSION AND THE NAME OF THE OTHER PATIENCE
NOW BROWN WHEN HE FOUND THAT JULIA MANNERING HAD GONE TO WOODBOURNE DETERMINED TO FOLLOW HER WITH THE PURPOSE OF RESUMING HIS ADDRESSES AND HE ACCORDINGLY SET OUT ON FOOT TOWARDS THE NORTH
CEDRIC AND ATHELSTANE WERE CONFINED IN ONE APARTMENT THE LADY ROWENA IN ANOTHER WHILE THE POOR JEW WAS HASTILY THRUST INTO A DUNGEON-VAULT THE FLOOR OF WHICH WAS DEEP BENEATH THE LEVEL OF THE GROUND AND HIS DAUGHTER REBECCA WAS LOCKED INTO A CELL IN A DISTANT AND SEQUESTERED TURRET
AND NO SOONER WERE THEY ALONE THAN THEIR BED WAS REMOVED IN THE SAME MYSTERIOUS MANNER AS ON THE PRECEDING EVENING
THE SECOND VOYAGE I DESIGNED AFTER MY FIRST VOYAGE TO SPEND THE REST OF MY DAYS AT BAGDAD BUT IT WAS NOT LONG ERE I GREW WEARY OF AN INDOLENT LIFE AND I PUT TO SEA A SECOND TIME WITH MERCHANTS OF KNOWN PROBITY
WHERE SAID SHE CAN HE GET SO MANY LARGE GOLD TRAYS AND SUCH PRECIOUS STONES TO FILL THEM
SHALL WE BE RULED BY THE GIANT
HE HAS WISHED TO SURPRISE US AND LET US SEE WHAT WONDERS CAN BE DONE IN ONLY ONE NIGHT ALADDIN ON HIS BEING CONVEYED BY THE GENIE TO HIS OWN HOME REQUESTED HIS MOTHER TO GO TO THE PRINCESS BUDDIR AL BUDDOOR AND TELL HER THAT THE PALACE WOULD BE READY FOR HER RECEPTION IN THE EVENING
THEY DESERVE YOUR ATTENTION EVEN MORE THAN THOSE OF THE FIRST UPON WHICH EVERY ONE HELD HIS PEACE AND SINDBAD PROCEEDED
AND OBSERVING LIKEWISE THAT THE NUMBER OF MY ENEMIES INCREASED I GAVE TOKENS TO LET THEM KNOW THAT THEY MIGHT DO WITH ME WHAT THEY PLEASED
A FOURTH COMBAT FOLLOWED
MEANWHILE I HAD MUCH LIBERTY SO THAT SCARCELY ANY NOTICE WAS TAKEN OF WHAT I DID AND THIS GAVE ME AN OPPORTUNITY ONE DAY TO GET AT A DISTANCE FROM THE HOUSES AND TO MAKE MY ESCAPE
AND BEHOLD AT THE DOOR STOOD A GREAT COMPANY OF MEN AS DESIROUS TO GO IN BUT DURST NOT
HE WAS NO DOUBT DOING AS THE LAW DIRECTED HIM BUT AS FAR AS CONCERNED THE INHABITANTS OF DERNCLEUGH HE WAS ACTING WITH GREAT HARSHNESS FOR MEG MERRILIES HAD ALL ALONG SHOWN A STRONG AFFECTION FOR HIS BOY LITTLE HARRY BERTRAM
SOMETIMES I WENT OUT IN HER TO DIVERT MYSELF BUT NO MORE HAZARDOUS VOYAGES WOULD I GO SCARCELY EVER ABOVE A STONE'S CAST OR TWO FROM THE SHORE I WAS SO APPREHENSIVE OF BEING HURRIED OUT OF MY KNOWLEDGE AGAIN BY THE CURRENTS OR WINDS OR ANY OTHER ACCIDENT
AND INTO WHICH THE SERVANT WHO USED TO CARRY ME ON HORSEBACK WOULD PUT A LEATHERN BELT AND BUCKLE IT ABOUT HIS WAIST
AFTER I HAD SATISFIED HIM HE ORDERED THAT I SHOULD WANT FOR NOTHING
FROM THE ISLE OF SALABAT WE WENT TO ANOTHER WHERE I FURNISHED MYSELF WITH CLOVES CINNAMON AND OTHER SPICES
NOW WHEN NIGHT WAS COME AND WHEN MRS DIFFIDENCE AND HER HUSBAND THE GIANT WERE GOT TO BED THEY BEGAN TO RENEW THEIR DISCOURSE OF THEIR PRISONERS
THEY CONTINUED THEIR JOURNEY AT GREAT SPEED
FOR MY OWN PART I SWAM AS FORTUNE DIRECTED ME AND WAS PUSHED FORWARD BY WIND AND TIDE
AND THE PRINCESS ON HER SIDE AFFORDED SIMILAR TESTIMONIES OF HER EXTREME PLEASURE
NOW WHILE I WAS GAZING UPON ALL THESE THINGS I TURNED MY HEAD TO LOOK BACK AND SAW IGNORANCE COME UP TO THE RIVER-SIDE
THEY WERE TO RETURN HOME ON THE MORROW AND HAD I BEEN ONE DAY LATER I MUST HAVE PERISHED BECAUSE THE INHABITED PART OF THE ISLAND WAS A GREAT DISTANCE OFF AND IT WOULD HAVE BEEN IMPOSSIBLE FOR ME TO HAVE REACHED IT WITHOUT A GUIDE
AND ALL THE REST BEGGED OF HIM FOR GOD'S SAKE THAT THEY MIGHT NOT BE SENT TO ENGLAND
MERE OUTWARD SHOW HE SAID IS TO BE DESPISED
NO REPLIED MEG MERRILIES
SOMETIMES SHE PRESENTED THE PONIARD TO ONE BREAST SOMETIMES TO ANOTHER AND OFTENTIMES SEEMED TO STRIKE HER OWN
BUT A SLAVE HAVING OPENED THE DOOR ALI BABA'S SON TOOK HIM OBLIGINGLY BY THE HAND AND IN A MANNER FORCED HIM IN
I BELIEVED HIM REALLY TO STAND IN NEED OF MY ASSISTANCE TOOK HIM UPON MY BACK AND HAVING CARRIED HIM OVER BADE HIM GET DOWN AND FOR THAT END STOOPED THAT HE MIGHT GET OFF WITH EASE
RIDING STRAIGHT UP TO BRIAN DE BOIS-GUILBERT HE STRUCK WITH THE SHARP END OF HIS SPEAR THE SHIELD OF THE VICTORIOUS NORMAN UNTIL IT RANG AGAIN
BABA MUSTAPHA SAID SHE YOU MUST MAKE HASTE AND SEW THE PARTS OF THIS BODY TOGETHER
I THEN FASTENED MY HANDKERCHIEF TO A STICK I USUALLY CARRIED AND THRUSTING IT UP THE HOLE WAVED IT SEVERAL TIMES IN THE AIR THAT IF ANY BOAT OR SHIP WAS NEAR THE SEAMEN MIGHT CONJECTURE SOME UNHAPPY MORTAL TO BE SHUT UP IN THE BOX
AND BEING EXCESSIVELY FATIGUED I FELL FAST ASLEEP AND SLEPT AS COMFORTABLY AS I BELIEVE FEW COULD HAVE DONE IN MY CONDITION AND FOUND MYSELF MORE REFRESHED WITH IT THAN I THINK I EVER WAS ON SUCH AN OCCASION
HIS UPPER LIP HUNG DOWN UPON HIS BREAST
IT WAS THEREFORE LIKELY TO BE DISPOSED OF VERY CHEAP AS NO ONE KNEW FOR CERTAIN THAT YOUNG BERTRAM WAS DEAD
THEN SAID HOPEFUL THAT'S GOOD NEWS
HOWEVER WHEN THE TIDE WAS OUT I GOT MOST OF THE PIECES OF THE CABLE ASHORE AND SOME OF THE IRON THOUGH WITH INFINITE LABOR
ALI BABA DID SO AND SEEING A MAN STARTED BACK IN ALARM AND CRIED OUT
WELL ON SATURDAY ABOUT MIDNIGHT THEY BEGAN TO PRAY AND CONTINUED IN PRAYER TILL ALMOST BREAK OF DAY
BUT THE THING WAS HUSHED UP AND NEVER KNOWN AT COURT FOR THE GIRL WAS AFRAID OF THE QUEEN'S ANGER
GOVERNOR AND PRESENTLY I KNEW THE CAPTAIN'S VOICE
REMEMBER TOO THAT HE WOULD EAT NO SALT WITH YOU
THEN SUDDENLY ALL HIS HAPPINESS WAS DASHED WITH SORROW FOR MESSENGERS CAME FROM VENICE TO TELL HIM THAT ANTONIO WAS RUINED AND THAT SHYLOCK DEMANDED FROM THE DUKE OF VENICE THE FULFILMENT OF THE BOND UNDER WHICH HE WAS ENTITLED TO A POUND OF THE MERCHANT'S FLESH
OUR STRENGTH WAS NOW THUS ORDERED FOR THE EXPEDITION
A LARGE BAGFUL OF SMALL SHOT AND A GREAT ROLL OF SHEET LEAD
I COMMUNICATED TO HIS MAJESTY A PROJECT I HAD FORMED OF SEIZING THE ENEMY'S WHOLE FLEET
THESE THREADS ARE PROPOSED AS PRIZES FOR THOSE PERSONS WHOM THE EMPEROR HATH A MIND TO DISTINGUISH BY A PECULIAR MARK OF HIS FAVOR
AS THE HOUR APPROACHED WHICH WAS TO DETERMINE THE FATE OF THE UNFORTUNATE JEWESS A VAST MULTITUDE HAD GATHERED TO WITNESS A SPECTACLE EVEN IN THAT AGE BUT SELDOM SEEN
AND AFTER HAVING PUT ONE OF HIS MEN INTO EACH WITH THE WEAPONS WHICH HE THOUGHT FIT LEAVING OPEN THE SEAM WHICH HAD BEEN UNDONE TO LEAVE THEM ROOM TO BREATHE HE RUBBED THE JARS ON THE OUTSIDE WITH OIL FROM THE FULL VESSEL
REVENGE HENCEFORTH SHALL POSSESS ME WHOLLY AND THOU THYSELF SHALT SAY THAT WHATEVER WAS THE LIFE OF ULRICA HER DEATH WELL BECAME THE DAUGHTER OF THE NOBLE TORQUIL
WE HOLD OUR BREATHS AS HE RIDES FULL-TILT AT THE NORMAN KNIGHT AND STRIKES HIM FULL ON THE VISOR OF HIS HELMET THROWING HORSE AND RIDER TO THE GROUND
THEY ALSO ASKED THEM WHERE THEY HAD LODGED WHAT DIFFICULTIES AND DANGERS WHAT COMFORTS AND PLEASURES THEY HAD MET IN THE WAY
IF YOU LAY DOWN YOUR ARMS IMMEDIATELY AND SUBMIT YOU SHALL HAVE YOUR LIVES ALL BUT WILL ATKINS UPON THIS WILL ATKINS CRIED OUT FOR GOD'S SAKE CAPTAIN GIVE ME QUARTER
BOTH I AND THE OTHER SLAVES OF THE RING ALADDIN AGREEABLY SURPRISED AT AN OFFER OF HELP SO LITTLE EXPECTED REPLIED GENIE SHOW ME WHERE THE PALACE I CAUSED TO BE BUILT NOW STANDS OR TRANSPORT IT BACK WHERE IT FIRST STOOD YOUR COMMAND ANSWERED THE GENIE IS NOT WHOLLY IN MY POWER
GOD HATH DENIED ME REPENTANCE
THE NEGROES PRESENTED ME TO THEIR KING
YEA AND TO PARDON ALSO WHAT I DID AS TO MY COMPLIANCE WITH THEE
HOWEVER THOUGH I COULD HAVE NO IDEA OF KILLING SUCH AN ANIMAL WITH THAT WEAK KIND OF AMMUNITION YET I HAD SOME HOPES OF FRIGHTENING HIM BY THE REPORT AND PERHAPS OF WOUNDING HIM ALSO
THEN APOLLYON STRADDLED QUITE OVER THE WHOLE BREADTH OF THE WAY AND SAID I AM VOID OF FEAR IN THIS MATTER
NOT LONG AFTER THE GRACE-CUP WAS SERVED ROUND AND THE GUESTS AFTER MAKING DEEP OBEISANCE TO THEIR LANDLORD AND THE LADY ROWENA AROSE AND RETIRED WITH THEIR ATTENDANTS FOR THE NIGHT
WHEN I CAME TO MY OWN HOUSE FOR WHICH I WAS FORCED TO INQUIRE ONE OF MY SERVANTS OPENING THE DOOR I BENT DOWN TO GO IN LIKE A GOOSE UNDER A GATE FOR FEAR OF STRIKING MY HEAD
ANOTHER PAUSE SUCCEEDED

IF YE SHOULD CHANCE TO BE HARD BESTEAD IN ANY FOREST BETWEEN TRENT AND TEES WIND THREE NOTES UPON IT AND YE SHALL FIND HELPERS AND RESCUE GRAMERCY FOR THE GIFT BOLD YEOMAN SAID THE KNIGHT
THE SHIP LAY VERY BROAD OFF SO WE THOUGHT IT BETTER SPOONING BEFORE THE SEA THAN TRYING OR HULLING
THE WEATHER HAD NOW CLEARED
I WAS OBLIGED TO CARRY HER BACK TO THE HOUSE ON MY HORSE WHERE REST FEEDING AND GREAT CARE SOON RESTORED HER TO HEALTH
I MIGHT CALL HIM SHE SAID A THING DIVINE FOR NOTHING NATURAL I EVER SAW SO NOBLE AND FERDINAND BEHOLDING HER BEAUTY WITH WONDER AND DELIGHT EXCLAIMED MOST SURE THE GODDESS ON WHOM THESE AIRS ATTEND NOR DID HE ATTEMPT TO HIDE THE PASSION WHICH SHE INSPIRED IN HIM FOR SCARCELY HAD THEY EXCHANGED HALF A DOZEN SENTENCES BEFORE HE VOWED TO MAKE HER HIS QUEEN IF SHE WERE WILLING
AND I DO NOT WONDER NOW AT THAT CUSTOM WHEN A MALEFACTOR WHO HAS THE HALTER ABOUT HIS NECK IS TIED UP AND JUST GOING TO BE TURNED OFF AND HAS A REPRIEVE BROUGHT TO HIM--I SAY I DO NOT WONDER THAT THEY BRING A SURGEON WITH IT TO LET HIM BLEED THAT VERY MOMENT THEY TELL HIM OF IT THAT THE SURPRISE MAY NOT DRIVE THE ANIMAL SPIRITS FROM THE HEART AND OVERWHELM HIM FOR SUDDEN JOYS LIKE GRIEFS CONFOUND AT FIRST
