ON WHICH THE SULTANESS ENJOINED ON HER THE NECESSITY OF SILENCE AND DISCRETION AS NO ONE WOULD GIVE CREDENCE TO SO STRANGE A TALE
GLUMDALCLITCH HAD LOCKED ME UP IN HER CLOSET WHILE SHE WENT SOMEWHERE UPON BUSINESS OR A VISIT
I CANNOT MAKE THE CHOICE BECAUSE I HAVE NOT THE MEANS OF SATISFYING YOUR EXORBITANT DEMAND SEIZE HIM AND STRIP HIM SLAVES SAID THE KNIGHT AND LET THE FATHERS OF HIS RACE ASSIST HIM IF THEY CAN THE ASSISTANTS STEPPED FORWARD AND LAYING HANDS ON THE UNFORTUNATE MAN WAITED THE HARDHEARTED BARON'S FURTHER SIGNAL
I WILL MANACLE YOUR NECK AND FEET TOGETHER AND YOU SHALL FEED ON FRESH WATER MUSSELS WITHERED ROOTS AND HUSK AND HAVE SEA-WATER TO DRINK
WHEN THIS SHOWER OF ARROWS WAS OVER I FELL A-GROANING WITH GRIEF AND PAIN AND THEN STRIVING AGAIN TO GET LOOSE THEY DISCHARGED ANOTHER VOLLEY LARGER THAN THE FIRST AND SOME OF THEM ATTEMPTED WITH SPEARS TO STICK ME IN THE SIDES
IN OUR VOYAGE WE TOUCHED AT SEVERAL ISLANDS WHERE WE SOLD OR EXCHANGED OUR GOODS
THEY HEARD ME AND SENT A BOAT TO BRING ME ON BOARD
IF YOU SHOULD EVER HAVE ANY STORY OF YOUR OWN TO TELL AND WANT TO TELL IT WELL I ADVISE YOU TO TAKE ROBINSON CRUSOE FOR A MODEL PARENTS AND TEACHERS WHO DO NOT READ ALOUD TO YOUNG CHILDREN OR WHO DO NOT PRACTISE TELLING STORIES TO CHILDREN PROBABLY DO NOT REALIZE WHAT SIMPLE BUT EXTRAORDINARILY VALUABLE OPPORTUNITIES FOR SELF-EDUCATION THEY ARE IGNORING TO SAY NOTHING OF THE HELP THEY CAN BE TO CHILDREN
BUT TO RETURN TO THE ASSAULT
THE PRINCESS WHO HAD LONG HEARD OF THIS HOLY WOMAN BUT HAD NEVER SEEN HER WAS VERY DESIROUS TO HAVE SOME CONVERSATION WITH HER
THEY HALLOOED AGAIN AND CALLED THEIR TWO COMRADES BY THEIR NAMES A GREAT MANY TIMES
AND HORSE AND MAN WENT HEAVILY TO THE GROUND
HE QUICKLY LAID AS MANY BAGS OF GOLD AS HE COULD CARRY AT THE DOOR OF THE CAVERN
THE SUFFERER WAS IVANHOE HIMSELF WHO HAD SO MYSTERIOUSLY DISAPPEARED ON THE CONCLUSION OF THE TOURNAMENT WHEN HIS FATHER CEDRIC HAD SENT HIS SERVANTS TO ATTEND HIM TO A PLACE OF SAFETY
PRESIDENT EMERITUS OF HARVARD UNIVERSITY WITH A READING GUIDE BY WILLIAM ALLAN NEILSON PH.D
ON HIS SON-IN-LAW BEING BROUGHT BEFORE HIM HE WOULD NOT HEAR A WORD FROM HIM BUT ORDERED HIM TO BE PUT TO DEATH
ALADDIN DID NOT CONFINE HIMSELF IN HIS PALACE BUT WENT WITH MUCH STATE SOMETIMES TO ONE MOSQUE AND SOMETIMES TO ANOTHER TO PRAYERS OR TO VISIT THE GRAND VIZIER OR THE PRINCIPAL LORDS OF THE COURT
AND SINCE HIS DEATH NOTWITHSTANDING ALL I CAN SAY TO HIM HE DOES NOTHING BUT IDLE AWAY HIS TIME IN THE STREETS AS YOU SAW HIM WITHOUT CONSIDERING HE IS NO LONGER A CHILD
BROWN THOUGH A SOLDIER AND A BRAVE ONE WAS TERRIFIED AS HE LAY IN HIS HIDING-PLACE
NOW NIGHT BEING COME AGAIN AND THE GIANT AND HIS WIFE BEING IN BED SHE ASKED HIM CONCERNING THE PRISONERS AND IF THEY HAD TAKEN HIS COUNSEL
IT WAS A VERY KIND AND AGREEABLE PRESENT AS ANY ONE MAY IMAGINE TO ONE IN MY CIRCUMSTANCES BUT NEVER WAS ANYTHING IN THE WORLD OF THAT KIND SO UNPLEASANT AWKWARD AND UNEASY AS IT WAS TO ME TO WEAR SUCH CLOTHES AT FIRST
THEY RIPPED IT OPEN AND AFTER EXAMINING THE CONTENTS WHICH INCLUDED ALL THE OWNER'S READY MONEY WITH THE EXCEPTION OF A TRIFLING SUM IN HIS POCKET THEY DIVIDED THE WHOLE AMONGST THEM
AND I MADE THE OTHER TWO CARRY PROVISIONS TO A CERTAIN DISTANCE WHERE FRIDAY WAS TO TAKE THEM
BUT AS I CAME NEARER I PERCEIVED PRESENTLY HE HAD A BOW AND ARROW AND WAS FITTING IT TO SHOOT AT ME
I TOOK HIM UP AND MADE MUCH OF HIM AND ENCOURAGED HIM ALL I COULD
BESIDES HE HEARD FROM WITHIN A CONCERT OF INSTRUMENTAL MUSIC ACCOMPANIED WITH THE HARMONIOUS NOTES OF NIGHTINGALES AND OTHER BIRDS
IT STUNNED HIM HE STAGGERED--YET HE MADE OFF AND I LOST SIGHT OF HIM TO MY CHAGRIN
SHOOTING A STAG WITH CHERRY-STONES BY R
THEY ARE COMING SAID SHE TO BROWN
UPON THIS I AWAKED FROM MY SLEEP
HIS DESIGN IS TO KILL YOU THEREFORE TAKE CARE OF YOURSELF AFTER THESE WORDS THE GENIE DISAPPEARED
THE NORMAN'S SPEAR STRIKING THE CENTRE OF HIS ANTAGONIST'S SHIELD WENT TO SHIVERS AND THE DISINHERITED KNIGHT REELED IN HIS SADDLE
ALI BABA RECEIVED COGIA HOUSSAIN WITH A SMILING COUNTENANCE AND IN THE MOST OBLIGING MANNER HE COULD WISH
BUT HE HARSHLY REFUSED HER AND MADE FERDINAND FOLLOW HIM TO HIS CELL
BUT THE CHARGE OF MAINTAINING ME ALTHOUGH I HAD A VERY SCANTY ALLOWANCE BEING TOO GREAT FOR A NARROW FORTUNE I WAS BOUND APPRENTICE TO MR JAMES BATES AN EMINENT SURGEON IN LONDON WITH WHOM I CONTINUED FOUR YEARS
BUT SHORTLY SAW AT A DISTANCE SUCH OBJECTS AS GREATLY DIMINISHED MY SATISFACTION AND WHICH I COULD NOT VIEW WITHOUT TERROR NAMELY A GREAT NUMBER OF SERPENTS SO MONSTROUS THAT THE LEAST OF THEM WAS CAPABLE OF SWALLOWING AN ELEPHANT
SUCH IS THE UNEVEN STATE OF HUMAN LIFE
AT BREAK OF DAY THE GENIE APPEARED AT THE APPOINTED HOUR BRINGING BACK THE BRIDEGROOM WHOM BY BREATHING UPON HE HAD LEFT MOTIONLESS AND ENTRANCED AT THE DOOR OF ALADDIN'S CHAMBER DURING THE NIGHT
HER LIPS VERMILION
PLACE FOR THE LADY ROWENA AS HE SPOKE A SIDE-DOOR AT THE UPPER END OF THE HALL OPENED AND ROWENA THE FAIR AND STATELY WARD OF CEDRIC FOLLOWED BY FOUR FEMALE ATTENDANTS ENTERED THE APARTMENT
I KNEW HIM AND YOU NOW FIND THAT MY SUSPICION WAS NOT GROUNDLESS ALI BABA WHO IMMEDIATELY FELT THE NEW OBLIGATION HE HAD TO MORGIANA FOR SAVING HIS LIFE A SECOND TIME EMBRACED HER
ALSO IT THUNDRED AND LIGHTNED IN MOST FEARFUL WISE THAT IT PUT ME INTO AN AGONY
THERE IS LIKEWISE ANOTHER DIVERSION WHICH IS ONLY SHOWN BEFORE THE EMPEROR AND EMPRESS AND FIRST MINISTER UPON PARTICULAR OCCASIONS
AT HIS SUGGESTION YOUR WIFE MAKES THIS PERNICIOUS DEMAND
GLOSSIN HAD HOWEVER IMPRESSED THE OLD MAN WITH A FIXED IDEA OF THE IMPENDING DANGER TO HIS HOUSE AND HE REFUSED TO ALLOW THE SOLDIERS TO GO
AND SHE HAD THE FINE AND SECRET JOY OF KNOWING THAT ALL HIS LOVE-WORDS CAME TO THE RIGHT EARS
TO THE OLDER BOYS AND GIRLS IT IS A STORY OF STIRRING ADVENTURE WHILE TO THE MATURE MAN IT IS A PICTURE OF CIVILIZATION
I WAS FOURTEEN MORE GETTING THE BRANCHES AND LIMBS AND THE VAST SPREADING HEAD CUT OFF WHICH I HACKED AND HEWED THROUGH WITH AXE AND HATCHET AND INEXPRESSIBLE LABOR
A SHORT CONSULTATION THEN TOOK PLACE BETWEEN BEAUMANOIR AND THE PRECEPTORS IN WHICH IT WAS DECIDED THAT BRIAN DE BOIS-GUILBERT WAS THE FITTEST KNIGHT TO DO BATTLE FOR THE HOLY ORDER
NOW I BEGAN TO TAKE COURAGE AND TO PEEP ABROAD AGAIN FOR I HAD NOT STIRRED OUT OF MY CASTLE FOR THREE DAYS AND NIGHTS SO THAT I BEGAN TO STARVE FOR PROVISIONS
WHEN I ATTENDED THE KING AFTER MY RECOVERY TO RETURN HIM THANKS FOR HIS FAVORS HE WAS PLEASED TO RALLY ME A GOOD DEAL UPON THIS ADVENTURE
ALI BABA'S SON DID NOT CHOOSE TO LIE UNDER SUCH OBLIGATION TO COGIA HOUSSAIN
THUS THE CAPTAIN AND HIS TROOP WERE FORCED TO RETIRE A SECOND TIME AND MUCH MORE DISSATISFIED
IT COST ME NEAR THREE MONTHS MORE TO CLEAR THE INSIDE AND WORK IT OUT SO AS TO MAKE AN EXACT BOAT OF IT
WITH QUICK LONG STRIDES THE GIPSY PROCEEDED STRAIGHT ACROSS THE WINTRY HEATH
I SHOULD BE VERY GLAD OF THAT SAYS THE CAPTAIN WITH ALL MY HEART WELL SAYS I I WILL SEND FOR THEM UP AND TALK WITH THEM FOR YOU SO I CAUSED FRIDAY AND THE TWO HOSTAGES--FOR THEY WERE NOW DISCHARGED THEIR COMRADES HAVING PERFORMED THEIR PROMISE--I SAY I CAUSED THEM TO GO TO THE CAVE AND BRING UP THE FIVE MEN PINIONED AS THEY WERE TO THE BOWER AND KEEP THEM THERE TILL I CAME
THIRDLY
AS HE APPROACHED THE CASTLE GATE HE WAS AT ONCE ADMITTED AND SHORTLY AFTER WAS USHERED INTO THE APARTMENT WHERE CEDRIC AND ATHELSTANE WERE CONFINED
WHERE'S COBWEB READY SAID COBWEB
SO THE FOUR MORTAL LOVERS WENT BACK TO ATHENS AND WERE MARRIED
AND IN SPITE OF MY GUARDS I BELIEVE THERE COULD NOT BE FEWER THAN TEN THOUSAND AT SEVERAL TIMES WHO MOUNTED MY BODY BY THE HELP OF LADDERS
THE CAPTAIN WHO WAS FOREMOST RAN IN UPON HIM AND KNOCKED HIM DOWN
HE WOULD THRUST HIM LIKE A CUR OVER HIS THRESHOLD AND WOULD EVEN SPIT ON HIM
FARE THEE WELL JEWESS!--THOU HAST TO DO WITH THEM THAT HAVE NEITHER SCRUPLE NOR PITY AND SO SAYING SHE LEFT THE ROOM LOCKING THE DOOR BEHIND HER
HASTEN TO LEAD YOUR FORCES TO THE ATTACK AND WHEN THOU SHALT SEE A RED FLAG WAVE FROM THE EASTERN TURRET PRESS THE NORMANS HARD
AT THE TIME THAT OUR STORY COMMENCES ONE GODFREY BERTRAM WAS THE LAIRD OF ELLANGOWAN AND THE OWNER OF THE NOW DIMINISHED ESTATES
THEN HOLDING A COUNCIL AND DELIBERATING UPON THIS OCCURRENCE THEY GUESSED THAT CASSIM WHEN HE WAS IN COULD NOT GET OUT AGAIN BUT COULD NOT IMAGINE HOW HE HAD LEARNED THE SECRET WORDS BY WHICH ALONE HE COULD ENTER
ROBBER AND VILLAIN HE EXCLAIMED I WILL PAY THEE NOTHING--NOT ONE SILVER PENNY WILL I PAY THEE--UNLESS MY DAUGHTER IS DELIVERED TO ME IN SAFETY AND HONOUR
HE'LL BE A LUCKY LAD AN HE WIN THROUGH WI'T FOOTNOTE
THE EMPEROR OF BLEFUSCU HAVING TAKEN THREE DAYS TO CONSULT RETURNED AN ANSWER CONSISTING OF MANY CIVILITIES AND EXCUSES
ALADDIN KNOWING THAT THIS WOULD BE SO HAD ALREADY GIVEN HIS COMMANDS TO THE GENIE OF THE LAMP
I WAITED A LONG TIME
AT WHICH THEY WERE NOT A LITTLE SORRY YET THEY DURST NOT GO OUT OF THE WAY
NOW AS THE WAVES WERE NOT SO HIGH AS AT FIRST BEING NEARER LAND I HELD MY HOLD TILL THE WAVE ABATED AND THEN FETCHED ANOTHER RUN WHICH BROUGHT ME SO NEAR THE SHORE THAT THE NEXT WAVE THOUGH IT WENT OVER ME YET DID NOT SO SWALLOW ME UP AS TO CARRY ME AWAY
MR BERTRAM HAD BEEN SOME DISTANCE FROM HOME ON THE DAY OF THE EVICTION
NOW THE MAN TO LOOK ON SEEMED VERY SAD
OUT OF GRATITUDE TO GOD FOR HIS MERCIES I CONTRIBUTED LIBERALLY TOWARD THE SUPPORT OF SEVERAL MOSQUES AND THE SUBSISTENCE OF THE POOR AND ENJOYED MYSELF WITH FRIENDS IN FESTIVITIES AND AMUSEMENTS
ON THE ONE SIDE HE HAD TO A GREAT DEGREE THE ABILITY TO UNDERSTAND MEN AND WOMEN AND READ THE THOUGHTS THAT WERE PASSING THROUGH THEIR MINDS
HE WAS A COMELY HANDSOME FELLOW PERFECTLY WELL MADE WITH STRAIGHT STRONG LIMBS NOT TOO LARGE
THERE YOU SHALL NOT SEE AGAIN SUCH THINGS AS YOU SAW WHEN YOU WERE IN THE LOWER REGION UPON THE EARTH TO WIT SORROW SICKNESS AFFLICTION AND HEALTH FOR THE FORMER THINGS ARE PASSED AWAY
PUCK WENT BACK AND TOLD OBERON WHAT HE HAD DONE AND OBERON SOON FOUND THAT HE HAD MADE A MISTAKE AND SET ABOUT LOOKING FOR DEMETRIUS AND HAVING FOUND HIM PUT SOME OF THE JUICE ON HIS EYES
SUPPER WAS GOT READY A GOOD BOTTLE OF WINE WAS OPENED AND THE LAIRD AND THE DOMINIC AND GUY MANNERING WERE ENJOYING THEMSELVES COMFORTABLY WHEN THE CONVERSATION WAS INTERRUPTED BY THE SHRILL VOICE OF SOMEONE COMING UPSTAIRS
HE WAS WEARING THE ROUGH SUIT IN WHICH HE HAD SPENT THE NIGHT IN THE GIPSY'S HOUSE HAVING BEEN UNABLE TO PROCURE A CHANGE ON ACCOUNT OF HIS PORTMANTEAU HAVING BEEN STOLEN
FOR BY THE HEAD OF MY FATHER THOU HAST NO OTHER OPTION SO MAY ABRAHAM JACOB AND ALL THE FATHERS OF OUR PEOPLE ASSIST ME SAID ISAAC
THUS WAS I EXPOSED TO THE MERCY OF THE WAVES THE REST OF THAT DAY AND THE FOLLOWING NIGHT
BUT ADDED HE MY SON WHAT IS PAST CANNOT BE RECALLED
FOR GOD'S SAKE TOM SMITH THROW DOWN YOUR ARMS AND YIELD OR YOU ARE ALL DEAD MEN THIS MOMENT WHO MUST WE YIELD TO
SHE THANKED HIM FOR HIS GOOD INTENTIONS
BUT I HAD A STRANGE UNEASINESS IN MY MIND TO GO DOWN TO THE POINT OF THE ISLAND
SO THEY CONSENTED TO ERECT THERE A PILLAR AND TO ENGRAVE UPON THE SIDE THEREOF THIS SENTENCE OVER THIS STILE IS THE WAY TO DOUBTING CASTLE WHICH IS KEPT BY GIANT DESPAIR WHO DESPISETH THE KING OF THE COELESTIAL COUNTRY AND SEEKS TO DESTROY HIS HOLY PILGRIMS MANY THEREFORE THAT FOLLOWED AFTER READ WHAT WAS WRITTEN AND ESCAPED THE DANGER
I ANSWERED I WAS AN ENGLISHMAN DRAWN BY ILL FORTUNE INTO THE GREATEST CALAMITY THAT EVER ANY CREATURE UNDERWENT AND BEGGED BY ALL THAT WAS MOVING TO BE DELIVERED OUT OF THE DUNGEON I WAS IN
THAT SHE SHOULD ACCEPT HIM AS A LOVER
I GAVE THE TENTH OF MY GAINS IN ALMS AS I HAD DONE UPON MY RETURN FROM MY OTHER VOYAGES AND RESTED FROM MY FATIGUES
I ACCEPT THE OFFER SAID THE KNIGHT
ON THE DAY FOLLOWING THE DEATH OF GLOSSIN DIRCK HATTERAICK WAS HIMSELF FOUND DEAD IN THE CELL HAVING HANGED HIMSELF BY MEANS OF A CORD TAKEN FROM HIS BED WHICH HE HAD CUNNINGLY CONTRIVED TO ATTACH TO THE PRISON WALL
AND HAVING SERVED FOR A LONG TIME IN INDIA WAS APPOINTED COLONEL OF HIS REGIMENT
THIS IS A MATTER OF THE FIRST IMPORTANCE AND FOR FEAR OF ANY TREACHERY I PROPOSE THAT WHOEVER UNDERTAKES THIS BUSINESS WITHOUT SUCCESS EVEN THOUGH THE FAILURE ARISES ONLY FROM AN ERROR OF JUDGMENT SHALL SUFFER DEATH WITHOUT WAITING FOR THE SENTIMENTS OF HIS COMPANIONS ONE OF THE ROBBERS STARTED UP AND SAID I SUBMIT TO THIS CONDITION AND THINK IT AN HONOR TO EXPOSE MY LIFE TO SERVE THE TROOP AFTER THIS ROBBER HAD RECEIVED GREAT COMMENDATIONS FROM THE CAPTAIN AND HIS COMRADES HE DISGUISED HIMSELF SO THAT NOBODY WOULD TAKE HIM FOR WHAT HE WAS
THOSE TWO I GOT TO MY RAFT WITH THE ARMS
MY SOUL CHUSETH STRANGLING RATHER THAN LIFE AND THE GRAVE IS MORE EASY FOR ME THAN THIS DUNGEON
ONE WOULD HAVE THOUGHT I COULD NOT HAVE HAD THE LEAST REFLECTION UPON MY MIND OF MY CIRCUMSTANCES WHILE I WAS MAKING THIS BOAT BUT I SHOULD HAVE IMMEDIATELY THOUGHT HOW I SHOULD GET IT INTO THE SEA
I HALLOOED AGAIN TO HIM AND MADE SIGNS TO COME FORWARD WHICH HE EASILY UNDERSTOOD AND CAME A LITTLE WAY
AND THE PRINCESS EXPRESSING HER WISHES HE IMMEDIATELY SENT FOUR SLAVES FOR THE PRETENDED HOLY WOMAN
FIVE HUNDRED WORKMEN WERE EMPLOYED TO MAKE TWO SAILS TO MY BOAT ACCORDING TO MY DIRECTIONS BY QUILTING THIRTEEN FOLDS OF THEIR STRONGEST LINEN TOGETHER
CASSIM'S WIFE STAYED AT HOME MOURNING UTTERING LAMENTABLE CRIES WITH THE WOMEN OF THE NEIGHBORHOOD WHO CAME ACCORDING TO CUSTOM DURING THE FUNERAL AND JOINING THEIR LAMENTATIONS WITH HERS FILLED THE QUARTER FAR AND NEAR WITH SOUNDS OF SORROW
MEANWHILE THE TILTYARD OF THE PRECEPTORY OF TEMPLESTOWE WAS PREPARED FOR THE COMBAT WHICH SHOULD DECIDE THE LIFE OR DEATH OF REBECCA
LIKE ALL GREAT BOOKS IT INTERESTS PEOPLE OF ALL AGES
AND TOOK ME BEFORE THE CAPTAIN WHO SEEING THAT I WAS IN RAGS GAVE ME ONE OF HIS OWN SUITS
IF I MAKE A RAFT AND LEAVE MYSELF TO THE CURRENT IT WILL CONVEY ME TO SOME INHABITED COUNTRY OR I SHALL PERISH
THE CAPTAIN WAS TERRIBLY AMAZED AND EVEN CONFOUNDED AT THIS BELIEVING THEY WOULD GO ON BOARD THE SHIP AGAIN AND SET SAIL GIVING THEIR COMRADES OVER FOR LOST AND SO HE SHOULD STILL LOSE THE SHIP WHICH HE WAS IN HOPES WE SHOULD HAVE RECOVERED
MANY TRICKS DID ARIEL PLAY THEM
BY GOOD FORTUNE HE HAD BEEN SO WELL TAUGHT THAT I WAS CARRIED BETWEEN HIS TEETH WITHOUT THE LEAST HURT OR EVEN TEARING MY CLOTHES
HERE I FOUND THE SUN VERY POWERFUL AND I WAS SO MUCH FATIGUED THAT I STEPPED INTO ONE OF THE CANNON TO COMPOSE ME WHERE I FELL FAST ASLEEP
BUT WAMBA SPRINGING FORWARD IN GOOD TIME CHECKED THE FATAL CAREER OF THE BLUE KNIGHT BY HAMSTRINGING HIS HORSE WITH A STROKE OF HIS SWORD
ACCORDINGLY HE WENT AMONG THE SHRUBS AND PERCEIVING THE DOOR CONCEALED BEHIND THEM STOOD BEFORE IT AND SAID OPEN SESAME THE DOOR INSTANTLY FLEW WIDE OPEN
THERE ALSO SHALL YOU BE CLOATHED WITH GLORY AND MAJESTY AND PUT INTO AN EQUIPAGE FIT TO RIDE OUT WITH THE KING OF GLORY
ON THE NEWS OF HAZLEWOOD'S BEING WOUNDED GETTING ABROAD THE NEIGHBOURHOOD WAS THROWN INTO A FERMENT OF INDIGNATION
MY NEXT CARE WAS WHAT TO LOAD IT WITH AND HOW TO PRESERVE WHAT I LAID UPON IT FROM THE SURF OF THE SEA
FOR I SAW MY DELIVERANCE INDEED VISIBLY PUT INTO MY HANDS ALL THINGS EASY AND A LARGE SHIP JUST READY TO CARRY ME AWAY WHITHER I PLEASED TO GO
I GOT IN AND THE BOY SHUT THE WINDOW CLOSE DOWN TO KEEP OUT THE COLD
AND INDEED IT WAS A PRESENT AS IF I HAD BEEN ONE THAT WAS NOT TO BE CARRIED AWAY WITH THEM BUT AS IF I HAD BEEN TO DWELL UPON THE ISLAND STILL
BUT I HAD THE GOOD FORTUNE TO RIP UP HIS BELLY BEFORE HE COULD DO ME ANY MISCHIEF
ROBINSON CRUSOE ALTHOUGH HUNDREDS HAVE TRIED BOTH AT HOME AND ABROAD NO ONE HAS BEEN ABLE TO WRITE A BOOK THAT COULD TAKE THE PLACE OF ROBINSON CRUSOE THE STORY OF THAT STURDY VOYAGING ENGLISHMAN WHO WAS ALWAYS ON THE LOOKOUT FOR ADVENTURES AND WAS NEVER DISCOURAGED BY ANY CIRCUMSTANCES IN WHICH HE FOUND HIMSELF
AN INTERVAL OF QUIET NOW SUCCEEDED THE BESIEGERS REMAINING IN POSSESSION OF THE OUTER DEFENCES OF THE CASTLE AND THE BESIEGED RETIRING FOR THE TIME WITHIN THE WALLS OF THE FORTRESS
THE PLAYS OF SHAKESPEARE WILLIAM SHAKESPEARE THE GREATEST OF ENGLISH WRITERS WAS BORN IN 1564 AND WAS PRETTY WELL EDUCATED FOR THOSE DAYS
I HAD IN VAIN ENTREATED THEM NOT TO MEDDLE WITH THE EGG
SINDBAD STOPPED HERE AND ORDERED THE MUSICIANS TO PROCEED WITH THEIR CONCERT WHICH THE STORY HAD INTERRUPTED
THEY HAVE JUST BEEN CELEBRATING IN FRANCE THE CENTENARY OF JEAN JACQUES ROUSSEAU
THE REST OF THE GREAT OFFICERS ARE MUCH UPON A PAR
MAKING A THOUSAND GESTURES AND MOTIONS WHICH I CANNOT DESCRIBE
I HAD NOW MADE A GOOD PROGRESS IN UNDERSTANDING AND SPEAKING THEIR LANGUAGE
THE PRINCESS IN ANTICIPATION OF THE SUCCESS OF HER SCHEME HAD SO PLACED HER WOMEN FROM THE GREAT HALL TO THE FOOT OF THE STAIRCASE THAT THE WORD WAS NO SOONER GIVEN THAT THE AFRICAN MAGICIAN WAS FALLEN BACKWARD THAN THE DOOR WAS OPENED AND ALADDIN ADMITTED TO THE HALL
ROBINSON CRUSOE WAS WRITTEN IN 1719 BY DANIEL DEFOE THE SON OF A BUTCHER WHEN HE WAS OVER SIXTY YEARS OF AGE
WE SAW BEFORE US A LARGE APARTMENT WITH A PORCH HAVING ON ONE SIDE A HEAP OF HUMAN BONES AND ON THE OTHER A VAST NUMBER OF ROASTING-SPITS
AND SO IT HAS COME TO BE READ AGAIN AND AGAIN AND ADMIRED AND CHERISHED THE WORLD OVER
THE LARGENESS OF ITS FEATURES MADE IT APPEAR THE MOST DEFORMED ANIMAL THAT CAN BE CONCEIVED
I HAD A GREAT HIGH SHAPELESS CAP MADE OF A GOAT'S SKIN WITH A FLAP HANGING DOWN BEHIND AS WELL TO KEEP THE SUN FROM ME AS TO SHOOT THE RAIN OFF FROM RUNNING INTO MY NECK NOTHING BEING SO HURTFUL IN THESE CLIMATES AS THE RAIN UPON THE FLESH UNDER THE CLOTHES
IF THE GRAVE CAN GIVE UP THE DEAD THAT IS MY DEAR AND HONOURED MASTER A LAWYER FRIEND OF THE COLONEL'S A MR PLEYDALL WAS STAYING AT WOODBOURNE THAT NIGHT AND HE AT ONCE SET ABOUT ENDEAVOURING TO SOLVE THE MYSTERY
I WAS ENDEAVORING TO FIND SOME GAP IN THE HEDGE WHEN I DISCOVERED ONE OF THE INHABITANTS IN THE NEXT FIELD ADVANCING TOWARD THE STILE OF THE SAME SIZE WITH HIM WHOM I SAW IN THE SEA PURSUING OUR BOAT
AND WHEN I THOUGHT FIT I TORE THEM IN PIECES AND SO WITHIN TEN DAYS I WILL DO YOU
ALONE ON A DESOLATE ISLAND BY DANIEL DEFOE WHEN I WAKED IT WAS BROAD DAY THE WEATHER CLEAR AND THE STORM ABATED SO THAT THE SEA DID NOT RAGE AND SWELL AS BEFORE
WHEN DAY APPEARED HE RETIRED BUT I DARED NOT LEAVE MY FORT UNTIL THE SUN AROSE
IN SPITE OF THIS OMINOUS INTELLIGENCE ISAAC PURSUED HIS WAY AND ON ARRIVING AT TEMPLESTOWE WAS AT ONCE SHOWN INTO THE PRESENCE OF THE GRAND MASTER HIMSELF
HE WHOSE PRISONER THOU ART SCORNS TO TAKE MEAN REVENGE FOR WHAT IS PAST
TO YOU ANTONIO HE SAID I OWE THE MOST IN MONEY AND IN LOVE
OUR MEN THEREFORE WANDERED ON THE SHORE TO FIND OUT SOME FRESH WATER NEAR THE SEA AND I WALKED ALONE ABOUT A MILE ON THE OTHER SIDE WHERE I OBSERVED THE COUNTRY ALL BARREN AND ROCKY
WHEN HE FOUND THAT HIS ATTEMPT HAD FAILED HE SET OUT TO RETURN TO AFRICA BUT AVOIDED THE TOWN LEST ANY PERSON WHO HAD SEEN HIM LEAVE IN COMPANY WITH ALADDIN SHOULD MAKE INQUIRIES AFTER THE YOUTH
AND BEFORE LONG THE GRAND MASTER PRECEDED BY A STATELY RETINUE APPROACHED HIS THRONE
THERE TITANIA ALWAYS SLEPT A PART OF THE NIGHT WRAPPED IN THE ENAMELED SKIN OF A SNAKE
HE ANSWERED SIR I PERCEIVE BY THE BOOK IN MY HAND THAT I AM CONDEMNED TO DIE AND AFTER THAT TO COME TO JUDGMENT AND I FIND THAT I AM NOT WILLING TO DO THE FIRST NOR ABLE TO DO THE SECOND
THUS MY FEAR BANISHED ALL MY RELIGIOUS HOPE ALL THAT FORMER CONFIDENCE IN GOD WHICH WAS FOUNDED UPON SUCH WONDERFUL EXPERIENCE AS I HAD HAD OF HIS GOODNESS
I HAVE TWO BOONS TO CRAVE ANSWERED THE GIPSY SPEAKING LOW AND HASTILY
AND NOW ABEL SAMPSON AS EVER YE LOVED THE HOUSE OF ELLANGOWAN AWAY WITH MY MESSAGE TO THE ENGLISH COLONEL AS IF LIFE AND DEATH WERE UPON YOUR HASTE SO SAYING SHE TURNED SUDDENLY FROM THE AMAZED DOMINIE WHO HURRIED BACK TO WOODBOURNE EXCLAIMING AS HE WENT PRODIGIOUS
MANNERING WAS MUCH AFFECTED WHEN THE OLD LAIRD FAILED TO REMEMBER HIM FOR HE HAD NOT FORGOTTEN HIS HOSPITABLE KINDNESS MANY YEARS BEFORE ON THE NIGHT WHEN LITTLE HARRY WAS BORN
IN THE MEANTIME THE ROBBER REJOINED HIS TROOP IN THE FOREST AND RECOUNTED TO THEM HIS SUCCESS EXPATIATING UPON HIS GOOD FORTUNE IN MEETING SO SOON WITH THE ONLY PERSON WHO COULD INFORM HIM OF WHAT HE WANTED TO KNOW
THE GRAND VIZIER WHO IN SECRET BORE NO GOODWILL TO ALADDIN INTIMATED HIS SUSPICION THAT THE PALACE WAS BUILT BY MAGIC AND THAT ALADDIN HAD MADE HIS HUNTING EXCURSION AN EXCUSE FOR THE REMOVAL OF HIS PALACE WITH THE SAME SUDDENNESS WITH WHICH IT HAD BEEN ERECTED
HE WAS SOON MUFFLED IN HIS RELIGIOUS DISGUISE
AND INDEED IT ALMOST SPOILED SOME OF THEM AND ALMOST DRIED UP THEIR MILK
ALTHOUGH MY EVIL DESTINY SO ORDERED THAT SHE HAD NOT POWER TO HINDER ME AS THE READER MAY KNOW HEREAFTER
THEN HER FEAR REDOUBLED AND HER GRIEF WAS THE MORE SENSIBLE BECAUSE SHE WAS FORCED TO KEEP IT TO HERSELF
THE TWO TRAVELLERS WERE SOON LOST UNDER THE BOUGHS OF THE FOREST PATH
NOW WHEN THEY WERE COME UP TO THE GATE THERE WAS WRITTEN OVER IT IN LETTERS OF GOLD BLESSED ARE THEY THAT DO HIS COMMANDMENTS THAT THEY MAY HAVE RIGHT TO THE TREE OF LIFE AND MAY ENTER IN THROUGH THE GATES INTO THE CITY
WHEN ALADDIN HAD GOT INTO HIS CHAMBER HE TOOK THE LAMP RUBBED IT IN THE SAME PLACE AS BEFORE WHEN IMMEDIATELY THE GENIE APPEARED AND SAID TO HIM WHAT WOULDST THOU HAVE
HE KNEW THAT IVANHOE HAD BEEN A CLOSE ATTENDANT ON HIS BROTHER KING RICHARD IN THE HOLY LAND
I HAD ONLY ONE MISFORTUNE THAT THE RATS ON BOARD CARRIED AWAY ONE OF MY SHEEP
WE OBSERVED ALSO AN AMPHIBIOUS ANIMAL LIKE A COW WHICH GAVE MILK
BY THIS YOU MAY SEE WE ARE RIGHT
AND WITH THAT HIS WIFE REPLIED I FEAR SAID SHE THAT THEY LIVE IN HOPE THAT SOME WILL COME TO RELIEVE THEM OR THAT THEY HAVE PICK-LOCKS ABOUT THEM BY THE MEANS OF WHICH THEY HOPE TO ESCAPE
THE TREMBLING OF THE ISLAND WAS NOTICED ON BOARD SHIP AND WE WERE CALLED UPON TO RE-EMBARK SPEEDILY LEST WE SHOULD ALL BE LOST
ALADDIN THEN ADDRESSED HIS MOTHER
IT WAS NOW ABOUT EIGHT O'CLOCK AT NIGHT AND THE CAPTAIN ORDERED SUPPER IMMEDIATELY THINKING I HAD ALREADY FASTED TOO LONG
BUT TOLD THE CAPTAIN I WOULD STAY THAT NIGHT TO PREPARE MY THINGS AND DESIRED HIM TO GO ON BOARD IN THE MEANTIME AND KEEP ALL RIGHT IN THE SHIP AND SEND THE BOAT ON SHORE NEXT DAY FOR ME
BUT HE WAS AT LAST IN PAIN AT MY LONG ABSENCE
AFTER WHICH THEY PROVED VERY HONEST AND QUIET FELLOWS
HINDBAD WHOSE FEAR WAS INCREASED AT THE SIGHT OF SO MANY PEOPLE AND OF A BANQUET SO SUMPTUOUS SALUTED THE COMPANY TREMBLING
BUT I WILL TELL YOU NOW WHAT IT WANTS AND THAT IS A ROC'S EGG HUNG UP IN THE MIDST OF THE DOME PRINCESS REPLIED ALADDIN IT IS ENOUGH THAT YOU THINK IT WANTS SUCH AN ORNAMENT
AND THEN WENT TO MORGIANA TO BID HER TO GET A GOOD SUPPER FOR HIS GUEST
AND HAVING REFRESHED HIM I MADE SIGNS FOR HIM TO GO AND LIE DOWN TO SLEEP SHOWING HIM A PLACE WHERE I HAD LAID SOME RICE-STRAW AND A BLANKET UPON IT WHICH I USED TO SLEEP UPON MYSELF SOMETIMES
AND THEREFORE SOMETIMES I SAT CONTRIVING WAYS TO GET HER ABOUT THE ISLAND AND AT OTHER TIMES I SAT MYSELF DOWN CONTENTED ENOUGH WITHOUT HER
BUT WHEN I CAME TO THE SHIP MY DIFFICULTY WAS STILL GREATER TO KNOW HOW TO GET ON BOARD
ALL HER ORNAMENTS HAD BEEN REMOVED AND A COARSE WHITE DRESS OF THE SIMPLEST FORM HAD BEEN SUBSTITUTED FOR HER ORIENTAL GARMENTS
I WAS POSITIVELY AGAINST THAT
AND TERRIBLY APPREHENSIVE HE WAS THAT THEY WOULD BE TOO POWERFUL FOR US
ALADDIN IGNORANT OF THEIR VALUE WOULD HAVE PREFERRED FIGS OR GRAPES OR POMEGRANATES
THEY WERE INTERRUPTED IN THEIR CONVERSATION BY MAC-GUFFOG WHO TOLD THEM THAT IT WAS TIME FOR THE VISITOR TO LEAVE
AFTER THE PRINCESS HAD PASSED BY AND ENTERED THE BATH ALADDIN QUITTED HIS HIDING-PLACE AND WENT HOME
THE UNHAPPY JEW EYED THEIR SAVAGE COUNTENANCES AND THAT OF FRONT DE-BOEUF IN HOPE OF DISCOVERING SOME SYMPTOMS OF RELENTING
AND WHEN I WAS DOWN THE HAILSTONES GAVE ME SUCH CRUEL BANGS ALL OVER THE BODY AS IF I HAD BEEN PELTED WITH TENNIS-BALLS
AND HAD IT RETURNED AGAIN IMMEDIATELY I MUST HAVE BEEN STRANGLED IN THE WATER
I SMILED AT HIM AND TOLD HIM THAT MEN IN OUR CIRCUMSTANCES WERE PAST THE OPERATION OF FEAR
THEY PROMISED FAITHFULLY TO BEAR THEIR CONFINEMENT WITH PATIENCE AND WERE VERY THANKFUL THAT THEY HAD SUCH GOOD USAGE AS TO HAVE PROVISIONS AND LIGHT LEFT THEM
AND FINDING THE WATER HAD SPENT ITSELF AND BEGAN TO RETURN I STRUCK FORWARD AGAINST THE RETURN OF THE WAVES AND FELT GROUND AGAIN WITH MY FEET
AND HAD I GOTTEN IT INTO THE WATER I MAKE NO QUESTION BUT I SHOULD HAVE BEGUN THE MADDEST VOYAGE AND THE MOST UNLIKELY TO BE PERFORMED THAT EVER WAS UNDERTAKEN
THE CHAIN ENABLED HIM TO MOVE A DISTANCE OF ABOUT FOUR FEET FROM THE BAR AND WHEN THUS SECURED HIS HANDCUFFS WERE REMOVED
THE FOOT BY TWENTY-FOUR IN A-BREAST AND THE HORSE BY SIXTEEN WITH DRUMS BEATING COLORS FLYING AND PIKES ADVANCED
GABRIEL THE GIPSY THE SAME MAN WHO HAD AVOIDED MEETING BERTRAM'S EYE WHEN OUT HUNTING WITH DANDIE DINMONT TOLD THE WHOLE STORY OF KENNEDY'S MURDER AS HE WAS AT WARROCH POINT ON THE DAY OF ITS OCCURRENCE
YOU MAY BE SURE MY THOUGHTS RAN MANY TIMES UPON THE PROSPECT OF LAND WHICH I HAD SEEN FROM THE OTHER SIDE OF THE ISLAND
THOSE PIECES OF GLASS WHICH I GOT FROM THE TREES IN THE GARDEN OF THE SUBTERRANEAN PALACE ARE JEWELS OF INESTIMABLE VALUE AND FIT FOR THE GREATEST MONARCHS
NOTWITHSTANDING THE TWILIGHT AND ALTHOUGH HIS DRESS AND ARMS SHOWED HIM TO BE AN OUTLAW WAMBA RECOGNISED HIM TO BE LOCKSLEY THE YEOMAN A MAN WHO HAD CARRIED OFF THE PRIZE FOR ARCHERY AT THE TOURNAMENT A DAY OR TWO BEFORE
I OFFERED TO LEAVE MY GOODS IN SECURITY FOR PAYMENT OF MY FREIGHT BUT THE CAPTAIN PROTESTED HE WOULD NOT RECEIVE ONE FARTHING
BUT WHEN HE HAD PRONOUNCED THE WORD AND THE DOOR HAD OPENED HE WAS STRUCK WITH HORROR AT THE DISMAL SIGHT OF HIS BROTHER'S BODY
THIS INFAMOUS MAGICIAN THE BASEST OF MEN WAS THE SOLE CAUSE OF MY MISFORTUNE THE AFRICAN MAGICIAN WHO WAS THUS TWICE FOILED IN HIS ENDEAVOR TO RUIN ALADDIN HAD A YOUNGER BROTHER WHO WAS AS SKILFUL A MAGICIAN AS HIMSELF AND EXCEEDED HIM IN WICKEDNESS AND HATRED OF MANKIND
UPON THIS MY SAVAGE FOR SO I CALL HIM NOW MADE A MOTION TO ME TO LEND HIM MY SWORD WHICH HUNG NAKED IN A BELT BY MY SIDE WHICH I DID
THIS WAS ABOUT NOON
ALL EYES WERE TURNED TO SEE THE NEW CHAMPION AND NO SOONER WERE THE BARRIERS OPENED THAN HE PACED INTO THE LISTS
THE DARK RED FLUSH WAS STILL ON HIS BROW
THE INHABITANTS ARE SO BARBAROUS THAT THEY STILL EAT HUMAN FLESH
IT WILL NOT BE SHE MUTTERED TO HERSELF
I BELIEVE YOU SON TO BE SO DUTIFUL A CHILD THAT YOU WILL NOT REFUSE MORGIANA FOR YOUR WIFE
BUT HOPED IF HE NOW MISSED HIS AIM TO SECURE IT ANOTHER TIME BY KEEPING UP A FRIENDLY CORRESPONDENCE WITH THE FATHER AND SON
SUCH IS THE LAW AND SHYLOCK IN HIS FEAR SAID THEN I WILL TAKE BASSANIO'S OFFER NO SAID PORTIA STERNLY YOU SHALL HAVE NOTHING BUT YOUR BOND
6TH
SOMETIMES I FANCIED IT MUST BE THE DEVIL AND REASON JOINED IN WITH ME IN THIS SUPPOSITION FOR HOW SHOULD ANY OTHER THING IN HUMAN SHAPE COME INTO THE PLACE
BUT HE BEING A MAN WELL EXPERIENCED IN THE NAVIGATION OF THOSE SEAS BID US ALL PREPARE AGAINST A STORM WHICH ACCORDINGLY HAPPENED ON THE DAY FOLLOWING
I AND THE OTHER SLAVES OF THE LAMP I AM HUNGRY SAID ALADDIN
BUT THE OTHER TWO WERE TAKEN INTO MY SERVICE UPON THE CAPTAIN'S RECOMMENDATION AND UPON THEIR SOLEMNLY ENGAGING TO LIVE AND DIE WITH US
HE THEN EMPTIED THE BAGS WHICH RAISED SUCH A GREAT HEAP OF GOLD AS DAZZLED HIS WIFE'S EYES AND THEN HE TOLD HER THE WHOLE ADVENTURE FROM BEGINNING TO END AND ABOVE ALL RECOMMENDED HER TO KEEP IT SECRET
I REMOVED FROM THE OLD JEWRY TO FETTER LANE AND FROM THENCE TO WAPPING HOPING TO GET BUSINESS AMONG THE SAILORS
SO THAT HAD MY CAVE BEEN TO BE SEEN IT LOOKED LIKE A GENERAL MAGAZINE OF ALL NECESSARY THINGS
THESE OBJECTS SERVED ONLY TO AUGMENT OUR DESPAIR
NO ONE WHO BEGINS TO READ GUY MANNERING WILL WISH TO PUT IT DOWN UNTIL HE HAS FINISHED IT IVANHOE RETOLD BY SIR EDWARD SULLIVAN AT THE TIME WHEN KING RICHARD OF THE LION HEART WAS ABSENT FROM HIS COUNTRY AND A PRISONER IN THE POWER OF THE PERFIDIOUS AND CRUEL DUKE OF AUSTRIA THERE LIVED IN ENGLAND A HIGHBORN SAXON NAMED CEDRIC
I APPROACHED HIS THRONE AND SALUTED HIM AS I USED TO DO THE KINGS OF THE INDIES
NESBIT ANTONIO WAS A RICH AND PROSPEROUS MERCHANT OF VENICE
MAY I GET OUT AGAIN WITH MY LIFE YOU SHALL POSSESS THE COUNTRY ALONE
KILL ME SAID THE CLOWN THE RED BUMBLE-BEE ON THE TOP OF THE THISTLE YONDER AND BRING ME THE HONEY-BAG
AND IN A WORD THE QUESTION WAS WHETHER I WOULD GO TO MANAGE THE TRADING PART UPON THE COAST OF GUINEA
BUT ALL MY DEVICES TO GET IT INTO THE WATER FAILED ME
AND MIRANDA IN TERROR PRAYED HER FATHER TO HAVE MERCY ON HER LOVER
I WAS CARRIED AS USUAL IN MY TRAVELLING BOX WHICH AS I HAVE ALREADY DESCRIBED WAS A VERY CONVENIENT CLOSET OF TWELVE FEET WIDE
WHILE THE FIFTH KNIGHT ALONE MAINTAINED THE HONOUR OF HIS PARTY
AS HE FANCIED THAT THIS WOMAN MIGHT BE SERVICEABLE TO HIM IN THE PROJECT HE HAD CONCEIVED HE MADE MORE MINUTE INQUIRIES AND REQUESTED TO BE INFORMED MORE PARTICULARLY WHO THAT HOLY WOMAN WAS AND WHAT SORT OF MIRACLES SHE PERFORMED
AND PARTICULARLY THE FEATURES OF MY MASTER'S COUNTENANCE ALTHOUGH HE WERE BUT A FARMER WHEN I BEHELD HIM FROM THE HEIGHT OF SIXTY FEET APPEARED VERY WELL PROPORTIONED
BUT HE STILL LIVED WITH THE LAIRD AS BEFORE AND WAS CHIEFLY EMPLOYED IN TEACHING BERTRAM'S DAUGHTER LITTLE LUCY WHO WAS NOW GROWING UP INTO A GENTLE AND BONNY GIRL
THE WAVE THAT CAME UPON ME AGAIN BURIED ME AT ONCE TWENTY OR THIRTY FEET DEEP IN ITS OWN BODY AND I COULD FEEL MYSELF CARRIED WITH A MIGHTY FORCE AND SWIFTNESS TOWARD THE SHORE A VERY GREAT WAY
IT WAS ALREADY GROWING DARK WHEN A SHRILL AND PIERCING SHOUT WAS HEARD FROM THE SEA SHORE UNDER THE WOOD AND ON HURRYING TO THE PLACE MR BERTRAM WAS HORRIFIED TO SEE THE DEAD BODY OF FRANK KENNEDY LYING ON THE BEACH RIGHT UNDER A HIGH PRECIPICE OF ROCKS
ALMOST IMMEDIATELY AFTER A BAND OF YEOMEN HEADED BY LOCKSLEY BROKE FORTH FROM THE GLADE WHO JOINING MANFULLY IN THE FRAY SOON DISPOSED OF THE RUFFIANS ALL OF WHOM LAY ON THE SPOT DEAD OR MORTALLY WOUNDED
I GOT IT DOWN TO MY RAFT WHOLE AS IT WAS WITHOUT LOSING TIME TO LOOK INTO IT FOR I KNEW IN GENERAL WHAT IT CONTAINED
SO THEY CALLED TO KNOW THE MATTER BUT THERE WAS NONE TO ANSWER ONLY THEY HEARD A GROANING
BUT IT WENT AGAINST MY STOMACH TO DRAW THE CARCASS OFF THE BED WHERE IT LAY STILL BLEEDING
ONE DAY ORLANDO MET THEM BUT HE DID NOT KNOW ROSALIND IN HER BOY'S CLOTHES THOUGH HE LIKED THE PRETTY SHEPHERD YOUTH BECAUSE HE FANCIED A LIKENESS IN HIM TO HER HE LOVED
PERHAPS THE SULTAN MAY NOT BE SO BUSY THE NEXT MORNING SHE REPAIRED TO THE SULTAN'S PALACE WITH THE PRESENT AS EARLY AS THE DAY BEFORE
MY PATRON DESIGNING TO RETURN WHEN IT WAS ROTTEN AND TAKE HIS TEETH TO TRADE WITH
MY DEAR FRIEND AND DELIVERER SAYS HE THERE'S YOUR SHIP
SO I SAW IN MY DREAM THAT THE MAN BEGAN TO RUN
AT THE CLOSE OF THE EVENING DURING WHICH THE PRINCESS HAD TRIED ALL SHE COULD TO PLEASE HIM SHE ASKED HIM TO EXCHANGE CUPS WITH HER AND GIVING THE SIGNAL HAD THE DRUGGED CUP BROUGHT TO HER WHICH SHE GAVE TO THE MAGICIAN
FOR BY LIFTING IT UP TO MY FACE I DISCOVERED THE METHODS THEY HAD TAKEN TO BIND ME AND AT THE SAME TIME WITH A VIOLENT PULL WHICH GAVE ME EXCESSIVE PAIN I A LITTLE LOOSENED THE STRINGS THAT TIED DOWN MY HAIR ON THE LEFT SIDE SO THAT I WAS JUST ABLE TO TURN MY HEAD ABOUT TWO INCHES
WHEN ALI BABA HEARD HIM MAKE THE DOOR CLOSE BY PRONOUNCING THESE WORDS SHUT SESAME EVERY MAN AT ONCE WENT AND BRIDLED HIS HORSE FASTENED HIS WALLET AND MOUNTED AGAIN
IN THE VERSION HERE GIVEN THE STORY HAS BEEN CONDENSED BY OMITTING THE LESS DRAMATIC PASSAGES BUT THE AUTHOR'S TEXT REMAINS OTHERWISE UNCHANGED CHRISTIAN STARTS ON HIS JOURNEY BY JOHN BUNYAN AS I WALK'D THROUGH THE WILDERNESS OF THIS WORLD I LIGHTED ON A CERTAIN PLACE WHERE WAS A DEN AND I LAID ME DOWN IN THAT PLACE TO SLEEP
AFTERWARD THE PRINCESS WOULD HAVE BROUGHT HIM BACK AGAIN INTO THE GREAT HALL TO MAKE HIM DINE WITH HER
THE EMPEROR AND HIS WHOLE COURT STOOD ON THE SHORE EXPECTING THE ISSUE OF THIS GREAT ADVENTURE
THAT SUCH THINGS AS THESE WERE THE TESTIMONIES WE HAD OF A SECRET HAND OF PROVIDENCE GOVERNING THE WORLD AND AN EVIDENCE THAT THE EYE OF AN INFINITE POWER COULD SEARCH INTO THE REMOTEST CORNER OF THE WORLD AND SEND HELP TO THE MISERABLE WHENEVER HE PLEASED
BUT THE SAIL WAS SPLIT AND WE HAULED DOWN THE YARD AND GOT THE SAIL INTO THE SHIP AND UNBOUND ALL THE THINGS CLEAR OF IT
HE HAD COME HE SAID TO TELL HER THAT HE WAS PREPARED TO REFUSE TO DO BATTLE FOR THE TEMPLARS AGAINST HER AND SACRIFICE HIS NAME AND HONOUR AS A MEMBER OF THE HOLY ORDER AND THAT HE WOULD LEAVE THE PRECEPTORY APPEAR IN THREE DAYS IN DISGUISE AND HIMSELF BE HER CHAMPION AGAINST ANY KNIGHT WHO SHOULD CONFRONT HIM ON ONE CONDITION
NO
AS THE BANQUET WENT ON CONVERSATION WAS INTERRUPTED BY THE ENTRANCE OF A PAGE WHO ANNOUNCED THAT THERE WAS A STRANGER AT THE GATE IMPLORING ADMITTANCE AND HOSPITALITY
HE TOOK IT IN HIS HAND LOOKED FOR THAT PART WHERE HIS MOTHER HAD RUBBED IT WITH THE SAND RUBBED IT ALSO WHEN THE GENIE IMMEDIATELY APPEARED AND SAID WHAT WOULDST THOU HAVE
AND THAT I SHALL LOSE MY GOOD MASTER ON THE OTHER HAND AS ALI BABA AND HIS WIFE WERE OFTEN SEEN TO GO BETWEEN CASSIM'S AND THEIR OWN HOUSE ALL THAT DAY AND TO SEEM MELANCHOLY NOBODY WAS SURPRISED IN THE EVENING TO HEAR THE LAMENTABLE SHRIEKS AND CRIES OF CASSIM'S WIFE AND MORGIANA WHO GAVE OUT EVERYWHERE THAT HER MASTER WAS DEAD
BE COMFORTED MY BROTHER FOR I FORGIVE THEE
AND THEREFORE WHEN HE WAS AGAIN ABOUT TO MOVE I SCREAMED AS LOUD AS FEAR COULD MAKE ME
WHEREUPON HE BEGAN AGAIN TO THINK THAT MY BRAIN WAS DISTURBED OF WHICH HE GAVE ME A HINT AND ADVISED ME TO GO TO BED IN A CABIN HE HAD PROVIDED
DO NOT BE AFRAID THAT THE LIQUOR WILL SPOIL YOUR CLOTHES FOR IT IS NOT OIL AND THE LAMP WILL BE DRY AS SOON AS IT IS THROWN OUT AFTER THESE WORDS THE MAGICIAN DREW A RING OFF HIS FINGER AND PUT IT ON ONE OF ALADDIN'S SAYING
HIS NAME IS APOLLYON
LET THE LAW HAVE ITS OWN--HE MUST SPEAK ERE HE DIE SHE THEN SUPPLIED THE TWO WITH LOADED PISTOLS AND STARTED AFRESH THROUGH THE WOOD IN THE DIRECTION OF WARROCH POINT
EXPLAIN YOURSELF I WILL REPLIED MORGIANA
IMMEDIATELY THE PALACE WAS TRANSPORTED INTO CHINA AND ITS REMOVAL WAS ONLY FELT BY TWO LITTLE SHOCKS THE ONE WHEN IT WAS LIFTED UP THE OTHER WHEN IT WAS SET DOWN AND BOTH IN A VERY SHORT INTERVAL OF TIME
AND IF YOU DO NOT MAKE HIM ASHAMED OF IT I DESPAIR OF HIS EVER COMING TO ANY GOOD
THEY HOWEVER DID NOT SEEM TO MIND HER
TWO OF THEM WERE KEPT PINIONED INDEED BECAUSE THE CAPTAIN WAS NOT ABLE TO TRUST THEM
AND MANY WERE THE REJOICINGS AT THE WEDDING
BUT THERE WAS NOTHING OF THIS APPEARED
BROTHER SAID CHRISTIAN WHAT SHALL WE DO
DE BOIS-GUILBERT SEEMED TO SPEAK SLIGHTINGLY OF THE ENGLISH WARRIORS WHILE GIVING THE PLACE OF HONOUR TO THE KNIGHTS OF THE TEMPLE
ON PUTTING OUT TO SEA WE WERE OVERTAKEN BY SUCH A SUDDEN GUST OF WIND AS OBLIGED THE CAPTAIN TO LOWER HIS YARDS AND TAKE ALL OTHER NECESSARY PRECAUTIONS TO PREVENT THE DANGER THAT THREATENED US
LET ME DIE IN PEACE IN PEACE THOU SHALT NOT DIE REPEATED THE VOICE
IT BEING TOO EXTRAORDINARY TO BE RELATED BY ANY OTHER THAN THE PERSON TO WHOM THE EVENTS HAD HAPPENED
I WILL MYSELF TELL THE NAME OF THE KNIGHT BEFORE WHOSE LANCE I FELL
WE TRADED FROM ISLAND TO ISLAND AND EXCHANGED COMMODITIES WITH GREAT PROFIT
A SENTENCE
AND WHEN THOU TALKEST OF THY JOURNEY AND OF WHAT THOU HAST HEARD AND SEEN THOU ART INWARDLY DESIROUS OF VAIN-GLORY IN ALL THAT THOU SAYEST OR DOEST
AND THE THIRD RAN FOR IT
AS HE WAS REFLECTING ON HIS MISERABLE SITUATION HIS ATTENTION WAS ATTRACTED BY A LOUD KNOCKING AT THE GATE OF THE GAOL
THE GOD OF ABRAHAM'S PROMISE HATH OPENED AN ESCAPE TO HIS DAUGHTER EVEN FROM THIS ABYSS OF INFAMY AS SHE SPOKE SHE THREW OPEN THE LATTICED WINDOW AND IN AN INSTANT AFTER STOOD ON THE VERY VERGE OF THE PARAPET OUTSIDE WITH NOT THE SLIGHTEST SCREEN BETWEEN HER AND THE TREMENDOUS DEPTH BELOW
OH I WANT NOTHING SAID THE CLOWN
AND I HAD THE MORTIFICATION TO SEE MY COAT SHIRT AND WAISTCOAT WHICH I HAD LEFT ON THE SHORE UPON THE SAND SWIM AWAY
AND WHEN THE SIGNAL FOR BATTLE WAS GIVEN SOME FIFTY KNIGHTS AT THE SAME MOMENT CHARGED WILDLY AT EACH OTHER IN THE LISTS
ALADDIN HAD FETCHED SOME WATER AND SPRINKLED IT IN HER FACE TO RECOVER HER
WHEN CLIMBING UP TO THE TOP OF THE HILL THERE HE STOOD AND POINTING TO THE SHIP HE EMBRACED ME IN HIS ARMS
AND THIS I CAN ASSURE YOU BECAUSE HE PULLED IT OUT BEFORE ME AND SHOWED IT TO ME IN TRIUMPH PRINCESS SAID ALADDIN I THINK I HAVE FOUND THE MEANS TO DELIVER YOU AND TO REGAIN POSSESSION OF THE LAMP ON WHICH ALL MY PROSPERITY DEPENDS
IN A LITTLE TIME I AND MY FAMILY AND FRIENDS CAME TO A RIGHT UNDERSTANDING
WHEN THEY HAD SET THEMSELVES OVER I OBSERVED THAT THE BOAT BEING GONE A GOOD WAY INTO THE CREEK AND AS IT WERE IN A HARBOR WITHIN THE LAND THEY TOOK ONE OF THE THREE MEN OUT OF HER TO GO ALONG WITH THEM AND LEFT ONLY TWO IN THE BOAT HAVING FASTENED HER TO THE STUMP OF A LITTLE TREE ON THE SHORE
FOR INDEED IT NEVER CAME INTO MY HEAD THAT I WAS NOW GOT AMONG PEOPLE OF MY OWN STATURE AND STRENGTH
ANOTHER TIME WALKING TO THE TOP OF A FRESH MOLEHILL I FELL TO MY NECK IN THE HOLE THROUGH WHICH THAT ANIMAL HAD CAST UP THE EARTH AND COINED SOME LIE NOT WORTH REMEMBERING TO EXCUSE MYSELF FOR SPOILING MY CLOTHES
I HAD ABOVE A BARREL AND A HALF OF POWDER LEFT
HIS FORBEARING AT PRESENT TO DELIVER THEM IS ON PURPOSE TO TRY THEIR LOVE WHETHER THEY WILL CLEAVE TO HIM TO THE END
AND A GREAT VIVACITY AND SPARKLING SHARPNESS IN HIS EYES
AND WHO KNOWS BUT THAT EVEN THIS PRODIGIOUS RACE OF MORTALS MIGHT BE EQUALLY OVERMATCHED IN SOME DISTANT PART OF THE WORLD WHEREOF WE HAVE YET NO DISCOVERY
UNDER THIS ASSUMED CHARACTER HE GRADUALLY CONVEYED A GREAT MANY SORTS OF RICH STUFFS AND FINE LINEN TO HIS LODGING FROM THE CAVERN BUT WITH ALL THE NECESSARY PRECAUTIONS TO CONCEAL THE PLACE WHENCE HE BROUGHT THEM
FOUR NEIGHBORS CARRIED THE CORPSE TO THE BURYING GROUND FOLLOWING THE IMAUN WHO RECITED SOME PRAYERS
AND THE DISINHERITED KNIGHT WAS FOR THE SECOND TIME NAMED CHAMPION OF THE DAY
THERE WAS A COLLECTION OF NEEDLES AND PINS FROM A FOOT TO HALF A YARD LONG
WHILE THESE THINGS WERE BEING DONE THE FORTY ROBBERS AGAIN VISITED THEIR RETREAT IN THE FOREST
WHEN THIS WAS DONE I WENT DOWN THE SHIP'S SIDE AND PULLING THEM TO ME I TIED FOUR OF THEM TOGETHER AT BOTH ENDS AS WELL AS I COULD IN THE FORM OF A RAFT AND LAYING TWO OR THREE SHORT PIECES OF PLANK UPON THEM CROSSWAYS I FOUND I COULD WALK UPON IT VERY WELL BUT THAT IT WAS NOT ABLE TO BEAR ANY GREAT WEIGHT THE PIECES BEING TOO LIGHT
THE SOUND OF THE VOICE HAD HOWEVER ALSO REACHED THE OLD MAN'S EARS
HOWEVER I WOULD NOT TRUST TO THE STRENGTH OF IT ANY MORE IN SUCH DANGEROUS ENTERPRISES
TO INVOKE YOUR PITY SAID THE LOVELY JEWESS WITH A VOICE SOMEWHAT TREMULOUS WITH EMOTION WOULD I AM AWARE BE AS USELESS AS I SHOULD HOLD IT MEAN
THERE'S THIRTY HEARTS THERE THAT WOULD HAVE SPENT THEIR LIFE-BLOOD ERE YE HAD SCRATCHED YOUR FINGER
BEFORE I WENT TO SLEEP I GAVE HIM TO UNDERSTAND THAT I HAD SOME VALUABLE FURNITURE IN MY BOX TOO GOOD TO BE LOST
EIGHT YEARS BEFORE BUNYAN'S BIRTH 74 PURITAN MEN AND 28 WOMEN MEMBERS OF DR ROBINSON'S CHURCH ESCAPED PERSECUTION BY SAILING IN THE MAYFLOWER AND LANDING AT PLYMOUTH ROCK
AND NOW WERE THESE TWO MEN AS TWERE IN HEAVEN BEFORE THEY CAME AT IT BEING SWALLOWED UP WITH THE SIGHT OF ANGELS AND WITH HEARING OF THEIR MELODIOUS NOTES
I THOUGHT MYSELF IN A DREAM AND COULD SCARCELY BELIEVE MYSELF OUT OF DANGER
SHE SPENT ALL THE NIGHT IN WEEPING
TOM SMITH TOM SMITH ANSWERED IMMEDIATELY IS THAT ROBINSON FOR IT SEEMS HE KNEW THE VOICE
EARLY THE NEXT MORNING THE MAGICIAN CALLED AGAIN FOR ALADDIN AND SAID HE WOULD TAKE HIM TO SPEND THAT DAY IN THE COUNTRY AND ON THE NEXT HE WOULD PURCHASE THE SHOP
LET EACH FRONT CONTAIN SIX WINDOWS AND LET THE LATTICES OF THESE EXCEPT ONE WHICH MUST BE LEFT UNFINISHED BE ENRICHED WITH DIAMONDS RUBIES AND EMERALDS SO THAT THEY SHALL EXCEED EVERYTHING OF THE KIND EVER SEEN IN THE WORLD
RASPE I HAD MARRIED A LADY OF GREAT BEAUTY WHO HAVING HEARD OF MY SPORTING EXPLOITS DESIRED A SHORT TIME AFTER OUR MARRIAGE TO GO OUT WITH ME ON A SHOOTING EXPEDITION
BY WHICH I PERCEIVED THAT THERE WAS SOME INDRAFT OF THE WATER AND CONSEQUENTLY I HOPED TO FIND SOME CREEK OR RIVER THERE WHICH I MIGHT MAKE USE OF AS A PORT TO GET TO LAND WITH MY CARGO
IT WAS A DEMAND TO SURRENDER THE PRISONERS WITHIN ONE HOUR FAILING WHICH THE CASTLE WOULD BE INSTANTLY BESIEGED
WE HAD SEVERAL SPARE YARDS AND TWO OR THREE LARGE SPARS OF WOOD AND A SPARE TOPMAST OR TWO IN THE SHIP
I AM SORRY I HAVE BROUGHT THEE OUT OF THE WAY AND THAT I HAVE PUT THEE INTO SUCH IMMINENT DANGER
MUCH ALARMED HE WENT SOFTLY DOWN INTO THE YARD AND GOING TO THE FIRST JAR WHILE ASKING THE ROBBER WHOM HE THOUGHT ALIVE IF HE WAS IN READINESS SMELLED THE HOT BOILED OIL WHICH SENT FORTH A STEAM OUT OF THE JAR
THEY RETIRED IN THE DAYTIME TO THEIR DENS WHERE THEY HID THEMSELVES FROM THE ROC THEIR ENEMY AND CAME OUT ONLY IN THE NIGHT
WHEN THIS ACTION WORTHY OF THE COURAGE OF MORGIANA WAS EXECUTED WITHOUT ANY NOISE AS SHE HAD PROJECTED SHE RETURNED INTO THE KITCHEN WITH THE EMPTY KETTLE
BUT RECOVERING HIMSELF INSTEAD OF INQUIRING HOW I CAME THITHER BEGAN TO QUARREL WITH ME AND ASKED WHY I STOLE HIS GOODS
LET IT SUFFICE TO INFORM HIM THAT IN OUR PASSAGE FROM THENCE TO THE EAST INDIES WE WERE DRIVEN BY A VIOLENT STORM TO THE NORTHWEST OF VAN DIEMEN'S LAND
I THEN TOOK UP A GREAT STONE AND SLEW HIM
I HIRED A HORSE AND GUIDE FOR FIVE SHILLINGS WHICH I BORROWED OF THE CAPTAIN
PRO-DI-GI-OUS THE KINDLY INTEREST OF MEG MERRILIES IN THE FATE OF BERTRAM DID NOT HOWEVER END HERE
I AM ONLY THE SLAVE OF THE RING AND NOT OF THE LAMP I COMMAND THEE THEN REPLIED ALADDIN BY THE POWER OF THE RING TO TRANSPORT ME TO THE SPOT WHERE MY PALACE STANDS IN WHAT PART OF THE WORLD SOEVER IT MAY BE THESE WORDS WERE NO SOONER OUT OF HIS MOUTH THAN THE GENIE TRANSPORTED HIM INTO AFRICA TO THE MIDST OF A LARGE PLAIN WHERE HIS PALACE STOOD AT NO GREAT DISTANCE FROM A CITY AND PLACING HIM EXACTLY UNDER THE WINDOW OF THE PRINCESS'S APARTMENT LEFT HIM
HE HAD WALKED FOR SOME DISTANCE WHEN HE STOPPED AT A SMALL PUBLIC-HOUSE TO PROCURE REFRESHMENT
THE FIRST JOLT HAD LIKE TO HAVE SHAKEN ME OUT OF MY HAMMOCK BUT AFTERWARD THE MOTION WAS EASY ENOUGH
I HAVE ALREADY OBSERVED HOW I BROUGHT ALL MY GOODS INTO THIS PALE AND INTO THE CAVE WHICH I HAD MADE BEHIND ME
AS I PERCEIVED HER COMING I CREPT CLOSE TO THE EGG SO THAT I HAD BEFORE ME ONE OF THE LEGS OF THE BIRD WHICH WAS AS BIG AS THE TRUNK OF A TREE
IT IS TO STAY WITH ME THAT YOU MAY EDIFY ME WITH YOUR WAY OF LIVING AND THAT I MAY LEARN FROM YOUR GOOD EXAMPLE PRINCESS SAID THE COUNTERFEIT FATIMA I BEG OF YOU NOT TO ASK WHAT I CANNOT CONSENT TO WITHOUT NEGLECTING MY PRAYERS AND DEVOTION THAT SHALL BE NO HINDRANCE TO YOU ANSWERED THE PRINCESS
BUT AS GOD WOULD HAVE IT WHILE APOLLYON WAS FETCHING OF HIS LAST BLOW THEREBY TO MAKE A FULL END OF THIS GOOD MAN CHRISTIAN NIMBLY STRETCHED OUT HIS HAND FOR HIS SWORD AND CAUGHT IT SAYING REJOICE NOT AGAINST ME O MINE ENEMY
BUT I NEVER WENT OUT OF THE SHIP TILL WE CAME INTO THE DOWNS WHICH WAS ON THE THIRD DAY OF JUNE 1706 ABOUT NINE MONTHS AFTER MY ESCAPE
ALADDIN WHO HAD NEVER BEEN USED TO SUCH TRAFFIC TOLD HIM HE WOULD TRUST TO HIS JUDGMENT AND HONOR
WHEN HE WAS COME UP TO CHRISTIAN HE BEHELD HIM WITH A DISDAINFUL COUNTENANCE AND THUS BEGAN TO QUESTION WITH HIM
NOW GUY MANNERING HIMSELF AMONGST OTHER ACCOMPLISHMENTS POSSESSED A KNOWLEDGE OF THE STARS
I WOULD SOMETIMES LIE DOWN AND LET FIVE OR SIX OF THEM DANCE ON MY HAND
IN ORDER TO DISPOSE OF THE MERCHANDISE WHEN HE HAD THUS AMASSED THEM TOGETHER HE TOOK A WAREHOUSE WHICH HAPPENED TO BE OPPOSITE TO CASSIM'S WHICH ALI BABA'S SON HAD OCCUPIED SINCE THE DEATH OF HIS UNCLE
GLUMDALCLITCH WAS PREVAILED ON TO BE OF THE COMPANY VERY MUCH AGAINST HER INCLINATION FOR SHE WAS NATURALLY TENDER HEARTED
HOWEVER I MADE A SHIFT TO CREEP ON ALL FOURS AND SHELTER MYSELF BY LYING FLAT ON MY FACE ON THE LEE-SIDE OF A BORDER OF LEMON-THYME
NEXT MORNING AS SOON AS THE SUN WAS UP WE EXPLORED THE ISLAND AND SAW SOME HOUSES WHICH WE APPROACHED
GOD BLESS YOU WITH ALL HAPPINESS AND PROSPERITY
THEREFORE JUDGE HOW I SHOULD FEEL AT YOUR TABLE IF THAT IS THE ONLY REASON SAID ALI BABA IT OUGHT NOT TO DEPRIVE ME OF THE HONOR OF YOUR COMPANY
YOU'VE MISSED YOUR BLOW YE BLOOD SPILLER
SHE SEVERELY REPRIMANDED THE GARDENER ON ACCOUNT OF HIS DOG
BUT THE PRINCIPAL DIFFICULTY WAS TO RAISE AND PLACE ME IN THIS VEHICLE
BUT AMONG US ALL WE CANNOT FURNISH JEWELS ENOUGH FOR SO GREAT A WORK I HAVE MORE THAN ARE NECESSARY SAID THE SULTAN
AND NOW I BEGAN TO APPLY MYSELF TO MAKE SUCH NECESSARY THINGS AS I FOUND I MOST WANTED PARTICULARLY A CHAIR AND A TABLE
ON THE THIRD DAY HE WANDERED INTO THE COUNTRY AND AS HE WAS APPROACHING A RIVER HE FELL DOWN THE BANK WITH SO MUCH VIOLENCE THAT HE RUBBED THE RING WHICH THE MAGICIAN HAD GIVEN HIM SO HARD BY HOLDING ON THE ROCK TO SAVE HIMSELF THAT IMMEDIATELY THE SAME GENIE APPEARED WHOM HE HAD SEEN IN THE CAVE WHERE THE MAGICIAN HAD LEFT HIM
CASSIM'S WIFE CONSIDERING HOW MUCH IT CONCERNED HER HUSBAND TO KEEP THE BUSINESS SECRET WAS THE MORE EASILY PERSUADED TO BELIEVE HER BROTHER-IN-LAW
UNWILLING TO BE FOUND ENGAGED IN HIS HELLISH OCCUPATION THE SAVAGE BARON GAVE THE SLAVES A SIGNAL TO RESTORE ISAAC'S GARMENT AND HASTILY QUITTED THE DUNGEON WITH HIS ATTENDANTS
WHO AS I WAS HIS CREATURE HAD AN UNDOUBTED RIGHT BY CREATION TO GOVERN AND DISPOSE OF ME ABSOLUTELY AS HE THOUGHT FIT
THEY WERE JUST GOING INTO THE BOAT WHEN FRIDAY AND THE MATE HALLOOED
THE SULTAN'S DAUGHTER WHO WAS PROMISED ME AS MY BRIDE IS THIS NIGHT MARRIED TO THE SON OF THE GRAND VIZIER
AND REACHING ONE OF HIS PAWS IN AT THE DOOR AS A CAT DOES WHEN SHE PLAYS WITH A MOUSE ALTHOUGH I OFTEN SHIFTED PLACE TO AVOID HIM HE AT LENGTH SEIZED THE LAPPET OF MY COAT WHICH BEING MADE OF THAT COUNTRY SILK WAS VERY THICK AND STRONG AND DRAGGED ME OUT
I FELLED A CEDAR-TREE AND I QUESTION MUCH WHETHER SOLOMON EVER HAD SUCH A ONE FOR THE BUILDING OF THE TEMPLE OF JERUSALEM
THE MANIAC FIGURE OF ULRICA WAS FOR A LONG TIME VISIBLE ON THE LOFTY STAND SHE HAD CHOSEN TOSSING HER ARMS ABROAD WITH WILD EXULTATION
HE REACHED THE VILLAGE AT LENGTH AND ENGAGED A ROOM AT THE GORDON ARMS A COMFORTABLE INN KEPT BY A MRS MAC-CANDLISH
THE LAIRD AND HIS SERVANTS RUSHED AWAY TO THE WOOD OF WARROCH
I EMBARKED IN A VESSEL THAT HAPPILY ARRIVED AT BUSSORAH
FEW OF THEM ASKED QUARTER NONE RECEIVED IT
LET HIM LOOK TO HIS BOND SAID SHYLOCK LET HIM LOOK TO HIS BOND MEANWHILE BASSANIO HAD REACHED BELMONT AND HAD VISITED THE FAIR PORTIA
AND THE TWO WERE ABOUT TO HASTEN AWAY FOR THE PURPOSE OF PROCURING AID WHEN A THIRD PERSON SUDDENLY APPEARED AND COMMANDED THEM BOTH TO HALT
THIS ENVOY HAD INSTRUCTIONS TO REPRESENT TO THE MONARCH OF BLEFUSCU THE GREAT LENITY OF HIS MASTER WHO WAS CONTENT TO PUNISH ME NO FURTHER THAN WITH THE LOSS OF MY EYES
THE DOG FOLLOWING THE SCENT CAME DIRECTLY UP AND TAKING ME IN HIS MOUTH RAN STRAIGHT TO HIS MASTER WAGGING HIS TAIL AND SET ME GENTLY ON THE GROUND
AND WITH THAT HE GAVE A DESPERATE STRUGGLE OR TWO AND GOT OUT OF THE MIRE ON THAT SIDE OF THE SLOUGH WHICH WAS NEXT TO HIS OWN HOUSE
AFTER WHICH I WAS QUITE IN THE DARK FOR ANOTHER MINUTE AND THEN MY BOX BEGAN TO RISE SO HIGH THAT I COULD SEE LIGHT FROM THE TOPS OF THE WINDOWS
THE WHOLE STORY AND CIRCUMSTANCES OF WHICH I SHALL FAITHFULLY RELATE
THE DOMINIE BELIEVING SHE WAS SOME SORCERESS ADDRESSED HER IN LATIN BUT THE GIPSY QUEEN ANGRILY INTERRUPTED HIM
AT NIGHT WE WENT TO SLEEP ON THE SEA-SHORE
WITH THAT HE LOOKED UGLY UPON THEM AND RUSHING TO THEM HAD DOUBTLESS MADE AN END OF THEM HIMSELF BUT THAT HE FELL INTO ONE OF HIS FITS FOR HE SOMETIMES IN SUN-SHINE WEATHER FELL INTO FITS AND LOST FOR A TIME THE USE OF HIS HAND
THE FEAR OF DEATH UNDER WHICH I LABORED TURNED ALL MY FOOD INTO POISON
ON THESE CONDITIONS I AM READY TO BESTOW THE PRINCESS MY DAUGHTER UPON HIM
5TH
UNSCATHED BY THE LANCE OF HIS ENEMY HE HAD DIED A VICTIM TO THE VIOLENCE OF HIS OWN CONTENDING PASSIONS
HE HAD AN ONLY SON WILFRED BY NAME WITH WHOM HE HAD QUARRELLED
THEREFORE I HAVE SHUT MYSELF OUT OF ALL THE PROMISES AND THERE NOW REMAINS TO ME NOTHING BUT THREATNINGS DREADFUL THREATNINGS FEARFUL THREATNINGS OF CERTAIN JUDGMENT AND FIERY INDIGNATION WHICH SHALL DEVOUR ME AS AN ADVERSARY
AND EVEN THE PRESIDENT OF THE ESTABLISHMENT DID NOT HESITATE TO AID IN PROCURING FALSE EVIDENCE AGAINST THE UNFORTUNATE JEWESS FOR THE PURPOSE OF INGRATIATING HIMSELF WITH BEAUMANOIR FROM WHOM HE HAD KEPT SECRET THE PRESENCE OF REBECCA IN THE HOLY PRECINCTS
THE SHIP SLACKENED HER SAILS AND I CAME UP WITH HER BETWEEN FIVE AND SIX IN THE EVENING SEPTEMBER 26TH
AND AS I SLEPT I DREAMED A DREAM
HAVING THUS PREPARED ALL THINGS AS WELL AS I WAS ABLE I SET SAIL ON THE TWENTY-FOURTH DAY OF SEPTEMBER 1701 AT SIX IN THE MORNING
KNOW ME THEN FROM HENCEFORTH SAID THE BLACK KNIGHT AS RICHARD PLANTAGENET
I DESIRE NO RECOMPENSE ANSWERED HIS FELLOW TRAVELLER
AND THE COMPARISON OF PHAETON WAS SO OBVIOUS THAT HE COULD NOT FORBEAR APPLYING IT ALTHOUGH I DID NOT MUCH ADMIRE THE CONCEIT
NEITHER IS THAT AT ALL TO BE WONDERED AT BECAUSE NATURE IN THAT COUNTRY OBSERVING THE SAME PROPORTION THROUGH ALL HER OPERATIONS A HAILSTONE IS NEAR EIGHTEEN HUNDRED TIMES AS LARGE AS ONE IN EUROPE
THE CONSEQUENCE OF WHICH THEY MUST NEEDS KNOW WOULD BE THE GALLOWS
THE FAITHFUL SERVANT AT ONCE SUGGESTED THAT HIS MASTER SHOULD CHANGE GARMENTS WITH HIM AND SO MAKE HIS ESCAPE
I WADED WITH WHAT HASTE I COULD AND SWAM IN THE MIDDLE ABOUT THIRTY YARDS TILL I FELT GROUND
BUT THAT WHICH COMFORTED ME MORE STILL WAS THAT LAST OF ALL AFTER I HAD MADE FIVE OR SIX SUCH VOYAGES AS THESE AND THOUGHT I HAD NOTHING MORE TO EXPECT FROM THE SHIP THAT WAS WORTH MY MEDDLING WITH--I SAY AFTER ALL THIS I FOUND A GREAT HOGSHEAD OF BREAD THREE LARGE RUNLETS OF RUM OR SPIRITS A BOX OF SUGAR AND A BARREL OF FINE FLOUR
HE GAVE ME A BOW AND ARROWS AND TAKING ME BEHIND HIM ON AN ELEPHANT CARRIED ME TO A THICK FOREST SOME LEAGUES FROM THE TOWN
I KEPT AMONG OTHER LITTLE NECESSARIES A PAIR OF SPECTACLES IN A PRIVATE POCKET WHICH AS I OBSERVED BEFORE HAD ESCAPED THE EMPEROR'S SEARCHERS
WHERE IT WAS OPPOSED BY NONE EXCEPT SKYRESH BOLGOLAM WHO WAS PLEASED WITHOUT ANY PROVOCATION TO BE MY MORTAL ENEMY
GO TO THE BARBICAN SAID THE VICTOR IN A TONE OF AUTHORITY AND WAIT THERE MY FURTHER ORDERS YET FIRST LET ME SAY SAID DE BRACY WHAT IT IMPORTS THEE TO KNOW
ALI BABA DID NOT VISIT THE ROBBERS CAVE FOR A WHOLE YEAR AS HE SUPPOSED THE OTHER TWO MIGHT BE ALIVE
I SPENT THE DAY IN WALKING ABOUT IN THE VALLEY RESTING MYSELF AT TIMES IN SUCH PLACES AS I THOUGHT MOST CONVENIENT
WE HAD VERY GOOD WEATHER ONLY EXCESSIVELY HOT ALL THE WAY UPON OUR OWN COAST TILL WE CAME TO THE HEIGHT OF CAPE ST AUGUSTINO
I TOLD MY WIFE SHE HAD BEEN TOO THRIFTY FOR I FOUND SHE HAD STARVED HERSELF AND DAUGHTER TO NOTHING
SHE IS THE ADMIRATION OF THE WHOLE TOWN FOR HER FASTING HER AUSTERITIES AND HER EXEMPLARY LIFE
SIRE I PRAY YOU TO LET ME KNOW THE CRIME BY WHICH I HAVE THUS LOST THE FAVOR OF THY COUNTENANCE YOUR CRIME ANSWERED THE SULTAN WRETCHED MAN
BUT NONE COULD GUESS WHO HE MIGHT BE
THEN BIDDING THEM GOOD-BYE HE STARTED TO FOLLOW MEG MERRILIES ACCOMPANIED BY DINMONT WHO HAD COME UP A FEW MINUTES BEFORE
THEREFORE TO HIM LET ME GIVE LASTING PRAISE AND THANK AND BLESS HIS HOLY NAME ALWAYS
GABRIEL THE HUNTSMAN ON THE MOORS HE SAID HAD INFORMED HIM IN A MYSTERIOUS WAY THAT BERTRAM WAS IN GAOL AND THAT HE WAS BADLY IN NEED OF A GOOD FRIEND TO STAY WITH HIM NIGHT AND DAY FOR A DAY OR TWO
I WENT UP THE SHORE AND DOWN THE SHORE BUT IT WAS ALL ONE
I WAS NOT ABLE TO LIFT UP THE ROOF OF MY CLOSET WHICH OTHERWISE I CERTAINLY SHOULD HAVE DONE AND SAT ON THE TOP OF IT
AT LENGTH I TOLD THEM THERE WOULD BE NOTHING DONE IN MY OPINION TILL NIGHT
AFTER LISTENING FOR SOME TIME I VENTURED TO RAISE MY HEAD AND LOOK ROUND WHEN TO MY UNSPEAKABLE JOY I PERCEIVED THE LION HAD BY THE EAGERNESS WITH WHICH HE SPRANG AT ME JUMPED FORWARD AS I FELL INTO THE CROCODILE'S MOUTH
THEREFORE WITHOUT SHOWING THE LEAST SURPRISE OR TROUBLE HE CONFESSED ALL AND OFFERED HIS BROTHER PART OF HIS TREASURE TO KEEP THE SECRET
IT WAS THE KNIGHT OF IVANHOE
THINK ON THY SINS IT SAID REGINALD FRONT-DE-BOEUF
WHAT SAID SHE HAS ALI BABA GOLD SO PLENTIFUL AS TO MEASURE IT
FOR WHY SAID HE SHOULD YOU CHUSE LIFE SEEING IT IS ATTENDED WITH SO MUCH BITTERNESS
FOR BESIDES THAT MY AGE NOW REQUIRED REST I WAS RESOLVED NO MORE TO EXPOSE MYSELF TO SUCH RISKS AS I HAD ENCOUNTERED SO THAT I THOUGHT OF NOTHING BUT TO PASS THE REST OF MY DAYS IN TRANQUILLITY
WOULD YOU DESTROY THIS FINE OLD CASTLE SIR HIS FACE PERSON AND VOICE WERE SO EXACTLY LIKE THOSE OF HIS FATHER WHEN ALIVE THAT GLOSSIN ALMOST BELIEVED THAT THE GRAVE HAD GIVEN UP ITS DEAD
WHERE A LITTLE CONTEMPTIBLE VARLET WITHOUT THE LEAST TITLE TO BIRTH PERSON WIT OR COMMON-SENSE SHALL PRESUME TO LOOK WITH IMPORTANCE AND PUT HIMSELF UPON A FOOT WITH THE GREATEST PERSONS OF THE KINGDOM
THERE ARE MANY SORTS OF TRADES
SHE ONLY CAST AT HIM A SORROWFUL LOOK EXPRESSIVE OF GREAT AFFLICTION
AND HE FOUND HIMSELF ALONE WITH THE FORMER PARTNER OF HIS GUILT
AT THIS ALARMING SPECTACLE I CONTINUED IMMOVABLE AND WAS SO MUCH TERRIFIED THAT MY BOW AND ARROWS FELL OUT OF MY HAND
A SHEPHERD AND SHEPHERDESS WHO HAD BEEN FRIENDS WITH ROSALIND WHEN SHE WAS HERSELF DISGUISED AS A SHEPHERD WERE MARRIED ON THE SAME DAY AND ALL WITH SUCH PRETTY FEASTINGS AND MERRY-MAKINGS AS COULD BE NOWHERE WITHIN FOUR WALLS BUT ONLY IN THE BEAUTIFUL GREEN WOOD
AS SOON AS I HAD FINISHED THEY TOLD ME BY THE PERSON WHO SPOKE ARABIC AND INTERPRETED TO THEM WHAT I SAID THAT I MUST GO ALONG WITH THEM AND TELL MY STORY TO THEIR KING MYSELF
THAT IF THEY DID THEY WOULD BE FETCHED INTO THE CASTLE AND BE LAID IN IRONS
BUT OUR MEN HAD THE START OF HIM HALF A LEAGUE AND THE SEA THEREABOUT BEING FULL OF SHARP-POINTED ROCKS THE MONSTER WAS NOT ABLE TO OVERTAKE THE BOAT
OFTEN POINTING FORWARDS WHICH AS I AFTERWARDS FOUND WAS TOWARDS THE CAPITAL CITY ABOUT HALF A MILE DISTANT WHITHER IT WAS AGREED BY HIS MAJESTY IN COUNCIL THAT I MUST BE CONVEYED
AS HE WANDERED THROUGH THE FOREST A DOG WHICH HE RECOGNISED JUMPED UP AND FAWNED UPON HIM AND GURTH THE SWINEHERD SHORTLY AFTER MADE HIS APPEARANCE
BUT HIS ATTENTION AND THAT OF THE OTHER SPECTATORS WAS ARRESTED BY THE SOUND OF A SOLITARY TRUMPET WHICH BREATHED A NOTE OF DEFIANCE FROM THE NORTHERN END OF THE ENCLOSURE
THE CHAINS THAT HELD MY LEFT LEG WERE ABOUT TWO YARDS LONG AND GAVE ME NOT ONLY THE LIBERTY OF WALKING BACKWARDS AND FORWARDS IN A SEMICIRCLE BUT BEING FIXED WITHIN FOUR INCHES OF THE GATE ALLOWED ME TO CREEP IN AND LIE AT MY FULL LENGTH IN THE TEMPLE
THE SON OF THE BLESSED IS VERY PITIFUL
AT THE SAME TIME I HEARD THE REAPERS NOT ABOVE A HUNDRED YARDS BEHIND ME
WHILE HE WAS ENGAGED IN CONVERSATION WITH MISS BERTRAM AND HER COMPANION A VOICE WAS HEARD CLOSE BY WHICH LUCY AT ONCE RECOGNISED AS THAT OF HER FATHER'S ENEMY GLOSSIN AND SHE SENT THE DOMINIE TO KEEP HIM AWAY
I ASSURED HIM THAT HE MUST BE MISTAKEN BY ALMOST HALF FOR I HAD NOT LEFT THE COUNTRY WHENCE I CAME ABOVE TWO HOURS BEFORE I DROPPED INTO THE SEA
AND THE LADY ROWENA THE JEW AND HIS DAUGHTER EXPERIENCED THE SAME MISFORTUNE
THE BED WAS EIGHT YARDS FROM THE FLOOR
GULLIVER IS SHIPWRECKED AND SWIMS FOR HIS LIFE BY JONATHAN SWIFT MY FATHER HAD A SMALL ESTATE IN NOTTINGHAMSHIRE
OR THE WONDERFUL LAMP THERE ONCE LIVED IN ONE OF THE LARGE AND RICH CITIES OF CHINA A TAILOR NAMED MUSTAPHA
AND HE WAS RECOGNISED BESIDES AS THE MOST TYRANNICAL OPPRESSOR OF THE JEWISH PEOPLE
AND THE NEXT DAY ALADDIN WHO COULD NOT BEAR THE THOUGHT OF HUNGER PUTTING ONE OF THE SILVER DISHES UNDER HIS VEST WENT OUT EARLY TO SELL IT AND ADDRESSING HIMSELF TO A JEW WHOM HE MET IN THE STREETS TOOK HIM ASIDE AND PULLING OUT THE PLATE ASKED HIM IF HE WOULD BUY IT
EMBRACE THY RELIGION AND WHAT RELIGION CAN IT BE THAT HARBOURS SUCH A VILLAIN
I WAS A FOOL THAT I DID NOT TRY TO DO IT BEFORE
IT IS A COMFORT FOR ME TO FIND AS IT WERE MY BROTHER IN A SON WHO HAS HIS MOST REMARKABLE FEATURES THE AFRICAN MAGICIAN PERCEIVING THAT THE WIDOW WEPT AT THE REMEMBRANCE OF HER HUSBAND CHANGED THE CONVERSATION AND TURNING TOWARD HER SON ASKED HIM WHAT BUSINESS DO YOU FOLLOW
THE CHARACTERS OF THIS LETTER WERE OF AZURE AND THE CONTENTS AS FOLLOWS
GULLIVER LEAVES LILLIPUT BY JONATHAN SWIFT THREE DAYS AFTER MY ARRIVAL WALKING OUT OF CURIOSITY TO THE NORTHEAST COAST OF THE ISLAND I OBSERVED ABOUT HALF A LEAGUE OFF IN THE SEA SOMEWHAT THAT LOOKED LIKE A BOAT OVERTURNED
OR BUT HE MAY IN SHORT TIME HAVE ANOTHER OF HIS FITS BEFORE US AND MAY LOSE THE USE OF HIS LIMBS
THUS SINDBAD FINISHED THE STORY OF HIS THIRD VOYAGE
I COULD HANG DRAW GIVE LIBERTY AND TAKE IT AWAY AND NO REBELS AMONG ALL MY SUBJECTS
IVANHOE WAS SOON ON FOOT HASTENING TO MEND HIS FORTUNE WITH HIS SWORD
ALL THE REMEDY THAT OFFERED TO MY THOUGHTS AT THAT TIME WAS TO GET UP INTO A THICK BUSHY TREE LIKE A FIR BUT THORNY WHICH GREW NEAR ME AND WHERE I RESOLVED TO SIT ALL NIGHT AND CONSIDER THE NEXT DAY WHAT DEATH I SHOULD DIE FOR AS YET I SAW NO PROSPECT OF LIFE
AND BEFORE I SHOW IT ALL TO YOU TELL ME FIRST WHAT YOU THINK OF THIS HALL UPON THIS QUESTION THE COUNTERFEIT FATIMA SURVEYED THE HALL FROM ONE END TO THE OTHER
WE HAD ON BOARD NO LARGE CARGO OF GOODS EXCEPT OF SUCH TOYS AS WERE FIT FOR OUR TRADE WITH THE NEGROES SUCH AS BEADS BITS OF GLASS SHELLS AND OTHER TRIFLES ESPECIALLY LITTLE LOOKING-GLASSES KNIVES SCISSORS HATCHETS AND THE LIKE
AND I MADE NO DOUBT WE SHOULD BE ABLE TO DEAL WELL ENOUGH WITH THE TEN THAT WERE COMING CONSIDERING THAT THE CAPTAIN HAD SAID THERE WERE THREE OR FOUR HONEST MEN AMONG THEM ALSO

BUT LIKE MANY MORE OF THE CONQUERED ENGLISH PEOPLE HE HAD FELT THE TYRANNY AND OPPRESSIVE INSOLENCE OF THE HAUGHTY NORMAN BARONS
FAREWELL AND SO SAYING THE TEMPLAR LEFT THE APARTMENT
I HAD SEPARATED MYSELF SOMEWHAT FROM MY COMPANIONS WHEN IN THE OPENING OF A BEAUTIFUL GLADE I BEHELD A NOBLE STAG WITH A FINE FULL-GROWN CHERRY-TREE ABOVE TEN FEET HIGH BETWEEN HIS ANTLERS
MY GREATEST APPREHENSION WAS FOR MINE EYES WHICH I SHOULD HAVE INFALLIBLY LOST IF I HAD NOT SUDDENLY THOUGHT OF AN EXPEDIENT
THEN HIS HORSE
NOW IT SO HAPPENED THAT COLONEL MANNERING ARRIVED AT THE VILLAGE OF KIPPLETRINGAN A DAY OR TWO BEFORE THE TIME AT WHICH THE SALE OF ELLANGOWAN WAS TO TAKE PLACE
AND WHAT HEART COULD FORBEAR TO BLESS HIM WHO HAD NOT ONLY IN A MIRACULOUS MANNER PROVIDED FOR ME IN SUCH A WILDERNESS AND IN SUCH A DESOLATE CONDITION BUT FROM WHOM EVERY DELIVERANCE MUST ALWAYS BE ACKNOWLEDGED TO PROCEED
HAVING KNOCKED THIS FELLOW DOWN THE OTHER WHO PURSUED HIM STOPPED AS IF HE HAD BEEN FRIGHTENED AND I ADVANCED TOWARDS HIM
AND THAT IT WAS MY BUSINESS TO BE GONE BEFORE THE TIDE OF FLOOD BEGAN OTHERWISE I MIGHT NOT BE ABLE TO REACH THE SHORE AT ALL
WHEN THE CAPTAIN SAW THEM ALL READY HE PUT HIMSELF AT THEIR HEAD AND THEY RETURNED THE WAY THEY HAD COME
WHEN MANNERING ARRIVED AT MR MERVYN'S HE SAID VERY LITTLE ABOUT THE INFORMATION WHICH HAD BEEN THE CAUSE OF HIS RETURN
OUR COURSE WAS EAST NORTHEAST THE WIND WAS AT SOUTHWEST
MY SON SAID SHE YOU MAY REJOICE YOU ARE ARRIVED AT THE HEIGHT OF YOUR DESIRES
BECAUSE THE HOUR AND THE MAN ARE BOTH COME AT THE APPOINTED SIGNAL BERTRAM AND HIS COMPANIONS RUSHED UPON HATTERAICK
I LOOKED I THOUGHT LIKE SAUL WHO COMPLAINED NOT ONLY THAT THE PHILISTINES WERE UPON HIM BUT THAT GOD HAD FORSAKEN HIM
IN HIS TERROR AT THE THOUGHT OF LOSING HIS PROPERTY AT ELLANGOWAN IF IT CAME TO BE KNOWN THAT HARRY BERTRAM WAS ALIVE YET AT ALL TIMES FERTILE IN EVERY KIND OF VILLAINOUS DEVICE GLOSSIN NOW HIT UPON A NEW PLAN TO GET RID OF THE MAN WHO STOOD BETWEEN HIM AND HIS PEACE OF MIND
ALL THIS TIME THE POOR MAN WAS IN AS GREAT AN ECSTASY AS I ONLY NOT UNDER ANY SURPRISE AS I WAS AND HE SAID A THOUSAND KIND AND TENDER THINGS TO ME TO COMPOSE AND BRING ME TO MYSELF
WHEN HE HAD MADE AN END OF HIS STORY HE CHARMED HER INTO SLEEP FOR ARIEL WAS AT HAND AND HE HAD WORK FOR HIM TO DO
WHEN THIS WAS DONE ALI BABA HID THE JARS AND WEAPONS
SOME OF THEM WERE EXCEEDING GLAD AND LOOKED UPWARD
WHEN AT LENGTH HE BEGAN TO COME TO HIMSELF OUT OF HIS AGONY OF TERROR HE SAID THAT HE HAD HIRED A BODY-GUARD OF SIX MEN AT ASHBY TOGETHER WITH MULES FOR CARRYING THE LITTER OF A SICK FRIEND
IT WAS ABOUT TWELVE AT NOON AND A SERVANT BROUGHT IN DINNER
LET ITS WALLS BE MASSIVE GOLD AND SILVER BRICKS LAID ALTERNATELY
THE LIFE THAT WE NOW LIVE IS MISERABLE
AND ACCORDINGLY THE SHIP BEING FITTED OUT AND THE CARGO FURNISHED AND ALL THINGS DONE AS BY AGREEMENT BY MY PARTNERS IN THE VOYAGE I WENT ON BOARD IN AN EVIL HOUR THE LST OF SEPTEMBER 1659 BEING THE SAME DAY EIGHT YEARS THAT I WENT FROM MY FATHER AND MOTHER AT HULL
AND THAT INDEED THERE WAS LITTLE LEFT IN HER THAT I WAS ABLE TO BRING AWAY IF I HAD HAD MORE TIME
IN A LITTLE TIME I BEGAN TO SPEAK TO HIM AND TEACH HIM TO SPEAK TO ME
ALL THAT I COULD DO WAS TO WAIT TILL THE TIDE WAS AT THE HIGHEST KEEPING THE RAFT WITH MY OAR LIKE AN ANCHOR TO HOLD THE SIDE OF IT FAST TO THE SHORE NEAR A FLAT PIECE OF GROUND WHICH I EXPECTED THE WATER WOULD FLOW OVER
SHE HAD A LIGHT SAPLING IN HER HAND AND AS THE LAIRD LOOKED UP TO WHERE SHE STOOD SHE SAID TO HIM
SO RIDE YOUR WAY FOR THESE ARE THE LAST WORDS YE'LL EVER HEAR MEG MERRILIES SPEAK AND THIS IS THE LAST TWIG THAT I'LL EVER CUT IN THE BONNY WOODS OF ELLANGOWAN AND HAVING UTTERED THIS DARK AND THREATENING SPEECH SHE TURNED CONTEMPTUOUSLY FROM HIM TO JOIN HER COMRADES IN MISFORTUNE
BUT I WAS SOON RELIEVED BY ONE OF OUR SERVANTS WHO WRUNG OFF THE BIRD'S NECK AND I HAD HIM NEXT DAY FOR DINNER BY THE QUEEN'S COMMAND
ACCORDINGLY AS SOON AS WOODBOURNE WAS MADE READY TO RECEIVE THEM THE COLONEL AND HIS DAUGHTER JULIA TOOK UP THEIR RESIDENCE THERE AND LUCY BERTRAM BECAME THEIR GUEST
I PROSTRATED MYSELF A SECOND TIME AND RISING AGAIN SAID COMMANDER OF THE FAITHFUL I CAN ASSURE YOUR MAJESTY HE DOTH NOT EXCEED THE TRUTH
A RAPID CURRENT CARRIES THE SHIP ALONG WITH IT AND WE SHALL ALL PERISH IN LESS THAN A QUARTER OF AN HOUR
BUT THE EAGERNESS OF MY FANCY PREVAILED AND TO WORK I WENT
BUT LET ME NOW RELATE THAT WHICH HAPPENED TO MYSELF SOME LITTLE TIME AGO
BUT DISCOVERING A LEAK WE UNSHIPPED OUR GOODS AND WINTERED THERE
SHE KNEW THAT IF SHE TOLD DEMETRIUS THAT HERMIA WAS GOING AS SHE WAS TO THE WOOD OUTSIDE ATHENS HE WOULD FOLLOW HER AND I CAN FOLLOW HIM AND AT LEAST I SHALL SEE HIM SHE SAID TO HERSELF
FAREWELL FRONT-DE-BOEUF
AND AMONG THOSE THAT DID SO THERE WERE TWO THAT RESOLVED TO FETCH HIM BACK BY FORCE
THE BOAT WHICH WAS A LARGE ONE DREW NEARER AND NEARER AND AS IT REACHED THE LAND SOME TWENTY MEN JUMPED ON SHORE AND DISAPPEARED UP A DARK PASSAGE WHICH DIVIDED THE PRISON FROM THE CUSTOM-HOUSE
AT LAST HE LAYS HIS HEAD FLAT UPON THE GROUND CLOSE TO MY FOOT AND SETS MY OTHER FOOT UPON HIS HEAD AS HE HAD DONE BEFORE
ARE YOU OF ANY TRADE AT THIS QUESTION THE YOUTH HUNG DOWN HIS HEAD AND WAS NOT A LITTLE ABASHED WHEN HIS MOTHER ANSWERED ALADDIN IS AN IDLE FELLOW
WE PASSED BY SEVERAL ISLANDS AND AT LAST ARRIVED AT BUSSORAH FROM WHENCE I CAME TO THIS CITY WITH THE VALUE OF 100,000 SEQUINS
THE CEREMONIES OF MARRIAGE BEING OVER I WENT AND DWELT WITH MY WIFE AND FOR SOME TIME WE LIVED TOGETHER IN PERFECT HARMONY
SOME BORE FRUIT ENTIRELY WHITE AND SOME CLEAR AND TRANSPARENT AS CRYSTAL
SHE PAUSED IN HER SINGING AND BROWN HEARD A FEW DEEP GROANS COME FROM THE DYING MAN
AS THE PRINCE ASSUMED HIS THRONE HE GAVE SIGNAL TO THE HERALDS TO PROCLAIM THE LAWS OF THE TOURNAMENT WHICH WERE BRIEFLY AS FOLLOWS

HOW SHE SAVED HIS LIFE FROM SMUGGLERS WHO WOULD HAVE MURDERED HIM

WILFRED PLACING HIS FOOT ON HIS BREAST AND THE SWORD'S POINT TO HIS THROAT COMMANDED HIM TO YIELD HIM OR DIE ON THE SPOT
BY THIS MEANS I SAY WE HAD A FULL VIEW OF THEM AND THE CAPTAIN KNEW THE PERSONS AND CHARACTERS OF ALL THE MEN IN THE BOAT OF WHOM BE SAID THERE WERE THREE VERY HONEST FELLOWS WHO HE WAS SURE WERE LED INTO THIS CONSPIRACY BY THE REST BEING OVERPOWERED AND FRIGHTENED
THEY BEGAN TO CUT THAT FIRST
HE WENT THROUGH THEM WITH ALL THE PRECAUTION THE FEAR OF DEATH COULD INSPIRE CROSSED THE GARDEN WITHOUT STOPPING TOOK DOWN THE LAMP FROM THE NICHE THREW OUT THE WICK AND THE LIQUOR AND AS THE MAGICIAN HAD DESIRED PUT IT IN HIS WAISTBAND

FOR MY PART I ALWAYS BELIEVED AND HAVE HEARD SAY IT WANTED NOTHING
HE SLEPT THUS TILL MORNING

THEY GAVE US THAT HERB AT FIRST ON PURPOSE TO DEPRIVE US OF OUR SENSES THAT WE MIGHT NOT BE AWARE OF THE SAD DESTINY PREPARED FOR US
UPON THIS HE SPOKE SOME WORDS TO ME AND THOUGH I COULD NOT UNDERSTAND THEM YET I THOUGHT THEY WERE PLEASANT TO HEAR FOR THEY WERE THE FIRST SOUND OF A MAN'S VOICE THAT I HAD HEARD MY OWN EXCEPTED FOR ABOVE TWENTY-FIVE YEARS
I ALSO ENCOURAGED THEM BY TELLING THEM THAT IF IT LAY IN MY POWER TO SEND ANY VESSEL TO TAKE THEM IN I WOULD NOT FORGET THEM
HE WITH DIFFICULTY SUPPRESSED A SHOUT AND WAS MUCH RELIEVED WHEN HE HEARD A VOICE BEHIND HIM SAY
BY THIS MEANS ALL HER QUARTER WAS FREE AND ALL THAT WAS IN THAT PART WAS DRY
