HE HAD THE PATIENCE TO HEAR THE RELATION OF MY ADVENTURES WHICH SURPRISED HIM AND HE AFTERWARD GAVE ME CLOTHES AND COMMANDED CARE TO BE TAKEN OF ME
BUT YOU ARE SPARED BECAUSE THIS REQUEST DOES NOT COME FROM YOURSELF
AFTER HAVING LAIN SOME TIME AND SEEING THE ELEPHANTS GONE I GOT UP AND FOUND I WAS UPON A LONG AND BROAD HILL ALMOST COVERED WITH THE BONES AND TEETH OF ELEPHANTS
AND AS SOON AS IT WAS DAY WENT TO THEM TELLING THEM BY HER TEARS THE CAUSE OF HER COMING
FIFTEEN HUNDRED OF THE EMPEROR'S LARGEST HORSES EACH ABOUT FOUR INCHES AND AN HALF HIGH WERE EMPLOYED TO DRAW ME TOWARDS THE METROPOLIS WHICH AS I SAID WAS HALF A MILE DISTANT
AND WITH THAT HE BEAT THEM ALL THE WAY THITHER
THEY DRANK ALSO OF THE WATER OF THE RIVER WHICH WAS PLEASANT AND ENLIVENING TO THEIR WEARY SPIRITS
YOU SEE THEREFORE THE IMPOSSIBILITY OF MY DOING WHAT YOU DESIRE WELL REPLIED THE ROBBER YOU MAY HOWEVER REMEMBER A LITTLE OF THE WAY THAT YOU WERE LED BLINDFOLD
AT LAST THEY ARRIVED BETWEEN TWO MOUNTAINS OF MODERATE HEIGHT AND EQUAL SIZE DIVIDED BY A NARROW VALLEY WHICH WAS THE PLACE WHERE THE MAGICIAN INTENDED TO EXECUTE THE DESIGN THAT HAD BROUGHT HIM FROM AFRICA TO CHINA
I SHOWED HIM A CORN THAT I HAD CUT OFF WITH MY OWN HAND FROM A MAID OF HONOR'S TOE
WHEN ALADDIN HAD EXAMINED EVERY PORTION OF THE PALACE AND PARTICULARLY THE HALL WITH THE FOUR-AND-TWENTY WINDOWS AND FOUND IT TO FAR EXCEED HIS FONDEST EXPECTATIONS HE SAID GENIE THERE IS ONE THING WANTING--A FINE CARPET FOR THE PRINCESS TO WALK UPON FROM THE SULTAN'S PALACE TO MINE
BOHUN HE SAID ADDRESSING ONE OF HIS ATTENDANT KNIGHTS DO THINE OFFICE THE OFFICER STEPPED FORWARD AND LAYING HIS HAND ON THE SHOULDER OF ALBERT DE MALVOISIN SAID I ARREST THEE OF HIGH TREASON WHO DARES TO ARREST A KNIGHT OF THE TEMPLE IN MY PRESENCE SAID THE GRAND MASTER
HOWEVER I WENT DOWN THUS TWO OR THREE DAYS AND HAVING SEEN NOTHING I BEGAN TO BE A LITTLE BOLDER AND TO THINK THERE WAS REALLY NOTHING IN IT BUT MY OWN IMAGINATION
I REMEMBER WHEN I WAS AT LILLIPUT THE COMPLEXIONS OF THOSE DIMINUTIVE PEOPLE APPEARED TO ME THE FAIREST IN THE WORLD
AND DRANK OF THE WATER WHICH WAS VERY LIGHT AND GOOD
THE PALER BALAS RUBIES
AND I WILL WIND THEE IN MY ARMS FROM THE PAINTING BY ARTHUR RACKHAM THE JUNIOR CLASSICS SELECTED AND ARRANGED BY WILLIAM PATTEN MANAGING EDITOR OF THE HARVARD CLASSICS INTRODUCTION BY CHARLES W
AMONGST THOSE WHO PARTOOK OF THE FOREST HOSPITALITY OF THE OUTLAWS WERE IVANHOE AND GURTH WHO JUST THEN CAME ON THE SCENE THE FORMER NOW ALL BUT CURED OF HIS WOUND THANKS TO THE HEALING BALSAM WITH WHICH HE HAD BEEN PROVIDED BY REBECCA THE JEWESS
BUT ALADDIN WAS INCORRIGIBLE AND HIS FATHER TO HIS GREAT GRIEF WAS FORCED TO ABANDON HIM TO HIS IDLENESS AND WAS SO MUCH TROUBLED ABOUT HIM THAT HE FELL SICK AND DIED IN A FEW MONTHS
HE SAW ALSO THAT IN THE DOOR-WAY STOOD MANY MEN IN ARMOUR TO KEEP IT BEING RESOLVED TO DO THE MEN THAT WOULD ENTER WHAT HURT AND MISCHIEF THEY COULD
BUT THERE WAS NO TIME FOR SUCH REFLECTIONS NOW
SHE WAS ATTENDED BY A GREAT CROWD OF LADIES SLAVES AND MUTES WHO WALKED ON EACH SIDE AND BEHIND HER
THE BOAT WAS CAST ON AN ISLAND AND PROSPERO AND HIS LITTLE ONE LANDED IN SAFETY
THEY ARE SEEN THREE DAYS SAIL OFF AT SEA
MY SERVANTS THOUGHT SHE HAD FOLLOWED ME
AND I MAY SAY WITH TRUTH THAT IN THE MIDST OF MY OWN MISFORTUNES I COULD NOT FORBEAR LAMENTING MY POOR NURSE THE GRIEF SHE WOULD SUFFER FOR MY LOSS THE DISPLEASURE OF THE QUEEN AND THE RUIN OF HER FORTUNE
I MAUN FOOTNOTE
ON THE FIFTH OF NOVEMBER WHICH WAS THE BEGINNING OF SUMMER IN THOSE PARTS THE WEATHER BEING VERY HAZY THE SEAMEN SPIED A ROCK WITHIN HALF A CABLE'S LENGTH OF THE SHIP
AS BOIS-GUILBERT ROLLED ON THE FIELD HIS ANTAGONIST SPRUNG FROM HORSEBACK AND WAS IN THE ACT OF COMMANDING HIS ADVERSARY TO YIELD OR DIE WHEN PRINCE JOHN GAVE THE SIGNAL THAT THE CONFLICT WAS AT AN END
AND IN JOINING HIS HANDS TO PRAY HE RUBBED THE RING WHICH THE MAGICIAN HAD PUT ON HIS FINGER
WHEN I CAME BACK I RESOLVED TO SETTLE IN LONDON TO WHICH MR BATES MY MASTER ENCOURAGED ME AND BY HIM I WAS RECOMMENDED TO SEVERAL PATIENTS
THE ARCHITECT WHO BUILT YOUR PALACE CAN GET YOU ONE AFTER THE PRINCESS HAD THANKED THE FALSE FATIMA FOR WHAT SHE BELIEVED HER GOOD ADVICE SHE CONVERSED WITH HER UPON OTHER MATTERS
I FELL WITH THE TREE AND THE ELEPHANT TAKING ME UP WITH HIS TRUNK LAID ME ON HIS BACK WHERE I SAT MORE LIKE ONE DEAD THAN ALIVE WITH MY QUIVER ON MY SHOULDER
THEY SEEMED VERY THANKFUL FOR IT AND SAID THEY WOULD MUCH RATHER VENTURE TO STAY THERE THAN BE CARRIED TO ENGLAND TO BE HANGED
BUT ARIEL BROUGHT HIM SAFE ASHORE
NOW I BEHELD IN MY DREAM THAT THEY HAD NOT JOURNEYED FAR BUT THE RIVER AND THE WAY FOR A TIME PARTED
LET MY DAUGHTER REBECCA GO FORTH TO YORK AND SHE WILL BRING THE TREASURE HERE THY DAUGHTER SAID FRONT-DE-BOEUF AS IF SURPRISED
AS THIS WAS ALSO ABOUT HALF-WAY BETWEEN MY OTHER HABITATION AND THE PLACE WHERE I HAD LAID UP MY BOAT I GENERALLY STAYED AND LAY HERE IN MY WAY THITHER FOR I USED FREQUENTLY TO VISIT MY BOAT
HERE THEREFORE CHRISTIAN AND HIS COMPANION WALKED WITH GREAT DELIGHT
THE DEBTS OF THE LAIRD BECAME AT LENGTH SO MANY THAT THE PROPERTY AT ELLANGOWAN HAD TO BE MORTGAGED AND THINGS ULTIMATELY WENT SO BADLY WITH THE POOR OWNER THAT THE MEN TO WHOM HE OWED SO MUCH MONEY DETERMINED TO INSIST ON THE ESTATE BEING SOLD TOGETHER WITH THE HOUSE AND ALL THE FURNITURE
I AM ROBIN HOOD OF SHERWOOD FOREST BEFORE MANY MORE MINUTES HAD GONE A SYLVAN REPAST WAS HASTILY PREPARED BENEATH A HUGE OAK-TREE FOR THE KING OF ENGLAND
BUT REBECCA REJECTED HIS PROFFERED LOVE WITH SCORN PROTESTING THAT SHE WOULD PROCLAIM HIS VILLAINY FROM ONE END OF EUROPE TO THE OTHER
HE WENT INTO THAT OF THE DRUGGISTS AND ENTERING ONE OF THE LARGEST AND BEST FURNISHED SHOPS ASKED THE DRUGGIST IF HE HAD A CERTAIN POWDER WHICH HE NAMED
UPON THIS HE CALLED ALOUD TO THE BOAT AND BADE HIS MEN BRING THE THINGS ASHORE THAT WERE FOR THE GOVERNOR
I WAS AFRAID OF TRAMPLING ON EVERY TRAVELLER I MET AND OFTEN CALLED ALOUD TO THEM TO HAVE THEM STAND OUT OF THE WAY SO THAT I HAD LIKE TO HAVE GOTTEN ONE OR TWO BROKEN HEADS FOR MY IMPERTINENCE
HE DID NOT CARE MUCH ABOUT THE QUEEN'S AFFECTION BUT HE WAS VERY PROUD OF HAVING FAIRIES TO WAIT ON HIM
AND TRULY AS TO MYSELF I THOUGHT IT WOULD NOT BE FOR MY REPUTATION THAT SUCH A STORY SHOULD GO ABOUT
I WAS A LITTLE SURPRISED BUT RECOVERED MYSELF WITH THE SATISFACTORY REFLECTION THAT I HAD LOST NO TIME NOR ABATED ANY DILIGENCE TO GET EVERYTHING OUT OF HER THAT COULD BE USEFUL TO ME
FROM THIS LITTLE WICKET-GATE AND FROM THE WAY THERETO HATH THIS WICKED MAN TURNED THEE TO THE BRINGING OF THEE ALMOST TO DESTRUCTION
THEY TOLD HIM THEY WERE PILGRIMS AND THAT THEY HAD LOST THEIR WAY
WHEN THE THREE PERSONS CAME TO THE CREEK I FOUND THAT TWO OF THEM COULD SWIM BUT THE THIRD COULD NOT AND THAT STANDING ON THE OTHER SIDE HE LOOKED AT THE OTHERS BUT WENT NO FARTHER AND SOON AFTER WENT SOFTLY BACK AGAIN
FOR THOUGH I SWAM VERY WELL YET I COULD NOT DELIVER MYSELF FROM THE WAVES SO AS TO DRAW BREATH TILL THAT WAVE HAVING DRIVEN ME OR RATHER CARRIED ME A VAST WAY ON TOWARD THE SHORE AND HAVING SPENT ITSELF WENT BACK AND LEFT ME UPON THE LAND ALMOST DRY BUT HALF DEAD WITH THE WATER I TOOK IN
AND TALKING UPON THE SUBJECT WITH A PERSON OF LEARNING THERE WHO WAS AN INTIMATE FRIEND OF MINE HE SAID THAT MY FACE APPEARED MUCH FAIRER AND SMOOTHER WHEN HE LOOKED ON ME FROM THE GROUND THAN IT DID UPON A NEARER VIEW WHEN I TOOK HIM UP IN MY HAND AND BROUGHT HIM CLOSE WHICH HE CONFESSED WAS AT FIRST A VERY SHOCKING SIGHT
ONE DAY HOWEVER AN OFFICER OF THE CALIPH'S INQUIRED FOR ME
THEN SAID CHRISTIAN TO THE INTERPRETER BUT ARE THERE NO HOPES FOR SUCH A MAN AS THIS
THE VILLAGE HAD BEEN COVERED WITH SNOW OVERNIGHT
THE CEREMONY IS PERFORMED IN HIS MAJESTY'S GREAT CHAMBER OF STATE WHERE THE CANDIDATES ARE TO UNDERGO A TRIAL OF DEXTERITY VERY DIFFERENT FROM THE FORMER AND SUCH AS I HAVE NOT OBSERVED THE LEAST RESEMBLANCE OF IN ANY OTHER COUNTRY OF THE OLD OR NEW WORLD
AND WHERE SIR SAID I IS YOUR BELIEF OF MY BEING PRESERVED HERE ON PURPOSE TO SAVE YOUR LIFE WHICH ELEVATED YOU A LITTLE WHILE AGO
THE SHIP WORE BRAVELY
SEIZE THEM SHE INSTANTLY SPRANG THE PARTRIDGES
BUT AFTER A TIME HE RECOVERED HIS SELF-POSSESSION AND THEN SET HIMSELF TO DISCOVER IF BERTRAM WHOM HE RECOGNISED HAD ANY KNOWLEDGE OF HIS OWN IDENTITY
THAT IS HE ADDED AFTER A MOMENT'S PAUSE I WILL PAY IT WITH THE HELP OF MY BRETHREN
THERE BELONGS TO THIS KING AN ISLAND NAMED CASSEL
HE CLIMBED UP A LARGE TREE PLANTED ON A HIGH ROCK WHOSE BRANCHES WERE THICK ENOUGH TO CONCEAL HIM AND YET ENABLED HIM TO SEE ALL THAT PASSED WITHOUT BEING DISCOVERED
I SLEPT ABOUT EIGHT HOURS AS I WAS AFTERWARDS ASSURED
I CONJURE THEE BY THE HABIT WHICH THOU DOST WEAR BY THE NAME THOU DOST INHERIT BY THE HONOUR OF THY MOTHER I CONJURE THEE TO SAY ARE THESE THINGS TRUE ANSWER HER BROTHER SAID THE GRAND MASTER
SO GREAT WAS HER SKILL AND KNOWLEDGE OF MEDICINE THAT SHE UNDERTOOK TO RESTORE THE INJURED KNIGHT TO HEALTH IN EIGHT DAYS TIME
AND AS AN OPPORTUNITY NOW OFFERS I WILL WITH YOUR LEAVE RELATE THE DANGERS I HAVE ENCOUNTERED WHICH I THINK WILL NOT BE UNINTERESTING TO YOU THE FIRST VOYAGE MY FATHER WAS A RICH MERCHANT
I WAS THOROUGHLY GLAD TO GET HER BACK AGAIN
I FELL INTO A HIGHROAD FOR SO I TOOK IT TO BE THOUGH IT SERVED TO THE INHABITANTS ONLY AS A FOOTPATH THROUGH A FIELD OF BARLEY
LORD'S SAKE CAPTAIN
THE SKIN OF A SERPENT WHOSE SCALES WERE AS BRIGHT AS AN ORDINARY PIECE OF GOLD AND HAD THE VIRTUE TO PRESERVE FROM SICKNESS THOSE WHO LAY UPON IT
ON THE MORNING AFTER THE RESTORATION OF ALADDIN'S PALACE THE SULTAN WAS LOOKING OUT OF HIS WINDOW AND MOURNING OVER THE FATE OF HIS DAUGHTER WHEN HE THOUGHT THAT HE SAW THE VACANCY CREATED BY THE DISAPPEARANCE OF THE PALACE TO BE AGAIN FILLED UP
AND WHEN THEY WERE WEARY SOME OF THEIR PAGES WOULD BLOW MY SAIL FORWARD WITH THEIR BREATH WHILE I SHOWED MY ART BY STEERING STARBOARD OR LARBOARD AS I PLEASED
WELL UNCLE WHAT IS TO BE DONE
THEN SAID CHRISTIAN TO HIS FELLOW IF THIS MEADOW LIETH ALONG BY OUR WAY-SIDE LET'S GO OVER INTO IT
YOU MUST ATTEND THIS GENTLEMAN SAID THE QUEEN
TO THE CHILD IT IS A FASCINATING FAIRY TALE
FRONT-DE-BOEUF AND ATHELSTANE HAVING DEFEATED THOSE IMMEDIATELY OPPOSED TO THEM WERE NOW FREE TO COME TO THE AID OF THEIR FRIEND THE TEMPLAR
WHERE LYING DOWN BEHIND A HILLOCK I TOOK OUT MY SMALL PERSPECTIVE GLASS AND VIEWED THE ENEMY'S FLEET AT ANCHOR CONSISTING OF ABOUT FIFTY MEN-OF-WAR AND A GREAT NUMBER OF TRANSPORTS
I LIKEWISE BROKE MY RIGHT SHIN AGAINST THE SHELL OF A SNAIL WHICH I HAPPENED TO STUMBLE OVER AS I WAS WALKING ALONE AND THINKING OF POOR ENGLAND
AND ON ITS CONCLUSION SEVERAL WITNESSES WERE CALLED TO PROVE THE RISKS TO WHICH BOIS-GUILBERT EXPOSED HIMSELF IN ENDEAVOURING TO SAVE REBECCA FROM THE BLAZING CASTLE
I LIVED FOR SOME TIME THERE UPON MY BREAD AND WATER WHEN ONE DAY JUST AS IT WAS ON THE POINT OF EXHAUSTION I HEARD SOMETHING TREAD AND BREATHING OR PANTING AS IT MOVED
PENDING THIS TIME SO FULL OF TERROR AND ANXIETY FOR POOR REBECCA THE BLACK KNIGHT HAVING LEFT THE COMPANY OF THE GENEROUS OUTLAW HELD HIS WAY TO A NEIGHBOURING RELIGIOUS HOUSE TO WHICH THE WOUNDED IVANHOE HAD BEEN REMOVED WHEN THE CASTLE WAS TAKEN
AS THEY LOOKED ON HIM IN ASTONISHMENT THE EYES OPENED BUT THEY WERE FIXED AND GLAZED
ALI BABA'S WIFE WENT HOME SET THE MEASURE UPON THE HEAP OF GOLD FILLED IT AND EMPTIED IT OFTEN UPON THE SOFA TILL SHE HAD DONE WHEN SHE WAS VERY WELL SATISFIED TO FIND THE NUMBER OF MEASURES AMOUNTED TO SO MANY AS THEY DID AND WENT TO TELL HER HUSBAND WHO HAD ALMOST FINISHED DIGGING THE HOLE
BY REASON OF WHICH THE WAY OF GOING BACK WAS VERY DANGEROUS
IN A LITTLE TIME I OBSERVED THE NOISE AND FLUTTER OF WINGS TO INCREASE VERY FAST AND MY BOX WAS TOSSED UP AND DOWN LIKE A SIGN ON A WINDY DAY
THOU DIDST THE SAME TO ME AND YET I AM WILLING TO PASS BY ALL IF NOW THOU WILT YET TURN AGAIN AND GO BACK
WE INDEED CAME BOTH TOGETHER UNTIL WE CAME TO THE SLOUGH OF DISPOND INTO THE WHICH WE ALSO SUDDENLY FELL
I'LL NO LIVE TO SEE IT MAYBE
FOR THOUGH THE STORM WAS ABATED CONSIDERABLY YET THE SEA WENT DREADFULLY HIGH UPON THE SHORE AND MIGHT BE WELL CALLED DEN WILD ZEE AS THE DUTCH CALL THE SEA IN A STORM
I ATE MY BREAKFAST BEFORE THE SUN WAS UP
WHETHER INHABITED OR NOT INHABITED
BUT WE MUST RETURN TO BERTRAM AND HIS COMPANION IN THEIR UNPLEASANT ABODE IN THE PRISON
HE ANSWERED BECAUSE I KNOW NOT WHITHER TO GO
THIS AT LENGTH PUT ME UPON THINKING WHETHER IT WAS NOT POSSIBLE TO MAKE MYSELF A CANOE OR PERIAGUA SUCH AS THE NATIVES OF THOSE CLIMATES MAKE EVEN WITHOUT TOOLS OR AS I MIGHT SAY WITHOUT HANDS OF THE TRUNK OF A GREAT TREE
WHEN I ADVANCED TO THE MIDDLE OF THE CHANNEL THEY WERE YET IN MORE PAIN BECAUSE I WAS UNDER WATER TO MY NECK
AT LAST WHEN HE HAD RECOVERED HIMSELF HE RECEIVED THE PRESENT FROM ALADDIN'S MOTHER'S HAND SAYING HOW RICH
HOW WAS IT POSSIBLE I COULD GET ON SHORE
BUT WHEN HE WAS CONVINCED THAT THE WINDOW WHICH SEVERAL WORKMEN HAD BEEN SO LONG ABOUT WAS FINISHED IN SO SHORT A TIME HE EMBRACED ALADDIN AND KISSED HIM BETWEEN HIS EYES
HOW IT CAME THITHER I KNEW NOT NOR COULD I IN THE LEAST IMAGINE
SHOTS WERE FIRED AND THE GLITTERING BROADSWORDS OF THE SOLDIERS BEGAN TO FLASH IN THE AIR
NOW CHRISTIAN AND HIS FELLOW HEARD HIM FALL
AND HAVING PASSED THE NIGHT IN THE SAME UNPLEASANT WAY THEY WERE IN THE MORNING CONVEYED TO THE PALACE OF THE SULTAN
THAT WAS A FELON STROKE EXCLAIMED THE BLACK KNIGHT AS THE HORSE FELL TO THE EARTH BEARING HIS RIDER ALONG WITH HIM
THE INNUMERABLE CONCOURSE OF PEOPLE THROUGH WHOM HE PASSED MADE THE AIR ECHO WITH THEIR ACCLAMATIONS ESPECIALLY EVERY TIME THE SIX SLAVES WHO CARRIED THE PURSES THREW HANDFULS OF GOLD AMONG THE POPULACE
ON THE VERGE OF A WOOD WAS AN EXTENSIVE MEADOW OF THE FINEST AND MOST BEAUTIFUL GREEN TURF SURROUNDED ON ONE SIDE BY THE FOREST AND FRINGED ON THE OTHER BY STRAGGLING OAK-TREES
THERE I STUDIED PHYSIC TWO YEARS AND SEVEN MONTHS KNOWING IT WOULD BE USEFUL IN LONG VOYAGES
HIS VERY AFFECTIONS WERE TIED TO ME LIKE THOSE OF A CHILD TO A FATHER AND I DARE SAY HE WOULD HAVE SACRIFICED HIS LIFE TO SAVE MINE UPON ANY OCCASION WHATSOEVER
MITCHELL ONCE SAID
BUT NOW I AM SPEAKING OF THE PALACE PRAY HOW DO YOU LIKE IT
HE SAW ALSO UPON THE TOP THEREOF CERTAIN PERSONS WALKING WHO WERE CLOATHED ALL IN GOLD
I WAS AN HOUR WALKING TO THE END OF THIS FIELD WHICH WAS FENCED IN WITH A HEDGE OF AT LEAST ONE HUNDRED AND TWENTY FEET HIGH AND THE TREES SO LOFTY THAT I COULD MAKE NO COMPUTATION OF THEIR ALTITUDE
THERE ARE YOUR GOODS
HE APPEARED AS TALL AS AN ORDINARY SPIRE STEEPLE AND TOOK ABOUT TEN YARDS AT EVERY STRIDE AS NEAR AS I COULD GUESS
AFTER SOME TIME SPENT IN THIS WAY ONE OF THE PARTY WENT OUT AND BROUGHT IN A PORTMANTEAU WHICH BROWN AT ONCE RECOGNISED AS THE ONE HE HAD LEFT IN THE CHAISE
AND BEING ADVISED TO ALTER MY CONDITION I MARRIED MISS MARY BURTON SECOND DAUGHTER TO MR EDMUND BURTON HOSIER IN NEWGATE STREET WITH WHOM I RECEIVED FOUR HUNDRED POUNDS FOR A PORTION
FIFTY ROBES OF RICH STUFF
IT IS A SIGN THAT HE LOVES YOU AND HAS SOME USE FOR YOUR SERVICE IN THE WORLD
WHEN HE REACHED THE ENTRANCE OF THE CAVERN HE PRONOUNCED THE WORDS OPEN SESAME THE DOOR IMMEDIATELY OPENED AND WHEN HE WAS IN CLOSED UPON HIM
ALL THESE THINGS I SAY WHICH I OUGHT TO HAVE CONSIDERED WELL AND DID COME INTO MY THOUGHTS AFTERWARDS YET GAVE ME NO APPREHENSIONS AT FIRST AND MY HEAD RAN MIGHTILY UPON THE THOUGHT OF GETTING OVER TO THE SHORE
I ATTEMPTED TO RISE BUT WAS NOT ABLE TO STIR
ON HIS WAY HE HAPPENED TO MEET LITTLE BERTRAM WHO WAS WALKING WITH THE DOMINIE AND AS HE HAD OFTEN PROMISED TO GIVE THE CHILD A RIDE HE TOOK HIM UP ON HIS NAG AND RODE OFF TOWARDS THE POINT
THE PAIN MADE HIM BREAK OUT INTO A FRIGHTFUL YELL
HERE I WALKED ON FOR SOME TIME BUT COULD SEE LITTLE ON EITHER SIDE IT BEING NOW NEAR HARVEST AND THE CORN RISING AT LEAST FORTY FEET
THE VESSEL WAS AN ENGLISH MERCHANTMAN RETURNING FROM JAPAN BY THE NORTH AND SOUTH SEAS
WHEN HE CAME TO HIM HE STOOD LIKE ONE AMAZED LOOKING AT HIM TURNING HIM FIRST ON ONE SIDE THEN ON THE OTHER
HE HAD LOST THE ROAD TO KIPPLETRINGAN WHITHER HE WAS BOUND BUT WAS LUCKY ENOUGH TO FIND A GUIDE TO CONDUCT HIM THERE BEFORE HE HAD GONE COMPLETELY ASTRAY
THERE HE RUBBED HIS LAMP AND THE OBEDIENT GENIE APPEARED
AT THE UPPER END SAT A COMELY VENERABLE GENTLEMAN WITH A LONG WHITE BEARD AND BEHIND HIM STOOD A NUMBER OF OFFICERS AND DOMESTICS ALL READY TO ATTEND HIS PLEASURE
I WENT TO WORK UPON THIS BOAT THE MOST LIKE A FOOL THAT EVER MAN DID WHO HAD ANY OF HIS SENSES AWAKE
BUT HOWEVER MY BROTHER LET'S BE PATIENT AND ENDURE A WHILE
IT MEANS HE SAID IN A FALTERING VOICE THAT MY BROTHER RICHARD HAS OBTAINED HIS FREEDOM IT IS TIME THEN SAID FITZURSE HIS CONFIDENTIAL ATTENDANT TO DRAW OUR PARTY TO A HEAD AND PREPARE OUR FORCES TO MEET HIM IN SULLEN ILL-HUMOUR THE PRINCE LEFT THE PLACE OF TOURNAMENT TO HOLD HIGH FESTIVAL AT THE CASTLE OF ASHBY
UPON THIS I PREPARED TO GO ON BOARD THE SHIP
IN THE MIDDLE OF THIS WORK I FINISHED MY FOURTH YEAR IN THIS PLACE AND KEPT MY ANNIVERSARY WITH THE SAME DEVOTION AND WITH AS MUCH COMFORT AS EVER BEFORE
I THEN CAME BACK TO MY HOUSE AND GAVE ORDER FOR WHICH I HAD A WARRANT FOR A GREAT QUANTITY OF THE STRONGEST CABLE AND BARS OF IRON
THE SUDDEN SOUND MADE THE MURDERERS BEAR BACK ONCE MORE AND WAMBA DID NOT HESITATE TO RUSH IN AND ASSIST HIS KNIGHT TO RISE
THIS I TOOK TO BE A GOOD OMEN AND WENT TO THEM WITHOUT ANY SCRUPLE
THE ROBBER AT HIS RETURN TO HIS COMPANY VALUED HIMSELF MUCH ON THE PRECAUTION HE HAD TAKEN WHICH HE LOOKED UPON AS AN INFALLIBLE WAY OF DISTINGUISHING ALI BABA'S HOUSE FROM THE OTHERS
AND UPON DEBATE WITH MYSELF I CONCLUDED THAT THIS ISLAND WHICH WAS SO EXCEEDINGLY PLEASANT FRUITFUL AND NO FARTHER FROM THE MAINLAND THAN AS I HAD SEEN WAS NOT SO ENTIRELY ABANDONED AS I MIGHT IMAGINE
RASPE SHOOTING A STAG WITH CHERRYSTONES R
BUT PLEASE DON'T LET ANY OF YOUR PEOPLE DISTURB ME

ILL MET BY MOONLIGHT PROUD TITANIA SAID THE KING
MOST UNWILLING WAS HIS TESTIMONY AND GIVEN WITH MANY TEARS
HOW BEAUTIFUL AFTER HE HAD ADMIRED AND HANDLED ALL THE JEWELS ONE AFTER ANOTHER HE TURNED TO HIS GRAND VIZIER AND SHOWING HIM THE DISH SAID BEHOLD
AND IT WAS GREEN ALL THE YEAR LONG
I SWEAR BY EARTH AND SEA AND SKY I WILL OFFER THEE NO OFFENCE
OFFERING ME AT THE SAME TIME BUT UNDER THE STRICTEST CONFIDENCE HIS GRACIOUS PROTECTION IF I WOULD CONTINUE IN HIS SERVICE
AND I WENT HOME AGAIN FILLED WITH THE BELIEF THAT SOME MAN OR MEN HAD BEEN ON SHORE THERE
YOUR SUPPER WILL BE SPOILED IF I KEEP IT BACK SO LONG DO NOT BE ANGRY MORGIANA REPLIED ALI BABA
SO I RETIRED IN THE DARK FROM THEM THAT THEY MIGHT NOT SEE WHAT KIND OF A GOVERNOR THEY HAD AND CALLED THE CAPTAIN TO ME
OR THAT AT SOME TIME OR OTHER HE MAY FORGET TO LOCK US IN
WITH A TREMBLING HAND HE PRODUCED FROM HIS BOSOM A SMALL BOX OF OINTMENT BEARING SOME HEBREW CHARACTERS UPON THE LID WHICH WAS WITH MOST OF THE AUDIENCE A SURE PROOF THAT THE DEVIL HAD STOOD APOTHECARY
HAVING GOT MY SECOND CARGO ON SHORE--THOUGH I WAS FAIN TO OPEN THE BARRELS OF POWDER AND BRING THEM BY PARCELS FOR THEY WERE TOO HEAVY BEING LARGE CASKS--I WENT TO WORK TO MAKE ME A LITTLE TENT WITH THE SAIL AND SOME POLES WHICH I CUT FOR THAT PURPOSE AND INTO THIS TENT I BROUGHT EVERYTHING THAT I KNEW WOULD SPOIL EITHER WITH RAIN OR SUN
SHORTLY AFTER HER DEPARTURE ALADDIN MOUNTING HIS HORSE AND ATTENDED BY HIS RETINUE OF MAGNIFICENT ATTENDANTS LEFT HIS PATERNAL HOME FOREVER AND WENT TO THE PALACE IN THE SAME POMP AS ON THE DAY BEFORE
IT HAS A HORN UPON ITS NOSE ABOUT A CUBIT IN LENGTH
TO SAVE THE DUKE FROM HIS ENEMIES WAS IMPOSSIBLE BUT MUCH COULD BE DONE TO REMIND HIM OF A SUBJECT'S LOVE
APOLLYON THEREFORE FOLLOWED HIS WORK AMAIN AND CHRISTIAN AGAIN TOOK COURAGE AND RESISTED AS MANFULLY AS HE COULD
HERMIA'S FATHER WAS SO ANGRY WITH HER FOR REFUSING TO DO AS HE WISHED THAT HE ACTUALLY BROUGHT HER BEFORE THE DUKE OF ATHENS TO ASK THAT SHE MIGHT BE KILLED IF SHE STILL REFUSED TO OBEY HIM
DESCEND MY SON SAID THE AFRICAN MAGICIAN THOSE STEPS AND OPEN THAT DOOR
HE CONSIDERED AWHILE WITH THE CAUTION OF ONE WHO ENDEAVORS TO LAY HOLD ON A SMALL DANGEROUS ANIMAL IN SUCH A MANNER THAT IT SHALL NOT BE ABLE EITHER TO SCRATCH OR BITE HIM AS I MYSELF HAVE SOMETIMES DONE WITH A WEASEL IN ENGLAND
WHEN HE GOT WITHIN HIS MOTHER'S DOOR THE JOY TO SEE HER AND HIS WEAKNESS FOR WANT OF SUSTENANCE MADE HIM SO FAINT THAT HE REMAINED FOR A LONG TIME AS DEAD
MORGIANA REMEMBERING ALI BABA'S ORDERS GOT HIS BATHING LINEN READY AND ORDERED ABDALLA TO SET ON THE POT FOR THE BROTH
I WAS COVERED AGAIN WITH WATER A GOOD WHILE BUT NOT SO LONG BUT I HELD IT OUT
AND THESE WERE ANSWERED BY A FURIOUS DISCHARGE OF WHIZZING SHAFTS AND MISSILES FROM THE WALLS
IN A WORD TO TRY THEM AND TELL ME WHETHER HE THOUGHT THEY MIGHT BE TRUSTED OR NOT TO GO ON BOARD AND SURPRISE THE SHIP
WHEN IT BECAME QUITE DARK HE PULLED THE LAMP OUT OF HIS BREAST AND RUBBED IT
THE CAPTAIN HAVING LOST TWO BRAVE FELLOWS OF HIS TROOP WAS AFRAID OF DIMINISHING IT TOO MUCH BY PURSUING THIS PLAN TO GET INFORMATION OF THE RESIDENCE OF THEIR PLUNDERER
BY THIS TIME I FOUND MY STRENGTH GONE AND DESPAIRED OF SAVING MY LIFE WHEN HAPPILY A WAVE THREW ME ON AN ISLAND
I NOW BEGAN TO BE WEARY AND SEEING NOTHING TO ENTERTAIN MY CURIOSITY I RETURNED GENTLY DOWN TOWARD THE CREEK
THE PLATES OF IRON FASTENED AT THE BOTTOM OF THE BOX FOR THOSE WERE THE STRONGEST PRESERVED THE BALANCE WHILE IT FELL AND HINDERED IT FROM BEING BROKEN ON THE SURFACE OF THE WATER
AND THE TERRIBLE SCENE CAME BACK TO HIS MIND WITH ALL ITS ACCOMPANIMENTS OF HORROR AS HE STEALTHILY APPROACHED THE CAVERN
OUR VOYAGE WAS VERY PROSPEROUS BUT I SHALL NOT TROUBLE THE READER WITH A JOURNAL OF IT
AND THAT IF SO I SHOULD CERTAINLY HAVE THEM COME AGAIN IN GREATER NUMBERS AND DEVOUR ME
THIS AGREEABLE RETREAT WAS VERY COMFORTABLE TO ME AFTER MY MISFORTUNES AND THE KINDNESS OF THIS GENEROUS PRINCE COMPLETED MY SATISFACTION
BUT THE KINDNESS OF SOME NEIGHBOURS NAMED MAC-MORLAN TO SOME EXTENT ASSUAGED THE MISERY OF HER POSITION
ABOUT NOON THE ROBBERS VISITED THEIR CAVE
THOU KNOWEST THAT FOR THE MOST PART HIS SERVANTS COME TO AN ILL END BECAUSE THEY ARE TRANSGRESSORS AGAINST ME AND MY WAYS
FIRST IN THE MANNER OF MY OWN COUNTRY AND AFTERWARDS IN THE METHOD PRESCRIBED BY THEIR LAWS WHICH WAS TO HOLD MY RIGHT FOOT IN MY LEFT HAND AND TO PLACE THE MIDDLE FINGER OF MY RIGHT HAND ON THE CROWN OF MY HEAD AND MY THUMB ON THE TIP OF MY RIGHT EAR
AND IT AFFORDED ME A GREAT MANY CURIOUS SPECULATIONS AFTERWARDS WHEN I HAD RECOVERED FROM MY FIRST SURPRISE
WHENEVER THE GIPSY WOMAN ADDRESSED THEM SHE SPOKE ANGRILY TO THEM
BECAUSE THEY REPENTED HE FORGAVE THEM AND TOLD THEM THE STORY OF HIS LIFE SINCE THEY HAD CRUELLY COMMITTED HIM AND HIS BABY DAUGHTER TO THE MERCY OF WIND AND WAVES
WHICH THE MONKEY OBSERVING AND FINDING HIMSELF ALMOST ENCOMPASSED NOT BEING ABLE TO MAKE SPEED ENOUGH WITH HIS THREE LEGS LET ME DROP ON A RIDGE TILE AND MADE HIS ESCAPE

HE WANDERED AMONGST THE RUINS OF THE COTTAGES WHERE HE FOUND NO ONE ALTHOUGH HE NOTICED THE REMAINS OF A FIRE IN ONE OF THE HUTS
I AM TORMENTED WITH A VIOLENT PAIN IN MY HEAD AND REQUEST YOUR ASSISTANCE AND HOPE YOU WILL NOT REFUSE ME THAT CURE WHICH YOU IMPART TO AFFLICTED PERSONS SO SAYING HE ROSE BUT HELD DOWN HIS HEAD

WAS I NOT THE MAN YES SAID BERTRAM STARTING FROM HIS SEAT AS IF A SUDDEN LIGHT HAD BURST IN UPON HIS MIND

ALADDIN WHO WAS NOW NO LONGER RESTRAINED BY THE FEAR OF A FATHER GAVE HIMSELF ENTIRELY OVER TO HIS IDLE HABITS AND WAS NEVER OUT OF THE STREETS FROM HIS COMPANIONS
FOR THEY SAY THAT LIONS WILL NOT PREY ON ANYTHING THAT IS DEAD OR SLEEPING
BUT THEY SEARCHED LONG AND IN VAIN FOR ANY TRACE OF KENNEDY OR THE BOY
OTHERS LAUGHED
HE FOUND OLD MR BERTRAM SITTING IN AN EASY CHAIR ON THE SLOPE BESIDE THE CASTLE WITH HIS FEET WRAPPED IN BLANKETS AND BESIDE HIM HIS DAUGHTER AND THE DOMINIE AND A HANDSOME YOUNG MAN WHOM HE DID NOT RECOGNISE BUT WHO HE AFTERWARDS LEARNED WAS A GENTLEMAN CALLED CHARLES HAZLEWOOD WHO WAS DEEPLY IN LOVE WITH MISS BERTRAM
I PURSUED IT FOR A CONSIDERABLE TIME TILL AT LAST I PERCEIVED A LIGHT RESEMBLING A STAR
THEN SAID CHRISTIAN NOW I SEE THAT PATIENCE HAS THE BEST WISDOM AND THAT UPON MANY ACCOUNTS
MY INTENTION WAS TO REACH IF POSSIBLE ONE OF THOSE ISLANDS WHICH I HAD REASON TO BELIEVE LAY ON THE NORTHEAST OF VAN DIEMEN'S LAND
AT THE END OF THE LANE THERE WAS A POST-CHAISE AND HORSES WAITING
WHICH BY KEEPING OFF AT SEA TO AVOID THE INDRAFT OF THE BAY OR GULF OF MEXICO WE MIGHT EASILY PERFORM AS WE HOPED IN ABOUT FIFTEEN DAYS SAIL
FOR I WAS WET HAD NO CLOTHES TO SHIFT ME NOR ANYTHING EITHER TO EAT OR DRINK TO COMFORT ME
COGIA HOUSSAIN RETURNED THE COMPLIMENT BY ASSURING ALI BABA THAT THOUGH HIS SON MIGHT NOT HAVE ACQUIRED THE EXPERIENCE OF OLDER MEN HE HAD GOOD SENSE EQUAL TO THE EXPERIENCE OF MANY OTHERS
HOWEVER WE HAD NO REMEDY BUT TO WAIT AND SEE WHAT THE ISSUE OF THINGS MIGHT PRESENT
BUT THE MONEY HE HAD TAKEN FROM THE ROBBERS HE CONVEYED THITHER BY NIGHT
IN A WORD I BROUGHT AWAY ALL THE SAILS FIRST AND LAST
THE KING WHEN HE DISMISSED ME MADE ME A VERY CONSIDERABLE PRESENT
AND THEY BEING HEEDLESS DID BOTH FALL SUDDENLY INTO THE BOG
THEN SAID THE INTERPRETER TO CHRISTIAN HAST THOU CONSIDERED ALL THESE THINGS
THE ATTACKING PARTY THEN DREW THEIR SWORDS AND ASSAILED HIM ON EVERY SIDE
THEY WERE ALL IN FLAMING FIRE ALSO THE HEAVENS WERE IN A BURNING FLAME
HE MOUNTED HIS HORSE AND WHEN HE CAME TO THE CAVE HE ALIGHTED TIED HIS HORSE TO A TREE THEN APPROACHING THE ENTRANCE AND PRONOUNCING THE WORDS OPEN SESAME THE DOOR OPENED
I DURST NOT PRESUME TO CALL
BUT NEITHER WOULD THIS DELIVER ME FROM THE FURY OF THE SEA WHICH CAME POURING IN AFTER ME AGAIN
BUT I MUST CORRECT YOUR ERROR CONCERNING MYSELF
BUT I FOUND ALL MY LABOR TO LITTLE PURPOSE
FINDS THE PRINT OF A MAN'S FOOT ON THE SAND BY DANIEL DEFOE IT WOULD HAVE MADE A STOIC SMILE TO HAVE SEEN ME AND MY LITTLE FAMILY SIT DOWN TO DINNER
TO ME THEY ARE VALUELESS
AND THAT WHICH WAS PARTICULARLY AFFLICTING TO ME WAS THAT I HAD NO WEAPON EITHER TO HUNT AND KILL ANY CREATURE FOR MY SUSTENANCE OR TO DEFEND MYSELF AGAINST ANY OTHER CREATURE THAT MIGHT DESIRE TO KILL ME FOR THEIRS
THEN SAID CHRISTIAN TO THE INTERPRETER EXPOUND THIS MATTER MORE FULLY TO ME
WHAT DOEST THOU HERE CHRISTIAN
HERE IS A LETTER AND IF I MISTAKE NOT IT IS IN SAXON THE TEMPLAR TOOK THE PAPER FROM HIS HAND AND READ IT
AND SHORTLY AFTER HIS APPOINTMENT HE BEGAN LITTLE BY LITTLE TO BECOME VERY UNPOPULAR WITH THE GIPSIES WITH WHOM HE HAD BEFORE BEEN SUCH A FAVOURITE
ALONSO WHO SEEMED SORRIEST OF THEM ALL FOR HIS PAST CRIMES LAMENTED THE LOSS OF HIS HEIR
OR IF I PLEASED I MIGHT CALL MYSELF KING OR EMPEROR OVER THE WHOLE COUNTRY WHICH I HAD POSSESSION OF
BUT THE HOPE OF FURNISHING MYSELF WITH NECESSARIES ENCOURAGED ME TO GO BEYOND WHAT I SHOULD HAVE BEEN ABLE TO HAVE DONE UPON ANOTHER OCCASION
THOU THOU THE DAUGHTER OF MY FATHER'S FRIEND AND COMPANION IN ARMS THY FATHER'S FRIEND ECHOED URFRIED
SO I PULLED OFF MY CLOTHES--FOR THE WEATHER WAS HOT TO EXTREMITY--AND TOOK THE WATER
FOR WAITING THEREABOUTS TILL EVENING I WENT UP TO THE ROCK AGAIN AND THEN THE TIDE OF EBB BEING MADE I PLAINLY SAW THE CURRENT AGAIN AS BEFORE ONLY THAT IT RAN FARTHER OFF BEING NEAR HALF A LEAGUE FROM THE SHORE WHEREAS IN MY CASE IT SET CLOSE UPON THE SHORE AND HURRIED ME AND MY CANOE ALONG WITH IT WHICH AT ANOTHER TIME IT WOULD NOT HAVE DONE
BUT AS I HAD BOTH SCISSORS AND RAZORS SUFFICIENT I HAD CUT IT PRETTY SHORT EXCEPT WHAT GREW ON MY UPPER LIP WHICH I HAD TRIMMED INTO A LARGE PAIR OF MAHOMETAN WHISKERS SUCH AS I HAD SEEN WORN BY SOME TURKS AT SALLEE FOR THE MOORS DID NOT WEAR SUCH THOUGH THE TURKS DID
ON A PLATFORM BEYOND THE SOUTHERN ENTRANCE WERE PITCHED FIVE MAGNIFICENT PAVILIONS ADORNED WITH PENNONS OF RUSSET AND BLACK THE CHOSEN COLOURS OF THE FIVE KNIGHTS CHALLENGERS
HATE THEREFORE HIS TURNING THEE OUT OF THE WAY AND ABHOR THYSELF FOR HEARKENING TO HIM
I SAY BESIDES FOR I SAW IT THAT KING RICHARD HIMSELF AND FIVE OF HIS KNIGHTS HELD A TOURNAMENT AFTER THE TAKING OF ST JOHN-DE ACRE AS CHALLENGERS AND PROVED THEMSELVES SUPERIOR TO ALL COMERS THE SWARTHY COUNTENANCE OF THE TEMPLAR GREW DARKER WITH A BITTER SCOWL OF RAGE AS HE LISTENED TO THESE WORDS
THE OTHER PRISONERS HAD BETTER USAGE
AND I WAS NOT WITHOUT SECRET WISHES THAT I WERE ON SHORE THERE FANCYING THAT SEEING THE MAINLAND AND AN INHABITED COUNTRY I MIGHT FIND SOME WAY OR OTHER TO CONVEY MYSELF FURTHER AND PERHAPS AT LAST FIND SOME MEANS OF ESCAPE
AT THAT SUMMONS THE GENIE APPEARED AND SAID WHAT WOULDST THOU HAVE
IT IS IMPOSSIBLE TO EXPRESS THE JOY OF BOTH AT SEEING EACH OTHER AFTER SO CRUEL A SEPARATION
I COULD FORCE NOTHING ON HIM BUT A FOOTMAN'S TOOTH WHICH I OBSERVED HIM TO EXAMINE WITH GREAT CURIOSITY AND FOUND HE HAD A FANCY FOR IT
HE WAS ACCORDINGLY USHERED INTO A SMALL ILL-FURNISHED APARTMENT THROUGH THE BARRED WINDOWS OF WHICH HE COULD GET A GLIMPSE OF THE SEA WHICH WAS DASHING SULLENLY AGAINST THE OUTER WALLS
BROTHER BE NOT SURPRISED TO SEE US
BUT THAT WHICH ASTONISHED HIM MOST WAS TO KNOW HOW I KILLED THE OTHER INDIAN SO FAR OFF
AS SOON AS THEY WERE ALONE THE OLD WOMAN ADDRESSED THE JEWESS TELLING HER THAT SHE WAS ONCE AS YOUNG AND FAIR AS HERSELF WHEN FRONT-DE-BOEUF THE FATHER OF THE MAN WHO NOW LORDED IT IN THE CASTLE ATTACKED THE PLACE AND SLEW HER FATHER AND HIS SEVEN SONS AND SHE BECAME THE PREY AND SCORN OF THE CONQUEROR
AND NOW WALDEMAR FITZURSE SAY ME THE TRUTH
AFTER THEY WERE ALL ENTERED AND HAD FORMED A SEMI-CIRCLE BEFORE THE SULTAN'S THRONE THE BLACK SLAVES LAID THE GOLDEN TRAYS ON THE CARPET PROSTRATED THEMSELVES TOUCHING THE CARPET WITH THEIR FOREHEADS AND AT THE SAME TIME THE WHITE SLAVES DID THE SAME
NOW THIS ISLAND WAS ENCHANTED AND FOR YEARS HAD LAIN UNDER THE SPELL OF A FELL WITCH SYCORAX WHO HAD IMPRISONED IN THE TRUNKS OF TREES ALL THE GOOD SPIRITS SHE FOUND THERE
THEREFORE TO THIS END HE SENT HIM HARNESS'D OUT
THE COMBAT ON THE SECOND DAY OF THE TOURNAMENT WAS ON A MUCH MORE EXTENDED SCALE THAN THAT OF THE PREVIOUS ONE
THAT'S NOT FOR NOTHING
BUT THE TRUTH IS I CAN EAT NO VICTUALS THAT HAVE ANY SALT IN THEM
TO THIS END WHEN SHE HAD FINISHED WHAT SHE HAD TO DO IN THE KITCHEN SHE HELPED ABDALLA TO CARRY UP THE DISHES
AND THIS I DID OUT OF THE SHORT PIECES OF BOARDS THAT I BROUGHT ON MY RAFT FROM THE SHIP
HE WAS NOT LONG IN DETERMINING HOW HE SHOULD PAY THE LAST DUES TO HIS BROTHER
ON HIS RETURN HE HAD RECOURSE TO AN OPERATION OF GEOMANCY TO FIND OUT WHERE THE LAMP WAS--WHETHER ALADDIN CARRIED IT ABOUT WITH HIM OR WHERE HE LEFT IT
SO AWAY HE WENT AND CHRISTIAN SAW HIM NO MORE
THE PICTURE OF THE BRAVE CAPTAIN IN HIS HAIRY GOATSKIN CLOTHES POLL ON HIS SHOULDER HIS FAITHFUL DOG BY HIS SIDE AND FRIDAY FOLLOWING ALONG BEHIND IS ONE THAT REMAINS STAMPED FOR LIFE ON EVERY READER'S MIND
EIGHTY POLES EACH OF ONE FOOT HIGH WERE ERECTED FOR THIS PURPOSE AND VERY STRONG CORDS OF THE BIGNESS OF PACKTHREAD WERE FASTENED BY HOOKS TO MANY BANDAGES WHICH THE WORKMEN HAD GIRT ROUND MY NECK MY HANDS MY BODY AND MY LEGS
WHENCE CAME YOU GOOD WOMAN SAID HE THAT YOU DON'T KNOW THAT THE GRAND VIZIER'S SON IS TO MARRY THE PRINCESS BUDDIR AL BUDDOOR THE SULTAN'S DAUGHTER TO-NIGHT
THIS WAS EXEMPLIFIED IN ME AT THIS TIME IN THE MOST LIVELY MANNER IMAGINABLE
THIS I BEGAN AND IT COST ME A PRODIGIOUS DEAL OF PAINS BUT WHO GRUDGE PAINS WHO HAVE THEIR DELIVERANCE IN VIEW
I GOT IT CLEANED AND PUT IT INTO MY CABINET
THEN CHRISTIAN ASKED WHAT IS THE REASON OF THE DISCONTENT OF PASSION
REMOVE THE BRIDEGROOM SAID ALADDIN TO THE GENIE AND KEEP HIM A PRISONER TILL TO-MORROW DAWN AND THEN RETURN WITH HIM HERE ON ALADDIN BEING LEFT ALONE WITH THE PRINCESS HE ENDEAVORED TO ASSUAGE HER FEARS AND EXPLAINED TO HER THE TREACHERY PRACTISED UPON HIM BY THE SULTAN HER FATHER
ALL THESE I SECURED TOGETHER WITH SEVERAL THINGS BELONGING TO THE GUNNER PARTICULARLY TWO OR THREE IRON CROWS AND TWO BARRELS OF MUSKET BULLETS SEVEN MUSKETS ANOTHER FOWLING-PIECE WITH SOME SMALL QUANTITY OF POWDER MORE
SO WE WORKED AT THE OAR TOWARD THE LAND THOUGH WITH HEAVY HEARTS LIKE MEN GOING TO EXECUTION
IF THEY DESIRED THAT AS I HAD LIBERTY TO LEAVE THE ISLAND I HAD SOME INCLINATION TO GIVE THEM THEIR LIVES IF THEY THOUGHT THEY COULD SHIFT ON SHORE
BUT I HAVE A LITTLE COTTON WHICH I HAVE SPUN
IT IS TRUE HE WENT AWKWARDLY IN THESE CLOTHES AT FIRST
FOR ALTHOUGH MY PROPER EMPLOYMENT HAD BEEN TO BE SURGEON OR DOCTOR TO THE SHIP YET OFTEN UPON A PINCH I WAS FORCED TO WORK LIKE A COMMON MARINER
THERE IS ALSO A PEARL-FISHERY IN THE MOUTH OF ITS PRINCIPAL RIVER
AND HAVING CUT ME A SHORT STICK LIKE A TRUNCHEON FOR MY DEFENCE I TOOK UP MY LODGING
AND IN FIVE OR SIX YEARS TIME I HAD A WOOD BEFORE MY DWELLING GROWING SO MONSTROUSLY THICK AND STRONG THAT IT WAS INDEED PERFECTLY IMPASSABLE
I AM GLAD I HAVE WITH ME A MERCIFUL BROTHER
NESBIT AS YOU LIKE IT E
BUT I SOON FOUND IT WAS IMPOSSIBLE TO AVOID IT
THE MOTHER AND SON SAT AT BREAKFAST TILL IT WAS DINNER TIME AND THEN THEY THOUGHT IT WOULD BE BEST TO PUT THE TWO MEALS TOGETHER
THEY LISTENED VERY ATTENTIVELY TO MY DISCOURSES ON THESE HEADS BUT ESPECIALLY TO THAT PART WHICH RELATED TO THE BUYING OF NEGROES WHICH WAS A TRADE AT THAT TIME NOT FAR ENTERED INTO
BUT BECAUSE THE READER MAY BE CURIOUS TO HAVE SOME IDEA OF THE STYLE AND MANNER OF EXPRESSION PECULIAR TO THAT PEOPLE AS WELL AS TO KNOW THE ARTICLES UPON WHICH I RECOVERED MY LIBERTY I HAVE MADE A TRANSLATION OF THE WHOLE INSTRUMENT WORD FOR WORD AS NEAR AS I WAS ABLE WHICH I HERE OFFER TO THE PUBLIC
AS HE OFFERED TO ADVANCE SHE EXCLAIMED REMAIN WHERE THOU ART PROUD TEMPLAR OR AT THY CHOICE ADVANCE
WHICH I SUPPOSE MUST BE IMPUTED TO THE GREAT HEIGHT THEY WERE AT
WHEN ALI BABA GOT HOME HE DROVE HIS ASSES INTO A LITTLE YARD SHUT THE GATES VERY CAREFULLY THREW OFF THE WOOD THAT COVERED THE PANNIERS CARRIED THE BAGS INTO THE HOUSE AND RANGED THEM IN ORDER BEFORE HIS WIFE
AS I SAT QUIETLY MEDITATING AT MY TABLE I HEARD SOMETHING BOUNCE IN AT THE CLOSET-WINDOW AND SKIP ABOUT FROM ONE SIDE TO THE OTHER
TARRY TILL I SHALL SHEW THEE ONE THING MORE AND THEN THOU SHALT GO THY WAY
BUT GOOD BROTHER LET ME GO BEFORE
THE INTERPRETER THEN BID HIM TELL TO CHRISTIAN THE REASON OF HIS SO DOING
ON THE VERY DAY THAT THE THREE MONTHS CONTAINED IN THE SULTAN'S PROMISE EXPIRED THE MOTHER OF ALADDIN AGAIN WENT TO THE PALACE AND STOOD IN THE SAME PLACE IN THE DIVAN
BY THE WHICH NOTWITHSTANDING ALL THAT CHRISTIAN COULD DO TO AVOID IT APOLLYON WOUNDED HIM IN HIS HEAD HIS HAND AND FOOT THIS MADE CHRISTIAN GIVE A LITTLE BACK
IT SHALL BE A TEST FOR ALL WE MEET DURING OUR PROGRESS TOWARD A RIPENED JUDGMENT AND SO LONG AS OUR TASTE IS UNSPOILED WE SHALL ENJOY READING IT
DURING THIS STORM WHICH WAS FOLLOWED BY A STRONG WIND WEST SOUTHWEST WE WERE CARRIED BY MY COMPUTATION ABOUT FIVE HUNDRED LEAGUES TO THE EAST SO THAT THE OLDEST SAILOR ON BOARD COULD NOT TELL IN WHAT PART OF THE WORLD WE WERE
THE NEXT DAY DAWNED IN UNCLOUDED SPLENDOUR AND AT TEN O'CLOCK THE WHOLE PLAIN WAS CROWDED WITH HORSEMEN HORSEWOMEN AND FOOT PASSENGERS HASTENING TO THE TOURNAMENT
IN THE MEANTIME I FELT AT LEAST FORTY MORE OF THE SAME KIND AS I CONJECTURED FOLLOWING THE FIRST
IN HIS WILD DISMAY AND TERROR FOR HIS CHILD AND REMEMBERING THE WORDS OF MEG MERRILIES THE LAIRD HURRIED AWAY TO DERNCLEUGH HOPING TO GET SOME NEWS OF HIM FROM ANY OF THE GIPSIES WHO MIGHT STILL BE LINGERING ROUND THE PLACE
WHO AFTER THE FIRST TIME DURST NOT OFFER HIM LESS FOR FEAR OF LOSING SO GOOD A BARGAIN
THE VANQUISHED OF WHOM VERY FEW REMAINED SCATTERED AND ESCAPED INTO THE NEIGHBOURING WOOD
AND BEHIND HIM THERE IS ANOTHER WHO STANDS WITH A ROD OF GOLD ON THE TOP OF WHICH IS AN EMERALD HALF A FOOT LONG AND AN INCH THICK
HIS HAIR WAS LONG AND BLACK NOT CURLED LIKE WOOL
SHE LAY ALMOST WHERE SHE DID AT FIRST BUT NOT QUITE
THE BREECHES WERE MADE OF THE SKIN OF AN OLD HE-GOAT WHOSE HAIR HUNG DOWN SUCH A LENGTH ON EITHER SIDE THAT LIKE PANTALOONS IT REACHED TO THE MIDDLE OF MY LEGS
OPEN THE CARRIAGE THEN
AND AS SHE FINISHED MANNERING HEARD HER MURMUR SOMETHING ABOUT THE THREAD OF LIFE BEING THREE TIMES BROKEN AND THREE TIMES MENDED AND DISTINCTLY HEARD HER SAY
PILGRIM SAID THE LADY AFTER A MOMENT'S PAUSE DURING WHICH SHE SEEMED UNCERTAIN HOW TO ADDRESS HIM YOU THIS NIGHT MENTIONED A NAME--I MEAN THE NAME OF IVANHOE--I WOULD GLADLY HEAR NEWS OF HIM
GURTH THE SWINEHERD A SERVANT OF MUCH IMPORTANCE AT THAT TIME WHEN APPEALED TO OPEN THE GATE REFUSED TO LET THE VISITORS OUT AT SUCH AN UNSEASONABLE HOUR
WHEREAT MANY OF THE RABBLE BELOW COULD NOT FORBEAR LAUGHING
ONE DAY WHEN ALI BABA WAS IN THE FOREST AND HAD JUST CUT WOOD ENOUGH TO LOAD HIS ASSES HE SAW AT A DISTANCE A GREAT CLOUD OF DUST WHICH SEEMED TO APPROACH HIM
BEGINNING AT THE FIRST JAR AND SO ON TO THE LAST HE SAID TO EACH MAN
CLOSE BESIDE IT WAS THE OLD CASTLE OF ELLANGOWAN
AND SOME SOUGHT TO HIDE THEMSELVES UNDER THE MOUNTAINS
THOU BEAREST AN ENGLISH HEART AND MUST NEEDS OBEY ME
WHEN THE PRISONER WAS INTRODUCED TO THE MAGISTRATE'S ROOM GLOSSIN AT ONCE RECOGNISED THAT IT WAS DIRCK HATTERAICK THE SMUGGLER CAPTAIN
SHE HOWEVER REFUSED ALL OFFERS OF ASSISTANCE AND CALLED FOR HARRY BERTRAM
UPON MATURELY CONSIDERING THIS THEREFORE I RESOLVED TO DRAW ME A SECOND FORTIFICATION
WHEN I HAD RECOVERED MY BREATH HE THRUST ONE OF HIS FEET AGAINST MY SIDE AND STRUCK ME SO RUDELY WITH THE OTHER THAT HE FORCED ME TO RISE UP AGAINST MY WILL
WHEREUPON THEY STOLE OFF UNPERCEIVED AND IT WAS THREE WEEKS BEFORE I KNEW THE CAUSE OF MY AWAKING SO SUDDENLY
AND A GREAT WATCH-COAT TO COVER ME
FOLLOW ME AS I CREEP IN SHE SAID
BESIDES THESE BRING MY MOTHER SIX WOMEN SLAVES TO ATTEND HER AS RICHLY DRESSED AT LEAST AS ANY OF THE PRINCESS BUDDIR AL BUDDOOR'S EACH CARRYING A COMPLETE DRESS FIT FOR ANY SULTANESS
GULLIVER ESCAPES FROM THE EAGLE BY JONATHAN SWIFT PERILOUS CIRCUMSTANCES FROM WHICH I HAD ALREADY ESCAPED INSPIRED ME WITH A STRONG IMPULSE THAT I SHOULD SOME TIME RECOVER MY LIBERTY THOUGH IT WAS IMPOSSIBLE TO CONJECTURE BY WHAT MEANS OR TO FORM ANY PROJECT WITH THE LEAST HOPE OF SUCCEEDING
HE SAID HE COULD DISCOVER GREAT HOLES IN MY SKIN
GENIE SAID ALADDIN BUILD ME A PALACE FIT TO RECEIVE THE PRINCESS BUDDIR AL BUDDOOR
SINCE WE MUST HAVE BOOKS THERE IS ONE WHICH TO MY MIND FURNISHES THE FINEST TREATISE ON EDUCATION ACCORDING TO NATURE
SIX LARGE WHITE BREAD CAKES ON TWO PLATES TWO FLAGONS OF WINE AND TWO SILVER CUPS
WHEN DAY DAWNED THE OUTLAWS AND THEIR RESCUED PRISONERS ASSEMBLED AROUND THE TRYSTING-TREE IN THE OAK FOREST BESIDE THE NOW RUINED CASTLE
WITH THE FRUIT OF THESE TREES THEY WERE ALSO MUCH DELIGHTED
NO SAID HE I SHALL NOT DO THAT
THERE WAS NO POSSIBILITY OF ESCAPE
WHILE HIS SON WAS STILL ARGUING WITH HIM THE SHERIFF OF THE COUNTRY CAME IN HURRIEDLY AND TOLD HIM THAT HE HAD HAD INFORMATION THAT THE REMOVAL OF THE TROOPS FROM THE CUSTOM HOUSE WAS ONLY PART OF A PLAN AND THAT THEY SHOULD AT ONCE RETURN
ALIVE SAIDST THOU
AND IN NO LONGTIME AFTER THE TWO OCCUPANTS OF THE WRETCHED APARTMENT WERE FAST ASLEEP

MY SON TAKE IT OUT OF MY SIGHT AND PUT IT WHERE YOU PLEASE
GOOD BROTHER PLUCK IT OUT OF THY BOSOM AND TRY

THE NURSE TO QUIET HER BABE MADE USE OF A RATTLE WHICH WAS A KIND OF HOLLOW VESSEL FILLED WITH GREAT STONES AND FASTENED BY A CABLE TO THE CHILD'S WAIST
WITH HIS DAUGHTER WE WILL DEAL AS THE CHRISTIAN LAW AND OUR OWN HIGH OFFICE WARRANT POOR ISAAC WAS HURRIED OFF ACCORDINGLY AND EXPELLED FROM THE PRECEPTORY ALL HIS ENTREATIES AND EVEN HIS OFFERS UNHEARD AND DISREGARDED
FOR WITHOUT THAT YOU HAD NEVER SEEN ME AGAIN
HIS FACE WAS ROUND AND PLUMP

I WOULD HAVE SPOKEN PLAINER BUT THAT YOU ARE OLDER THAN I
RIDE YOUR WAYS LAIRD OF ELLANGOWAN
HE TOLD THE MAGICIAN HE HAD A GREATER INCLINATION TO THAT BUSINESS THAN TO ANY OTHER AND THAT HE SHOULD BE MUCH OBLIGED TO HIM FOR HIS KINDNESS
THE MAGICIAN APPOINTED HIS TIME AND DESIRED HIM TO TAKE CARE THAT THEY SHOULD BE HANDSOME AND WELL POLISHED
THREE OR FOUR DAYS AFTER THE FUNERAL ALI BABA REMOVED HIS FEW GOODS OPENLY TO HIS SISTER-IN LAW'S HOUSE IN WHICH IT WAS AGREED THAT HE SHOULD IN FUTURE LIVE
BUT LITTLE HE ANSWERED
BUT WHEN HE TALKED OF ASKING THE PRINCESS IN MARRIAGE SHE LAUGHED ALOUD
I SLEPT ABOUT TWO HOURS AND DREAMED I WAS AT HOME WITH MY WIFE AND CHILDREN WHICH AGGRAVATED MY SORROWS WHEN I AWAKED AND FOUND MYSELF ALONE IN A VAST ROOM BETWEEN TWO AND THREE HUNDRED FEET WIDE AND ABOUT TWO HUNDRED HIGH LYING IN A BED TWENTY YARDS WIDE

AND THEN I WENT TO TAKE HER UP WITH ONE HAND BY THE WAIST
A BOOK THAT EXERTS A DEEP AS WELL AS A WIDE INFLUENCE MUST PRODUCE CHANGES IN THE READER'S WAY OF THINKING AND EXCITE HIM TO ACTIVITY
THE DISHES WERE OF MASSY GOLD AND CONTAINED THE MOST DELICATE VIANDS
ALADDIN HAD NOT LONG CONCEALED HIMSELF BEFORE THE PRINCESS CAME
AND HAVING BY THE AMUSEMENT OF MY MIND BEEN AS IT WERE TIRED AND MY SPIRITS EXHAUSTED I SLEPT VERY SOUNDLY AND WAKED MUCH BETTER COMPOSED THAN I HAD EVER BEEN BEFORE
IMMEDIATELY A GENIE OF FRIGHTFUL ASPECT APPEARED AND SAID WHAT WOULDST THOU HAVE
IN A WORD I TOLD THEM I WOULD GO WITH ALL MY HEART IF THEY WOULD UNDERTAKE TO LOOK AFTER MY PLANTATION IN MY ABSENCE AND WOULD DISPOSE OF IT TO SUCH AS I SHOULD DIRECT IF I MISCARRIED
THAT NOTHING COULD NOW PASS WHICH WAS NOT EXTRAORDINARY
THE BANISHED DUKE'S DAUGHTER ROSALIND REMAINED WITH CELIA FREDERICK'S DAUGHTER AND THE TWO LOVED EACH OTHER MORE THAN MOST SISTERS
BUT I HAD SCARCELY SHUT MY EYES WHEN SOMETHING THAT FELL BY ME WITH A GREAT NOISE AWAKED ME
SEVERAL CAUSES WERE CALLED ACCORDING TO THEIR ORDER PLEADED AND ADJUDGED UNTIL THE TIME THE DIVAN GENERALLY BROKE UP WHEN THE SULTAN RISING RETURNED TO HIS APARTMENT ATTENDED BY THE GRAND VIZIER
AND THEN I MADE HIM A JERKIN OF GOAT'S SKIN AS WELL AS MY SKILL WOULD ALLOW FOR I WAS NOW GROWN A TOLERABLY GOOD TAILOR
IN HIS PERPLEXITY HE ORDERED THE GRAND VIZIER TO BE SENT FOR WITH EXPEDITION
I WENT ON IN FRONT TO START SOMETHING AND I SOON SAW MY DOG STOP BEFORE SEVERAL HUNDRED COVEYS OF PARTRIDGES
I ONCE WAS AS I THOUGHT FAIR FOR THE COELESTIAL CITY AND HAD THEN EVEN JOY AT THE THOUGHTS THAT I SHOULD GET THITHER
HE STARTED UP AND STRETCHED OUT HIS HANDS IN ORDER TO SACRIFICE I SOME OF US TO HIS RAGE
SOON AFTER I HEARD A GENERAL SHOUT WITH FREQUENT REPETITIONS OF THE WORDS PEPLOM SELAN AND I FELT GREAT NUMBERS OF PEOPLE ON MY LEFT SIDE RELAXING THE CORDS TO SUCH A DEGREE THAT I WAS ABLE TO TURN UPON MY RIGHT
I GUESSED HIS MEANING AND MY GOOD FORTUNE GAVE ME SO MUCH PRESENCE OF MIND THAT I RESOLVED NOT TO STRUGGLE IN THE LEAST AS HE HELD ME IN THE AIR ABOVE SIXTY FEET FROM THE GROUND ALTHOUGH HE GRIEVOUSLY PINCHED MY SIDES FOR FEAR I SHOULD SLIP THROUGH HIS FINGERS
HERE I SAT FOR SOME TIME FIVE HUNDRED YARDS FROM THE GROUND EXPECTING EVERY MOMENT TO BE BLOWN DOWN BY THE WIND OR TO FALL BY MY OWN GIDDINESS AND COME TUMBLING OVER AND OVER FROM THE RIDGE TO THE EAVES
CAPTION DISGUISED AS A TRAVELLER AND A STRANGER PAGE 27 FROM THE PAINTING BY EDMUND DULAC ALADDIN'S MOTHER TOOK THE CHINA DISH IN WHICH THEY HAD PUT THE JEWELS THE DAY BEFORE WRAPPED IT IN TWO FINE NAPKINS AND SET FORWARD FOR THE SULTAN'S PALACE
ALL THE PRECIOUS STONES THE JEWELLERS HAVE IN BAGDAD ARE NOT TO BE COMPARED TO MINE FOR SIZE OR BEAUTY
BUT HE WAS QUICKLY AS MUCH FRIGHTENED THE OTHER WAY
ABDALLA SEEING HER VERY UNEASY SAID DO NOT FRET AND TEASE YOURSELF BUT GO INTO THE YARD AND TAKE SOME OIL OUT OF ONE OF THE JARS MORGIANA THANKED ABDALLA FOR HIS ADVICE TOOK THE OIL-POT AND WENT INTO THE YARD
BROWN OBEYED WITH ALACRITY FEELING THAT HE WAS ALREADY OUT OF REACH OF DANGER WHEN THE VILLAINS HAD GONE OUT
THEY BOUGHT THESE AND SETTLED DOWN AS SHEPHERD AND SHEPHERDESS IN THE FOREST
AFTER TRAVERSING SEVERAL STREETS HE CAME TO THAT PART OF THE TOWN WHERE THE MERCHANTS AND ARTISANS HAD THEIR PARTICULAR STREETS ACCORDING TO THEIR TRADES
MORGIANA A SLAVE TO THE DECEASED FOLLOWED IN THE PROCESSION WEEPING BEATING HER BREAST AND TEARING HER HAIR
HE STATED THAT GLOSSIN WAS PRESENT AND ACCEPTED A BRIBE TO KEEP THE MATTER A SECRET
AND I HAD ORDERED A HAMMOCK TO BE FIXED BY SILKEN ROPES FROM THE FOUR CORNERS AT THE TOP TO BREAK THE JOLTS WHEN A SERVANT CARRIED ME BEFORE HIM ON HORSEBACK AS I SOMETIMES DESIRED
AND A GREAT NUMBER MORE COMING BEFORE HIM AT A QUICK PACE
A SET OF GALLANTS HE SAID WHO HAVE BEEN MASQUERADING IN SUCH GUISE AS OUR OWN ARE CARRYING A BAND OF PRISONERS TO TORQUILSTONE THE CASTLE OF FRONT-DE-BOEUF
AND THE JEWESS WAS COMMANDED TO FIND A CHAMPION BY THE THIRD DAY FOLLOWING
THIS WAS COMMITTED TO FRIDAY AND THE TWO OTHER MEN WHO CAME ON SHORE WITH THE CAPTAIN
SO I WAS THEN OBLIGED TO SHOOT AT HIM FIRST WHICH I DID AND KILLED HIM AT THE FIRST SHOT
YOU MUST OVERHANG THE NIGHT WITH DROOPING FOG AND LEAD THEM SO ASTRAY THAT ONE WILL NEVER FIND THE OTHER
THEN HE WENT TO THE STILE TO SEE AND BEHOLD A PATH LAY ALONG BY THE WAY ON THE OTHER SIDE OF THE FENCE
RASPE CROSSING THE THAMES WITHOUT THE AID OF BRIDGE BOAT OR BALLOON R
THEY CONVEYED THEMSELVES INTO THE TOWN WITH THE SAME PRECAUTION AS BEFORE
THEY DRESSED THE CORPSE OF THE WOMAN IN HER RICHEST APPAREL AND ALL HER JEWELS AS IF IT HAD BEEN HER WEDDING DAY
THIS DIVERSION IS ONLY PRACTISED BY THOSE PERSONS WHO ARE CANDIDATES FOR GREAT EMPLOYMENTS AND HIGH FAVOR AT COURT
HE WENT TO A COPPERSMITH AND ASKED FOR A DOZEN COPPER LAMPS
THAT THE WEATHER BEING CALM HE ROWED ROUND ME SEVERAL TIMES OBSERVED MY WINDOWS AND WIRE LATTICES THAT DEFENDED THEM

IN THE INTERVIEW WHICH TOOK PLACE BETWEEN THEM NO ONE ELSE BEING PRESENT IT TRANSPIRED THAT GLOSSIN HAD BEEN A KIND OF PARTNER WITH THE SMUGGLER AT THE TIME OF KENNEDY'S MURDER AND THE DISAPPEARANCE OF YOUNG HARRY BERTRAM
BROWN WAS ENTIRELY AT A LOSS TO MAKE OUT THE REASON THE GIPSY HAD FOR TAKING SUCH AN INTEREST IN PRESERVING HIS LIFE FROM HER COMRADES
DIDN'T I TELL YE WHEN YE TOOK AWAY THE BOY HARRY BERTRAM IN SPITE OF MY PRAYERS THAT HE WOULD COME BACK AGAIN IN HIS TWENTY FIRST YEAR
AS FOR MY BREECHES WHICH WERE ONLY LINEN AND OPEN-KNEED I SWAM ON BOARD IN THEM AND MY STOCKINGS
THE DAY AFTER HIS ARRIVAL AT THE VILLAGE OF KIPPLETRINGAN HE DETERMINED TO SEE MISS MANNERING
HE WAS A GOOD-TEMPERED EASY-GOING KIND OF MAN AND BECAME IN CONSEQUENCE VERY POPULAR WITH ALL THE POORER PEOPLE OF THE DISTRICT AND ESPECIALLY WITH THE GIPSIES A LARGE NUMBER OF WHOM WERE AT ALL TIMES TO BE FOUND IN THE NEIGHBOURHOOD
HE SNATCHED IT EAGERLY OUT OF THE SLAVE'S HAND AND THRUSTING IT AS FAR AS HE COULD INTO HIS BREAST OFFERED HIM HIS BASKET AND BADE HIM CHOOSE WHICH HE LIKED BEST
I MEASURED THE TAIL OF THE DEAD RAT AND FOUND IT TO BE TWO YARDS LONG WANTING AN INCH
FROM THIS TIME HE BELIEVED HE WAS THE ONLY PERSON IN THE WORLD WHO HAD THE SECRET OF OPENING THE CAVE AND THAT ALL THE TREASURE WAS AT HIS SOLE DISPOSAL
I THOUGHT PRINCE THAT NOTHING IN THE WORLD WAS SO BEAUTIFUL AS THE SULTAN MY FATHER'S PALACE BUT THE SIGHT OF THIS HALL ALONE IS SUFFICIENT TO SHOW I WAS DECEIVED WHEN THE SUPPER WAS ENDED THERE ENTERED A COMPANY OF FEMALE DANCERS WHO PERFORMED ACCORDING TO THE CUSTOM OF THE COUNTRY SINGING AT THE SAME TIME VERSES IN PRAISE OF THE BRIDE AND BRIDEGROOM
BEING ON SHORE THE FIRST THING THEY DID THEY RAN ALL TO THEIR OTHER BOAT
I DID NOT ATTAIN TO THIS HAPPY CONDITION WITHOUT ENDURING FOR SEVERAL YEARS MORE TROUBLE OF BODY AND MIND THAN CAN WELL BE IMAGINED
ADJOINING TO THIS I HAD MY ENCLOSURES FOR MY CATTLE THAT IS TO SAY MY GOATS AND I HAD TAKEN AN INCONCEIVABLE DEAL OF PAINS TO FENCE AND ENCLOSE THIS GROUND
HOW MANY OF THEM HAVE BEEN PUT TO SHAMEFUL DEATHS
AFTER WAITING FOR HIM IN ANXIETY FOR SOME TIME THE NEWS CAME IN THAT KENNEDY'S HORSE HAD COME BACK RIDERLESS TO ITS STABLE
AND GETTING ALL INTO HER WE LET GO AND COMMITTED OURSELVES BEING ELEVEN IN NUMBER TO GOD'S MERCY AND THE WILD SEA
IT IS NOT EASY FOR ANY ONE WHO HAS NOT BEEN IN THE LIKE CONDITION TO DESCRIBE OR CONCEIVE THE CONSTERNATION OF MEN IN SUCH CIRCUMSTANCES
THIS BOND GIVES YOU NO RIGHT TO ANTONIO'S BLOOD ONLY TO HIS FLESH
I PRAYED THE MERCHANT WHO OWNED THE NEST TO WHICH I HAD BEEN CARRIED FOR EVERY MERCHANT HAD HIS OWN TO TAKE AS MANY FOR HIS SHARE AS HE PLEASED
A LITTLE AFTER NOON I FOUND THE SEA VERY CALM AND THE TIDE EBBED SO FAR OUT THAT I COULD COME WITHIN A QUARTER OF A MILE OF THE SHIP
AND BEING ALMOST FAMISHED WITH HUNGER HAVING NOT EATEN A MORSEL FOR SOME HOURS BEFORE I LEFT THE SHIP I FOUND THE DEMANDS OF NATURE SO STRONG UPON ME THAT I COULD NOT FORBEAR SHOWING MY IMPATIENCE PERHAPS AGAINST THE STRICT RULES OF DECENCY BY PUTTING MY FINGER FREQUENTLY TO MY MOUTH TO SIGNIFY THAT I WANTED FOOD
THAT FALSE AND WICKED MAGICIAN WOULD NOT HAVE UNDERTAKEN SO LONG A JOURNEY TO SECURE THIS WONDERFUL LAMP IF HE HAD NOT KNOWN ITS VALUE TO EXCEED THAT OF GOLD AND SILVER
HOW SHALL I GRAPPLE WITH THE MISERY THAT I MUST MEET WITH IN ETERNITY
CAPTAIN SAID I LOOK AT ME AND YOU MAY KNOW THAT I AM SINDBAD WHOM YOU LEFT IN THAT DESERT ISLAND THE CAPTAIN HAVING CONSIDERED ME ATTENTIVELY RECOGNIZED ME
IN SHORT I TOOK ALL POSSIBLE CAUTION TO PRESERVE MY EFFECTS AND TO KEEP UP MY PLANTATION
THIS WAS A NEW PERPLEXITY
COME GOOD HOPEFUL AND LET US GO OVER
I DESIRED THE CAPTAIN WOULD PLEASE TO ACCEPT THIS RING IN RETURN OF HIS CIVILITIES WHICH HE ABSOLUTELY REFUSED
I SAW NO ELEPHANT DURING THE NIGHT BUT NEXT MORNING AT BREAK OF DAY I PERCEIVED A GREAT NUMBER

HE FOUGHT WITH THE LIONESS AND KILLED HER AND SAVED HIS BROTHER'S LIFE

I MADE A GOOD MEAL AND AFTERWARD FELL ASLEEP
APOLLYON BEWARE WHAT YOU DO FOR I AM IN THE KING'S HIGH-WAY THE WAY OF HOLINESS THEREFORE TAKE HEED TO YOURSELF

SAID THE GIANT I WILL THEREFORE SEARCH THEM IN THE MORNING

BOTH I AND THE OTHER SLAVES OF THE LAMP I COMMAND THEE REPLIED THE MAGICIAN TO TRANSPORT ME IMMEDIATELY AND THE PALACE WHICH THOU AND THE OTHER SLAVES OF THE LAMP HAVE BUILT IN THIS DITY WITH ALL THE PEOPLE IN IT TO AFRICA THE GENIE MADE NO REPLY BUT WITH THE ASSISTANCE OF THE OTHER GENIES THE SLAVES OF THE LAMP IMMEDIATELY TRANSPORTED HIM AND THE PALACE ENTIRE TO THE SPOT WHITHER HE HAD BEEN DESIRED TO CONVEY IT

RASPE I SET OFF FROM ROME ON A JOURNEY TO RUSSIA IN THE MIDST OF WINTER FROM A JUST NOTION THAT FROST AND SNOW MUST OF COURSE MEND THE ROADS WHICH EVERY TRAVELLER HAD DESCRIBED AS UNCOMMONLY BAD THROUGH THE NORTHERN PARTS OF GERMANY POLAND COURLAND AND LIVONIA

HE AFTER OBSTINATE AND I TO THIS GATE
AND HERE I MUST NEEDS OBSERVE THAT AS REASON IS THE SUBSTANCE AND ORIGIN OF THE MATHEMATICS SO BY STATING AND SQUARING EVERYTHING BY REASON AND BY MAKING THE MOST RATIONAL JUDGMENT OF THINGS EVERY MAN MAY BE IN TIME MASTER OF EVERY MECHANIC ART
FOR AS HUMAN CREATURES ARE OBSERVED TO BE MORE SAVAGE AND CRUEL IN PROPORTION TO THEIR BULK WHAT COULD I EXPECT BUT TO BE A MORSEL IN THE MOUTH OF THE FIRST AMONG THESE ENORMOUS BARBARIANS THAT SHOULD HAPPEN TO SEIZE ME

HIS FORE TEETH WERE VERY LONG AND SHARP AND STOOD OUT OF HIS MOUTH WHICH WAS AS DEEP AS THAT OF A HORSE

AND THAT WHATEVER WE MAY HEAP UP TO GIVE OTHERS WE ENJOY JUST AS MUCH AS WE CAN USE AND NO MORE
SHE HAS BETRAYED US TO THE SAXON CALL ON THEM AGAIN VALIANT BARON SAID THE HAG WITH A SMILE OF GRISLY MOCKERY
FOR HE TREATED THEM KINDLY AS LONG AS THEY DID HIS BIDDING AND HE EXERCISED HIS POWER OVER THEM WISELY AND WELL
BUT LET US NOT BE OUR OWN MURDERERS
THUS THEREFORE THEY WALKED ON TOGETHER
BUT AS I WALKED ON THE TABLE BEING AT GREAT SURPRISE ALL THE TIME AS THE INDULGENT READER WILL EASILY CONCEIVE AND EXCUSE I HAPPENED TO STUMBLE AGAINST A CRUST AND FELL FLAT ON MY FACE BUT RECEIVED NO HURT
ALL THESE HE PLACED UPON A CARPET AND DISAPPEARED
AND THE VERY SIGHT OF HIM BECAME HATEFUL TO THE UNHAPPY GODFREY BERTRAM
THE NAME OF THE ONE WAS OBSTINATE AND THE NAME OF THE OTHER WAS PLIABLE
GO AND EXECUTE MY WISHES WHEN ALADDIN GAVE THESE COMMANDS TO THE GENIE THE SUN WAS SET
FROM HENCE WE WENT TO OTHER ISLANDS AND AT LAST HAVING TOUCHED AT SEVERAL TRADING TOWNS OF THE CONTINENT WE LANDED AT BUSSORAH FROM WHENCE I PROCEEDED TO BAGDAD
SO THAT IF I HAD TAKEN OFF MY BELT BEFORE I WENT TO SLEEP I MUST HAVE INFALLIBLY BEEN TORN TO PIECES AND DEVOURED
I FELT MY BOX RAISED VERY HIGH IN THE AIR AND THEN BORNE FORWARD WITH PRODIGIOUS SPEED
REMEMBERING THE WORDS THE CAPTAIN OF THE ROBBERS USED TO CAUSE THE DOOR TO OPEN AND SHUT HE HAD THE CURIOSITY TO TRY IF HIS PRONOUNCING THEM WOULD HAVE THE SAME EFFECT
THE READER MAY PLEASE TO OBSERVE THAT IN THE LAST ARTICLE FOR THE RECOVERY OF MY LIBERTY THE EMPEROR STIPULATES TO ALLOW ME A QUANTITY OF MEAT AND DRINK SUFFICIENT FOR THE SUPPORT OF 1724 LILLIPUTIANS
PRAY TELL ME WHAT BEFELL YOU I SATISFIED HIS CURIOSITY AND WE BOTH OF US SET OUT NEXT MORNING TO THE HILL
THE COUNTERFEIT FATIMA ADVANCED TOWARD HIM WITH HIS HAND ALL THE TIME ON A DAGGER CONCEALED IN HIS GIRDLE UNDER HIS GOWN
BUT HOW IS IT THAT YOU CAME ALONE
AND ALL MY COMPANIONS EXCEPT THE TWO WITH ME WERE DROWNED
HAVING THUS FIXED FIFTY HOOKS TO AS MANY CABLES I WENT BACK TO THE NORTHEAST COAST AND PUTTING OFF MY COAT SHOES AND STOCKINGS WALKED INTO THE SEA IN MY LEATHERN JERKIN ABOUT AN HOUR BEFORE HIGH WATER
I MYSELF WAS OF THE NUMBER OF THE LATTER
WILL YOU GO BACK WITH US OR NO
BUT I'LL BE EVEN WITH YOU BEFORE YOU LEAVE THIS WOOD THEN OBERON CALLED HIS FAVORITE FAIRY PUCK
THE END OF IT WAS THAT HELENA AND HERMIA BEGAN TO QUARREL AND DEMETRIUS AND LYSANDER WENT OFF TO FIGHT
UPON THIS I SEEMED A LITTLE ANGRY WITH THE CAPTAIN AND TOLD HIM THAT THEY WERE MY PRISONERS NOT HIS
AFTER TRAVELLING THUS FOR SOME TIME SHE CAME AT LENGTH TO THE RUINED TOWER WHERE BERTRAM HAD PREVIOUSLY SPENT THE NIGHT IN CONCEALMENT FROM THE SMUGGLERS
I AM SINDBAD SAID I AND THOSE BALES MARKED WITH HIS NAME ARE MINE WHEN THE CAPTAIN HEARD ME SPEAK THUS HEAVENS HE EXCLAIMED WHOM CAN WE TRUST IN THESE TIMES
I SURVIVED ALL MY COMPANIONS
THE KEEPER HOWEVER TOLD HIM THAT AS THE PRISON RULES WERE NOW MUCH STRICTER THAN BEFORE HIS SEEING HATTERAICK WOULD BE ONLY ON CONDITION THAT HE SHOULD SPEND THE WHOLE NIGHT WITH HIM
I MADE MY ACKNOWLEDGMENTS BY PROSTRATING MYSELF AT HIS MAJESTY'S FEET BUT HE COMMANDED ME TO RISE
BUT A PROCLAMATION WAS SOON ISSUED TO FORBID IT UPON PAIN OF DEATH
HE SOON FOUND AN OPENING IN ONE OF THE WALLS THROUGH WHICH HE COULD OBSERVE MEG MERRILIES WITHOUT HIMSELF BEING SEEN
THEY SOON RETURNED AND WE OBSERVED THAT EACH OF THEM CARRIED BETWEEN ITS TALONS AN ENORMOUS ROCK
ONLY COME ALONG WITH ME AND FEAR NOTHING BABA MUSTAPHA WENT WITH MORGIANA WHO AFTER SHE HAD BOUND HIS EYES WITH A HANDKERCHIEF AT THE PLACE SHE HAD MENTIONED CONVEYED HIM TO HER DECEASED MASTER'S HOUSE AND NEVER UNLOOSED HIS EYES TILL HE HAD ENTERED THE ROOM WHERE SHE HAD PUT THE CORPSE TOGETHER
AND THEN SINKING YET FARTHER FORWARD LAY PROSTRATE AT HER FEET
I NOW HEARD A TRAMPLING OVER MY HEAD AND SOMEBODY CALLING THROUGH THE HOLE WITH A LOUD VOICE IN THE ENGLISH TONGUE IF THERE BE ANYBODY BELOW LET THEM SPEAK
MY COMRADES NOT TAKING NOTICE THAT THE BLACKS ATE NONE OF IT THEMSELVES THOUGHT ONLY OF SATISFYING THEIR HUNGER AND ATE WITH GREEDINESS
FOR THIS RAFT WAS SO UNWIELDY AND SO OVERLADEN THAT AFTER I HAD ENTERED THE LITTLE COVE WHERE I HAD LANDED THE REST OF MY GOODS NOT BEING ABLE TO GUIDE IT SO HANDILY AS I DID THE OTHER IT OVERSET AND THREW ME AND ALL MY CARGO INTO THE WATER
HE FELL DOWN AT MY FEET
TELL ME THY NAME OR WORK THY PLEASURE ON ME THE BLACK KNIGHT WHISPERED SOMETHING INTO THE EAR OF THE VANQUISHED
ALI BABA WITH GREAT PLEASURE TOOK THE TREAT UPON HIMSELF
AND NOW I WAS CALLED GOVERNOR AGAIN
AND WAS EVEN MORE PUZZLED BY HER CONDUCT WHEN SHE TOOK AN OLD PURSE FROM HER POCKET BEFORE PARTING AND GAVE IT TO HIM
I APPEALED IN VAIN
IN THE MEANTIME THERE SUDDENLY FELL SUCH A VIOLENT SHOWER OF HAIL THAT I WAS IMMEDIATELY BY THE FORCE OF IT STRUCK TO THE GROUND
I HAD SUNK DOWN TO THE CHURCH-YARD WHILST ASLEEP GENTLY AND IN THE SAME PROPORTION AS THE SNOW HAD MELTED AWAY
BUT WHILE I WAS PREPARING THIS I FOUND THE SKY OVERCAST AND THE WIND BEGAN TO RISE AND IN A QUARTER OF AN HOUR IT BLEW A FRESH GALE FROM THE SHORE
WHEN I HAD FINISHED I LOADED IT WITH SOME CHESTS OF RUBIES EMERALDS AMBERGRIS ROCK CRYSTAL AND BALES OF RICH STUFFS
WHEREFORE CHRISTIAN WAS LEFT TO TUMBLE IN THE SLOUGH OF DISPOND ALONE
THEY CONTINUED DRINKING AND TALKING FOR A CONSIDERABLE TIME BUT ALL THAT BROWN COULD MAKE OUT WAS THAT THERE WAS SOMEONE WHOM THEY WERE GOING TO MURDER
UPON WHICH THE REST YIELDED AND THE SHIP WAS TAKEN EFFECTUALLY WITHOUT ANY MORE LIVES LOST
AND WITH THAT CHRISTIAN'S SWORD FLEW OUT OF HIS HAND
I HOPE BEFORE THAT TIME MY SON WHOM YOU HAVE REGARDED WITH YOUR FAVOR WILL BE ABLE TO MAKE A NOBLER PRESENT THAN THIS ALADDIN WHO IS AN ENTIRE STRANGER TO YOUR MAJESTY THE SULTAN GRANTED HIS REQUEST AND HE SAID TO THE OLD WOMAN GOOD WOMAN GO HOME AND TELL YOUR SON THAT I AGREE TO THE PROPOSAL YOU HAVE MADE ME
AND THEN WAS MY NEIGHBOR PLIABLE DISCOURAGED AND WOULD NOT ADVENTURE FURTHER
AND KNOW TOO EVEN NOW THE DOOM WHICH ALL THY POWER AND STRENGTH IS UNABLE TO AVOID THOUGH IT IS PREPARED FOR THEE BY THIS FEEBLE HAND

MAURICE DE BRACY I SAY BEWARE DE BRACY BOWED LOW AND IN SILENCE THREW HIMSELF UPON A HORSE AND GALLOPED OFF THROUGH THE WOOD

NOT KNOWING WHAT TO DO I CLIMBED UP TO THE TOP OF A LOFTY TREE FROM WHICH I LOOKED ABOUT ON ALL SIDES TO SEE IF I COULD DISCOVER ANYTHING THAT COULD GIVE ME HOPES
HE CHANCED ON BOARD TO MEET A MAN WHOSE DAUGHTER WAS AT THE TIME IN COLONEL MANNERING'S SERVICE AT WOODBOURNE AND BY HIS MEANS CONTRIVED TO GET A LETTER DELIVERED TO MISS MANNERING IN WHICH HE BEGGED OF HER TO FORGIVE HIM FOR HIS RASH CONDUCT TOWARDS HAZLEWOOD
FOR WHERE IN ALL THE WORLD BESIDES SHALL WE FIND WALLS BUILT OF MASSY GOLD AND SILVER AND DIAMONDS RUBIES AND EMERALDS COMPOSING THE WINDOWS
THEY CHATTERED AS THEY CAME NEAR BUT WE UNDERSTOOD NOT THEIR LANGUAGE
I AM WILLING WITH ALL MY HEART SAID HE
CHILD SAID SHE TO WHOM ARE WE OBLIGED FOR THIS GREAT PLENTY AND LIBERALITY

MY DAUGHTER BETTY WHO IS NOW WELL MARRIED AND HAS CHILDREN WAS THEN AT HER NEEDLEWORK
CHRISTIAN BEGAN TO GIRD UP HIS LOINS AND TO ADDRESS HIMSELF TO HIS JOURNEY

NOW GIANT DESPAIR HAD A WIFE AND HER NAME WAS DIFFIDENCE

IN THAT WAR-CRY IS THE DOWNFALL OF THY HOUSE
ANY ONE MAY GUESS HOW READILY SUCH A PROPOSAL WOULD BE ACCEPTED BY MEN IN THEIR CONDITION

THEY WILL HAVE WORK TO-NIGHT
POOR LUCY BERTRAM NOW FOUND HERSELF AN ORPHAN WITHOUT HOUSE OR HOME

THE FOLLOWING DAY TO OUR GREAT TERROR WE SAW THE SERPENT AGAIN WHEN I EXCLAIMED O HEAVEN TO WHAT DANGERS ARE WE EXPOSED
AS SOON AS THEY GOT IN ORDER THEY DIVIDED INTO TWO PARTIES PERFORMED MOCK SKIRMISHES DISCHARGED BLUNT ARROWS DREW THEIR SWORDS FLED AND PURSUED ATTACKED AND RETIRED AND IN SHORT DISCOVERED THE BEST MILITARY DISCIPLINE I EVER BEHELD
AND CONSIDERING SHE WANTED VARIOUS UTENSILS BORROWED THEM OF HER NEIGHBORS

3DLY WHAT LITTLE WIND THERE WAS BLEW ME TOWARDS THE LAND

I MAINTAIN MY INNOCENCE

OUR VESSEL BEING COME TO A PORT ON THE MAINLAND IN THE INDIES WE TOUCHED THERE AND NOT BEING WILLING TO VENTURE BY SEA TO BUSSORAH I LANDED MY PROPORTION OF THE IVORY RESOLVING TO PROCEED ON MY JOURNEY BY LAND

ALL THIS WHILE I ATE NOTHING BUT WHAT WAS JUST NECESSARY TO SUPPORT NATURE
HE TOLD THEM HE MUST OBEY
IN THIS TERRIBLE AGITATION OF MIND I COULD NOT FORBEAR THINKING OF LILLIPUT WHOSE INHABITANTS LOOKED UPON ME AS THE GREATEST PRODIGY THAT EVER APPEARED IN THE WORLD
NOR IS IT POSSIBLE TO DESCRIBE HOW MANY VARIOUS SHAPES MY AFFRIGHTED IMAGINATION REPRESENTED THINGS TO ME IN HOW MANY WILD IDEAS WERE FOUND EVERY MOMENT IN MY FANCY AND WHAT STRANGE UNACCOUNTABLE WHIMSIES CAME INTO MY THOUGHTS BY THE WAY
THUS WAS ALADDIN DELIVERED FROM THE PERSECUTION OF THE TWO BROTHERS WHO WERE MAGICIANS
FOR THERE WAS NO MORE TO BE DONE BUT LET ONE OF THE CREW PUT HIS FINGER INTO THE RING AND TAKE THE BOX OUT OF THE SEA INTO THE SHIP AND SO INTO THE CAPTAIN'S CABIN
PERHAPS MANY TRAVELLERS HAVE NOT BEEN UNDER GREATER DIFFICULTIES AND DISTRESS THAN I WAS AT THIS JUNCTURE EXPECTING EVERY MOMENT TO SEE MY BOX DASHED TO PIECES OR AT LEAST OVERSET BY THE FIRST VIOLENT BLAST OR RISING WAVE
FOR HE HAD ALREADY INFORMED ME HOW THE SEAMEN DISPOSED OF MY CLOSET

THOU HAST THYSELF DECIDED THINE OWN FATE
THE SEAMEN WERE ALL PROVIDED WITH CORDAGE WHICH I HAD BEFOREHAND TWISTED TO A SUFFICIENT STRENGTH

IN SHORT I GAVE MYSELF UP AS LOST FOR THE LION WAS NOW UPON HIS HIND LEGS JUST IN THE ACT OF SEIZING ME
AND IT WAS INDEED A DISMAL PLACE ESPECIALLY TO MEN IN THEIR CONDITION
I CALLED HIM SO FOR THE MEMORY OF THE TIME

AFTER THIS I WENT EVERY DAY ON BOARD AND BROUGHT AWAY WHAT I COULD GET
TO PLEAD THAT MANY THINGS WHICH THESE MEN WHOM MAY HEAVEN PARDON HAVE SPOKEN AGAINST ME ARE IMPOSSIBLE WOULD AVAIL ME BUT LITTLE SINCE YOU BELIEVE IN THEIR POSSIBILITY AND STILL LESS WOULD IT ADVANTAGE ME TO EXPLAIN THAT THE PECULIARITIES OF MY DRESS LANGUAGE AND MANNERS ARE THOSE OF MY PEOPLE
THOUGH A WILD LAD WITH LITTLE EDUCATION HE MARRIED A SPLENDID WIFE WHO CHANGED THE EVIL COURSE OF HIS LIFE AND INTERESTED HIM IN RELIGION
WERE YE NOT FRIENDLESS HOUSELESS PENNILESS WHEN I TOOK YE BY THE HAND
WHICH WAS INDEED A PRODIGIOUS LEAP
THEN INDEED HE DID SMILE AND LOOK UPWARD
THE REMOVAL OF THE BODY AND THE LOSS OF SOME OF OUR MONEY PLAINLY SHOW THAT THE MAN WHOM WE KILLED HAD AN ACCOMPLICE
SIRE I COME AT THE END OF THREE MONTHS TO ASK OF YOU THE FULFILMENT OF THE PROMISE YOU MADE TO MY SON THE SULTAN LITTLE THOUGHT THE REQUEST OF ALADDIN'S MOTHER WAS MADE TO HIM IN EARNEST OR THAT HE WOULD HEAR ANY MORE OF THE MATTER
BUT A MORE DANGEROUS ACCIDENT HAPPENED TO ME IN THE SAME GARDEN WHEN MY LITTLE NURSE BELIEVING SHE HAD PUT ME IN A SECURE PLACE WHICH I OFTEN ENTREATED HER TO DO THAT I MIGHT ENJOY MY OWN THOUGHTS AND HAVING LEFT MY BOX AT HOME TO AVOID THE TROUBLE OF CARRYING IT WENT TO ANOTHER PART OF THE GARDEN WITH HER GOVERNESS AND SOME LADIES OF HER ACQUAINTANCE
AND NOW INSTEAD OF BEING PLEASED HE CONCEIVED A BASE ENVY AT HIS BROTHER'S PROSPERITY
BUT JUST FOR FUN YOU SHALL SIGN A BOND IN WHICH IT SHALL BE AGREED THAT IF YOU DO NOT REPAY ME IN THREE MONTHS TIME THEN I SHALL HAVE THE RIGHT TO A POUND OF YOUR FLESH TO BE CUT FROM WHAT PART OF YOUR BODY I CHOOSE NO CRIED BASSANIO TO HIS FRIEND YOU SHALL RUN NO SUCH RISK FOR ME WHY FEAR NOT SAID ANTONIO MY SHIPS WILL BE HOME A MONTH BEFORE THE TIME I WILL SIGN THE BOND THUS BASSANIO WAS FURNISHED WITH THE MEANS TO GO TO BELMONT THERE TO WOO THE LOVELY PORTIA
THEY ALL APPEARED VERY PENITENT AND BEGGED HARD FOR THEIR LIVES
GLOSSIN WAS CONFINED IN ANOTHER ROOM HIS MIND STILL TEEMING WITH SCHEMES OF FUTURE DECEIT TO COVER HIS FORMER VILLAINIES
THAT IF HE DID NOT THINK FIT TO DO SO IT WAS MY UNQUESTIONED DUTY TO RESIGN MYSELF ABSOLUTELY AND ENTIRELY TO HIS WILL
I DO NOT EXACTLY RECOLLECT WHETHER IT WAS EASTLAND OR JUGEMANLAND BUT I REMEMBER THAT IN THE MIDST OF A DREARY FOREST I SPIED A TERRIBLE WOLF MAKING AFTER ME WITH ALL THE SPEED OF RAVENOUS WINTER HUNGER
AND THEN IN A MOMENT SHE SAW PLAINLY THE DONKEY-HEADED CLOWN SHE HAD BEEN LOVING AND KNEW HOW FOOLISH SHE HAD BEEN
I WILL SHOW YOU WHAT VACANT APARTMENTS I HAVE THAT YOU MAY MAKE CHOICE OF THAT YOU LIKE BEST THE MAGICIAN FOLLOWED THE PRINCESS AND OF ALL THE APARTMENTS SHE SHOWED HIM MADE CHOICE OF THAT WHICH WAS THE WORST SAYING THAT IT WAS TOO GOOD FOR HIM AND THAT HE ONLY ACCEPTED IT TO PLEASE HER
THE FROG LAY CONCEALED TILL I WAS PUT INTO MY BOAT BUT THEN SEEING A RESTING PLACE CLIMBED UP AND MADE IT TO LEAN SO MUCH ON ONE SIDE THAT I WAS FORCED TO BALANCE IT WITH ALL MY WEIGHT ON THE OTHER TO PREVENT OVERTURNING
INDEED OUR PRESENT CONDITION IS DREADFUL AND DEATH WOULD BE FAR MORE WELCOME TO ME THAN THUS FOR EVER TO ABIDE
AND THOUGH MY MISTRESS HELD HER FAST FOR FEAR SHE MIGHT GIVE A SPRING AND SEIZE ME IN HER TALONS
BUT I THANKED HER AND COULD SPARE NO MORE SO SHE MARCHED OFF
BUT FOUND A NECK OR INLET OF WATER BETWEEN ME AND THE BOAT WHICH WAS ABOUT HALF A MILE BROAD
AND HOW SHE SWORE AN OATH TO KEEP THE SECRET TILL HE WAS ONE-AND-TWENTY AND VOWED THAT IF SHE LIVED TO SEE THE DAY OF HIS RETURN SHE WOULD SET HIM AGAIN IN HIS FATHER'S SEAT THOUGH EVERY STEP WAS ON A DEAD MAN
BUT HE SAID THAT CAN BY NO MEANS BE
AND THAT THEREFORE I HAD NOTHING TO DO BUT CONSIDER OF SOME SAFE RETREAT IN CASE I SHOULD SEE ANY SAVAGES LAND UPON THE SPOT
AND AS HE RAN SOME MOCKED OTHERS THREATENED AND SOME CRIED AFTER HIM TO RETURN
AS I FOUND SOME WEEKS AFTER WHEN I WENT TO PAY MY RESPECTS TO THE EMPEROR OF BLEFUSCU WHICH IN THE MIDST OF GREAT MISFORTUNES THROUGH THE MALICE OF MY ENEMIES PROVED A VERY HAPPY ADVENTURE TO ME AS I SHALL RELATE IN ITS PROPER PLACE
IT NOW OCCURRED TO ME THAT THE TIME OF OUR DELIVERANCE WAS COME AND THAT IT WOULD BE A MOST EASY THING TO BRING THESE FELLOWS IN TO BE HEARTY IN GETTING POSSESSION OF THE SHIP
HOWEVER WHEN SHE HAD AWHILE SEEN MY BEHAVIOR AND HOW WELL I OBSERVED THE SIGNS HER HUSBAND MADE SHE WAS SOON RECONCILED AND BY DEGREES GREW EXTREMELY TENDER OF ME
THEN WHEN THIS IS DONE ALL WILL BE WELL WITH THEM SO PUCK WENT AND DID AS HE WAS TOLD AND WHEN THE TWO HAD FALLEN ASLEEP WITHOUT MEETING EACH OTHER PUCK POURED THE JUICE ON LYSANDER'S EYES AND SAID WHEN THOU WAKEST THOU TAKEST TRUE DELIGHT IN THE SIGHT OF THY FORMER LADY'S EYE
REMEMBER YOUR PROMISE AND FOLLOW ME IT WAS IN VAIN THAT HIS SISTER AND HER COMPANION URGED HIM NOT TO GO WITH THE GIPSY
FOR FINDING I DID NOT FOLLOW HIM INTO THE WOOD HE RETURNED APPREHENDING I HAD LOST MY WAY OR MET WITH SOME ACCIDENT
THE MISTRESS SENT HER MAID FOR A SMALL DRAM CUP WHICH HELD ABOUT TWO GALLONS AND FILLED IT WITH DRINK
AND AT THE HOLE OR PLACE WHICH WAS LEFT TO GO IN OR OUT BY THE LADDER I HAD PLACED A KIND OF TRAP-DOOR WHICH IF IT HAD BEEN ATTEMPTED ON THE OUTSIDE WOULD NOT HAVE OPENED AT ALL BUT WOULD HAVE FALLEN DOWN AND MADE A GREAT NOISE
NO FURTHER EVIDENCE COULD BE PROCURED OF HER GUILT AND SHE WAS AT LENGTH SET FREE UNDER SENTENCE OF BANISHMENT FROM THE COUNTY
TO WHICH HE ANSWERED THAT DISCOURSING THIS MATTER WITH THE SAILORS WHILE I WAS ASLEEP ONE OF THEM SAID HE HAD OBSERVED THREE EAGLES FLYING TOWARD THE NORTH BUT REMARKED NOTHING OF THEIR BEING LARGER THAN THE USUAL SIZE
HE COULD NOT SLEEP ALL THAT NIGHT AND WENT TO HIM IN THE MORNING BEFORE SUNRISE
GURTH STARTED AS IF ELECTRIFIED AND HASTENED AT ONCE TO PROCURE THEIR MULES FOR THE TRAVELLERS AND TO OPEN THE POSTERN GATE TO LET THEM OUT
FAREWELL THE PRESENT CONSISTED FIRST OF ONE SINGLE RUBY MADE INTO A CUP ABOUT HALF A FOOT HIGH AN INCH THICK AND FILLED WITH ROUND PEARLS OF HALF A DRACHM EACH
AND AS I HAVE BEEN ALWAYS TOLD AND FOUND TRUE BY EXPERIENCE IN MY TRAVELS THAT FLYING OR DISCOVERING FEAR BEFORE A FIERCE ANIMAL IS A CERTAIN WAY TO MAKE IT PURSUE OR ATTACK YOU SO I RESOLVED IN THIS DANGEROUS JUNCTURE TO SHOW NO MANNER OF CONCERN
TWO OF THEM OF WHOM THE CAPTAIN WAS LESS ASSURED THAN ORDINARY I SENT WITH FRIDAY AND ONE OF THE THREE DELIVERED MEN TO MY CAVE WHERE THEY WERE REMOTE ENOUGH AND OUT OF DANGER OF BEING HEARD OR DISCOVERED OR OF FINDING THEIR WAY OUT OF THE WOODS IF THEY COULD HAVE DELIVERED THEMSELVES
BESIDES ON THE BANKS OF THIS RIVER ON EITHER SIDE WERE GREEN TREES THAT BORE ALL MANNER OF FRUIT
WE HAULED OFF UPON THE LANYARD OF THE WHIP-STAFF AND HELPED THE MAN AT THE HELM
AND WHAT COURSE TO TAKE FOR MY SECURITY I KNEW NOT
AND HAVING LOADED ONE OF HIS ASSES WITH THEM COVERED THEM OVER WITH WOOD
ON THE NEXT AUDIENCE DAY WHEN ALADDIN'S MOTHER WENT TO THE DIVAN AND PLACED HERSELF IN FRONT OF THE SULTAN AS USUAL THE GRAND VIZIER IMMEDIATELY CALLED THE CHIEF OF THE MACE-BEARERS AND POINTING TO HER BADE HIM BRING HER BEFORE THE SULTAN
I ALSO HEARD THE MEN THEMSELVES THAT THEY SANG WITH A LOUD VOICE SAYING BLESSING HONOUR GLORY AND POWER BE TO HIM THAT SITTETH UPON THE THRONE AND TO THE LAMB FOR EVER AND EVER
BUT IT PLEASED GOD ONCE MORE TO TAKE COMPASSION ON ME AND PUT IT IN MY MIND TO GO TO THE BANK OF THE RIVER WHICH RAN INTO THE GREAT CAVERN
THE NOISE OF OPENING THE WINDOW MADE ALADDIN TURN HIS HEAD THAT WAY AND PERCEIVING THE PRINCESS HE SALUTED HER WITH AN AIR THAT EXPRESSED HIS JOY
WHEN I GAZED TOWARD THE SEA I COULD SEE NOTHING BUT SKY AND WATER
I CANNOT TELL WHETHER I WERE MORE PLEASED OR MORTIFIED TO OBSERVE IN THOSE SOLITARY WALKS THAT THE SMALLER BIRDS DID NOT APPEAR TO BE AT ALL AFRAID OF ME BUT WOULD HOP ABOUT WITHIN A YARD'S DISTANCE LOOKING FOR WORMS AND OTHER FOOD WITH AS MUCH INDIFFERENCE AND SECURITY AS IF NO CREATURE AT ALL WERE NEAR THEM
SO I CAME HITHER
BUT SAID BASSANIO LET ME CHOOSE AT ONCE FOR AS I AM I LIVE UPON THE RACK THEN PORTIA BADE HER SERVANTS TO BRING MUSIC AND PLAY WHILE HER GALLANT LOVER MADE HIS CHOICE
WHEREAS WE COULD NOT POSSIBLY MAKE OUR VOYAGE TO THE COAST OF AFRICA WITHOUT SOME ASSISTANCE BOTH TO OUR SHIP AND TO OURSELVES
HE SAID HE WONDERED AT ONE THING VERY MUCH WHICH WAS TO HEAR ME SPEAK SO LOUD
AS THE VICTOR WAS LED TOWARDS THE THRONE OF THE LADY ROWENA IT WAS OBSERVED THAT HE TOTTERED
HE OFTEN BUILDS HIS LARGEST MEN-OF-WAR WHEREOF SOME ARE NINE FEET LONG IN THE WOODS WHERE THE TIMBER GROWS AND HAS THEM CARRIED ON THESE ENGINES THREE OR FOUR HUNDRED YARDS TO THE SEA
I WAS MUCH ASTONISHED AT THIS SUDDEN DARKNESS BUT MUCH MORE WHEN I FOUND IT OCCASIONED BY A BIRD OF A MONSTROUS SIZE THAT CAME FLYING TOWARD ME
AND AT NIGHT WHEN IT WAS READY SAID TO HER SON PERHAPS THE STRANGER KNOWS NOT HOW TO FIND OUR HOUSE
BUT TO MY GREAT DISAPPOINTMENT I FOUND AFTERWARDS THAT THE RATS HAD EATEN OR SPOILED IT ALL
FOR HER PART SHE WOULD HAVE NOTHING TO DO WITH GENIES AND NEVER SAY ANYTHING MORE ABOUT THEM
ONE FOOT NEARER AND I PLUNGE MYSELF FROM THE PRECIPICE
OUTSIDE THE LISTS WERE GALLERIES SPREAD WITH TAPESTRY AND CARPETS FOR THE CONVENIENCE OF THE LADIES AND NOBLES WHO WERE EXPECTED TO ATTEND THE TOURNAMENT
I NOW WALKED TOWARD THE BEACH WHERE I MET THE CREW OF A SHIP THAT HAD CAST ANCHOR TO TAKE IN WATER
BEING A MERCHANT I FREQUENTED MEN OF MY OWN PROFESSION AND PARTICULARLY INQUIRED FOR THOSE WHO WERE STRANGERS THAT PERCHANCE I MIGHT HEAR NEWS FROM BAGDAD OR FIND AN OPPORTUNITY TO RETURN
IN GOD'S NAME YOUNG MAN TELL ME YOUR NAME AND WHENCE YOU COME MY NAME IS BROWN MOTHER AND I COME FROM THE EAST INDIES HE ANSWERED
FOR IT IS OF GREAT IMPORTANCE TO KEEP THIS AFFAIR SECRET
THEN THEY CAME ALL CLOSE IN A RING AND FIRED A VOLLEY OF THEIR SMALL ARMS WHICH INDEED WE HEARD AND THE ECHOES MADE THE WOODS RING
TO WHAT FATE
AND AS HE MEANT TO CARRY HIM FURTHER TO EXECUTE HIS DESIGN HE TOOK AN OPPORTUNITY TO SIT DOWN IN ONE OF THE GARDENS ON THE BRINK OF A FOUNTAIN OF CLEAR WATER WHICH DISCHARGED ITSELF BY A LION'S MOUTH OF BRONZE INTO A BASIN PRETENDING TO BE TIRED
IT WAS NOT LONG BEFORE CEDRIC RECOGNISED THE VOICE OF HIS JESTER
BUT IT WOULD NOT TURN TO ACCOUNT
AND FIRST I LET HIM KNOW HIS NAME SHOULD BE FRIDAY WHICH WAS THE DAY I SAVED HIS LIFE
BUT TWILL DO YOURSELF MUCH GOOD REPLIED MEG MERRILIES
BUT ALL THE ROPES BROKE AND THE SHIP WAS CARRIED BY THE CURRENT TO THE FOOT OF AN INACCESSIBLE MOUNTAIN WHERE SHE STRUCK AND WENT TO PIECES
BUT WHEN I SPOKE IN THAT COUNTRY IT WAS LIKE A MAN TALKING IN THE STREETS TO ANOTHER LOOKING OUT FROM THE TOP OF A STEEPLE UNLESS WHEN I WAS PLACED ON A TABLE OR HELD IN ANY PERSON'S HAND
HE ADMIRED THE QUANTITY OF WOOD OF ALOES AND AMBERGRIS
WHICH BEING WELL PITCHED TO PREVENT LEAKING WAS PLACED ON THE FLOOR ALONG THE WALL IN AN OUTER ROOM OF THE PALACE
AND ON SEEING THE LARGE NUMBER OF OLD BOOKS WHICH WERE COMMITTED TO HIS CHARGE HE BECAME ALMOST CRAZY WITH DELIGHT AND SHOUTED HIS FAVOURITE WORD PRO-DI-GI-OUS TILL THE ROOF RUNG TO HIS RAPTURES
MY GOOD MOTHER SAID THE PRINCESS I AM OVERJOYED TO SEE SO HOLY A WOMAN AS YOURSELF WHO WILL CONFER A BLESSING UPON THIS PALACE
SCARED AND CONFOUNDED AS I WAS I COULD NOT FORBEAR GOING ON WITH THESE REFLECTIONS WHEN ONE OF THE REAPERS APPROACHING WITHIN TEN YARDS OF THE RIDGE WHERE I LAY MADE ME APPREHEND THAT WITH THE NEXT STEP I SHOULD BE SQUASHED TO DEATH UNDER HIS FOOT OR CUT IN TWO WITH HIS REAPING-HOOK
CAPTAIN BROWN AS HE WAS NOW KNOWN WAS A HANDSOME AND GALLANT YOUNG FELLOW
THIS HAPPENED TO ME IN FRANCE
IN SHORT THEY USED ALL THE JEWELS THE SULTAN HAD AND BORROWED OF THE VIZIER BUT YET THE WORK WAS NOT HALF DONE
DIRCK HATTERAICK TOLD HIM TOO VERY PLAINLY THAT IF HE WAS TO BE CONDEMNED HE WOULD LET THE SECRET OUT AND RUIN GLOSSIN
WHAT A VILLAIN CRIED THE GOLDSMITH
BUT ALL WAS IN VAIN
DO THOU SO TOO AND ALL SHALL BE WELL
ALI BABA MARRIED A WOMAN AS POOR AS HIMSELF AND LIVED BY CUTTING WOOD AND BRINGING IT UPON THREE ASSES INTO THE TOWN TO SELL
BUT THIS FRIGHTED ME MOST THAT THE ANGELS GATHERED UP SEVERAL AND LEFT ME BEHIND
AND THE THREE WERE LEFT ALONE
AND THE NEXT DAY THE WAGONERS ARRIVED WITH IT BUT NOT IN A VERY GOOD CONDITION
THE NEARER THE SULTAN APPROACHED ALADDIN'S PALACE THE MORE HE WAS STRUCK WITH ITS BEAUTY
WHEN THE OTHER BOAT AND THEIR MEN ENTERING AT THE FORECHAINS SECURED THE FORECASTLE OF THE SHIP AND THE SCUTTLE WHICH WENT DOWN INTO THE COOK-ROOM MAKING THREE MEN THEY FOUND THERE PRISONERS
FROM THENCE THEY WENT TO THE STOREHOUSES WHICH WERE FILLED WITH ALL THINGS NECESSARY BOTH FOR FOOD AND ORNAMENT
